### [130] [Evaluative Judgement in Teaching AI-based Translation: A Class-room Case Study of AI-Mediated Translation and Post-Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15483)
*Gokhan Dogru*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究基于23个匿名的学生项目，分析了在机器翻译与后编辑课程中，通过结构化比较通用大语言模型（LLM）与在线机器翻译系统，如何激发学生对人工智能辅助翻译的评价判断。学生将英文维基百科专业文本翻译成加泰罗尼亚语或西班牙语，生成四种系统输出，利用自动评估指标和人工适切性/流畅性评估进行评价，选择一个输出进行后编辑，并在书面报告中说明决策理由。研究以描述性统计呈现全部23个项目数据，定性分析基于22份附有书面报告的案例。结果显示，学生并未将自动指标视为最终权威：最终选择的后编辑输出常与指标排名不一致，其决策依据包括适切性、流畅性、术语准确性、自然度及预期后编辑工作量。本研究并非在受控条件下对系统进行基准测试，而是探讨学生在真实课堂任务中如何解释其系统选择。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 收集23个来自本科翻译课程的匿名学生项目数据，学生完成从英语到加泰罗尼亚语或西班牙语的专业文本翻译任务，生成四个不同系统的翻译输出；使用自动评估指标和人工适切性/流畅性评分进行评价；选择一个输出进行后编辑，并撰写书面报告解释选择理由；通过定量统计与定性分析相结合的方式，考察学生的选择逻辑与评价标准。

Result: 学生在选择后编辑目标时，往往不遵循自动指标的排名，而是综合考虑适切性、流畅性、术语准确性、自然度以及预期后编辑工作量等因素；表明自动评估指标不能作为唯一或最终判断依据，人类判断在实际翻译流程中仍具关键作用。

Conclusion: 本研究强调在真实教学环境中，学生对AI翻译系统的评价是多维度且基于经验判断的，自动指标虽有参考价值，但无法替代人类对翻译质量的综合评估。这为未来AI辅助翻译教学提供了重要启示，即应培养学生的批判性评估能力，而非依赖单一技术指标。

Abstract: Drawing on 23 anonymized student pro-jects from a fourth-year Machine Transla-tion and Post-editing course in a BA-level translation programme, this paper exam-ines how structured comparison of gen-eral-purpose LLMs and online MT sys-tems can elicit evaluative judgement in AI-mediated translation. Students translat-ed short specialised English Wikipedia texts into Catalan or Spanish, generated four system outputs, evaluated them using automatic metrics and human adequa-cy/fluency assessment, selected one output for post-editing, and justified their deci-sion in written reports. Descriptive counts are reported for all 23 projects, while qualitative interpretation is based on the 22 cases accompanied by written reports. Results show that students did not treat automatic metrics as final authority: final post-editing selections often diverged from metric rankings and were justified through adequacy, fluency, terminology, naturalness, and expected post-editing ef-fort. The study therefore does not bench-mark systems under controlled conditions; it analyses how students justified system choice within an authentic classroom as-signment.

### [131] [AthDGC: An Open Diachronic Greek Treebank with Indo-European Parallels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15510)
*Nikolaos Lavidas,Kiki Nikiforidou,Dag Haug,Leonid Kulikov,Vassiliki Geka,Vassileios Symeonidis,Theodoros Michalareas,Sofia Chionidi,Anastasia Tsiropina,Eleni Plakoutsi,Evangelos Argyropoulos*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AthDGC 是一个开放的端到端工作流程和数据集，是首个涵盖希腊语八个历史时期的公开许可依存句法标注语料库，使用统一的 PROIEL XML 2.0 模式，并实现了新约圣经与拉丁语（武加大本）、哥特语（沃尔菲拉）、古教会斯拉夫语（马里亚努斯）和古典亚美尼亚语之间的逐行对齐。该语料库基于 PROIEL 树库家族，采用 Stanford Stanza PROIEL 训练的工作流进行标注，句子级对齐使用 LaBSE 多语言句子嵌入模型，词级对齐通过 multilingual-BERT 注意力结合 AwesomeAlign 方法实现。v0.4 版本提供精选样本和开源工具包，完整标注语料库分区仍在希腊国家高性能计算平台进行 v0.5 审核。详细统计信息将在 v0.5 发布说明中公布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一个跨历史时期、多语言对齐的希腊语依存句法标注语料库，以支持历史语言学、对比语法和多语言自然语言处理研究，填补现有资源在希腊语多时段、多语言对齐方面的空白。

Method: 基于 PROIEL Treebank Family 的架构，采用 Stanford Stanza PROIEL 训练的工作流进行依存标注；句子级对齐使用 LaBSE 多语言嵌入模型；词级对齐通过 multilingual-BERT 注意力机制结合 AwesomeAlign 方法实现；所有数据遵循 PROIEL XML 2.0 标准，并在希腊国家 HPC 平台上进行审核。

Result: 成功构建了涵盖八种希腊语历史阶段的依存句法标注语料库，实现新约圣经与四种古代语言的逐行对齐；提供了 v0.4 版本的精选样本和开源工具包；完整语料库正在 v0.5 审核阶段，相关统计信息将随后发布。

Conclusion: AthDGC 是首个大规模、跨历史时期、多语言对齐的希腊语依存句法标注语料库，具有重要的学术价值和应用潜力，为历史语言学和多语言自然语言处理研究提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: AthDGC ("Athens-PROIEL") is an open, end-to-end workflow and dataset. It is, to the best of our knowledge, the first openly licensed dependency-parsed treebank of Greek that spans eight diachronic periods, namely Archaic, Classical, Koine, Late Antique, Byzantine, Late Byzantine, Early Modern, and Modern Greek, under a single PROIEL XML 2.0 schema, with verse-level cross-alignment of the New Testament to Latin (Vulgate), Gothic (Wulfila), Old Church Slavonic (Marianus), and Classical Armenian. AthDGC builds on the PROIEL Treebank Family (Haug and Johndal 2008; Eckhoff et al. 2018), which established the schema and the Koine-Greek reference set for the project. Annotation uses the Stanford Stanza PROIEL-trained workflow; sentence-level alignment uses LaBSE, a multilingual sentence-embedding model; word-level alignment uses multilingual-BERT attention through the AwesomeAlign procedure. The v0.4 release provides curated samples and the open-source toolkit; the full annotated corpus partitions remain under v0.5 audit on the Greek national HPC. Quantitative scale, per-witness verse counts, and per-period annotated-row counts are reported in the v0.5 release notes, after the audit pass completes. Concept DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.20439182.

</details>


### [132] [SHARD: Safe and Helpful Alignment via Self-Reframing Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15517)
*Viswonathan Manoranjan,Amogh Gupta,Anvesh Rao Vijjini,Thomas Hofweber,Snigdha Chaturvedi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SHARD是一种自重构蒸馏方法，通过哲学指南重写敏感提示以揭示良性意图，再将原始回答重构为更安全、更有帮助的形式，并微调模型以学习这些自我重构的回答。在DNA和LINGUASAFE英文子集上，SHARD提升了多数模型家族的帮助性，同时保持安全性，且性能可与使用更大教师模型的蒸馏相媲美，表明模型能够内化自身生成的安全且有帮助的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在处理敏感提示时常表现不佳，可能完全拒绝、提供通用的安全套话，或无法满足用户可安全回答的合理信息需求。需要一种方法提升模型在保持安全的同时提供更多有用信息的能力。

Method: SHARD首先利用哲学指南重写敏感提示以揭示潜在的良性意图；然后将原始响应重构为更安全、更有帮助的形式；最后用这些自我重构的响应对模型进行微调，使其学会生成既安全又具有帮助性的输出。

Result: 在DNA和LINGUASAFE英文子集上的实验表明，SHARD显著提升了大多数模型家族的帮助性，同时维持了高水平的安全性。此外，其性能与使用更大教师模型的蒸馏相当，证明了模型能有效内化自身生成的优质响应。

Conclusion: SHARD展示了通过自我重构和蒸馏，大语言模型可以在不牺牲安全性的前提下显著提升帮助性，为构建更智能、更负责任的语言系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Large language models often struggle with sensitive prompts. They may refuse outright, provide generic safety boilerplate, or fail to address the user's legitimate informational needs that can be answered safely. We introduce SHARD, a self-reframing distillation method to improve safe-helpfulness. It first rewrites sensitive prompts to surface benign intent using philosophical guidelines, then reframes its original responses into safe, more helpful ones, and finally fine-tunes the model on its self-reframed responses. Across DNA and the English subset of LINGUASAFE, SHARD improves helpfulness for most model families while preserving safety. It also remains competitive with distillation from a larger teacher model, suggesting that models can internalize safe and helpful behavior elicited from their own. Warning: This paper contains content that may be offensive or harmful.

</details>


### [133] [Emergent retokenization symmetry in large language models: phenomenology and applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15521)
*Kanishk Jain,Matthew Day,Tankut Can*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了语言模型在固定词汇表下的分词冗余问题，发现尽管训练仅使用标准分词，模型仍部分表现出分词对称性。通过‘重分词’（retokenization）——在不改变字节和语义的前提下替换提示的分词方式——来探测模型对等价表示的敏感性和鲁棒性。结果显示，重分词能揭示模型的组合理解能力，并带来不同于传统温度采样的新采样维度，在某些任务中可发现常规采样遗漏的解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型的分词过程存在多种合法但不同的编码方式，而训练通常只使用一种标准分词。这可能导致模型对输入表示的敏感性偏差，影响其在下游任务中的表现。因此，需要探究模型是否具备对不同但等价分词形式的鲁棒性与理解能力。

Method: 采用重分词技术，即在保持原始字节串不变的情况下，将标准分词替换为其他合法分词方式，从而隔离分词变化对模型行为的影响。通过这一方法，评估模型在预训练和微调后对等价输入表示的敏感性、表示多样性及任务性能表现。

Result: 实验表明，模型在一定程度上表现出对重分词的鲁棒性，即对等价输入表示具有一定的对称性。这种对称性虽不完全，但在特定任务中可通过重分词发现传统采样无法找到的解决方案，说明重分词可作为新的推理时采样策略。

Conclusion: 重分词是一种有效且干净的探针工具，能够揭示大模型的组合理解能力和对输入表示的敏感性；同时，它提供了一种基于语义等价输入的新采样路径，可能提升模型在复杂问题中的探索能力。

Abstract: Tokenization introduces representational redundancy: under a fixed token vocabulary, every byte string admits many valid token encodings, or segmentations, that decode to the same surface string. However, given a prompt, most language model tokenizers break this representational symmetry by returning a canonical segmentation. Training only on canonical segmentations should influence inference behavior, and there is little reason to expect models to respect segmentation symmetry on downstream tasks. We find that this symmetry partially emerges during training. Here, we probe this emergent symmetry through experiments testing token compositional understanding, representation diversity, and task focused benchmark performance. We primarily use \textbf{retokenization} -- replacing a prompt's canonical tokenization with an alternative segmentation while preserving its bytes exactly. Relative to other prompt perturbations, retokenization is unusually clean because it isolates segmentation effects without changing syntax, semantics or surface form. We use retokenization to study sensitivity and robustness to semantically identical input representations across pretraining and post-training. Moreover, this partial retokenization symmetry suggests a distinct inference-time sampling axis. While temperature sampling generates diverse outputs from the model using its next-token probability distribution, retokenization generates diversity from the model's internal computations through semantically equivalent input representations. We find that while this retokenization sampling strategy can hurt performance on easy problems, it can also recover solutions that conventional sampling does not find. Overall, our work presents retokenization as a simple yet powerful probe of large language models, shedding light on compositional understanding and prompt sensitivity, and offering a novel sampling strategy.

</details>


### [134] [EIBench: A Simulator-Based Benchmark and Turn-Credit RL for Emotion Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15532)
*Rongzhi Zhu,Xiang Huang,Yuchuan Wu,Rui Wang,Zequn Sun,Tao Ren,Weiyao Luo,Bingxue Qiu,Jieping Ye,Yongbin Li,Wei Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出EIBench基准，用于评估和训练大模型在多轮交互中的情绪管理能力。该基准包含2222个场景，涵盖支持、防御、修复和魅力四类互动策略，通过模拟用户情绪-关系状态的动态变化，提供密集的逐轮反馈与最终结果奖励。实验表明当前模型在支持与建立亲密度方面表现良好，但在用户施压下的边界维护能力不足。为此提出CTC-GRPO方法，利用模拟器提供的逐轮状态更新作为密集反馈，显著提升模型表现（如Qwen3-8B从-22.4升至+22.4），并在多个外部评测中取得显著进步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM情绪评估多集中于静态理解或单轮对话，无法有效衡量模型在多轮交互中对用户情绪与关系状态的动态管理能力。真实情绪管理需要持续调节情感与关系，因此亟需一个能反映长期互动效果的评估与训练框架。

Method: 构建EIBench——基于模拟器的多轮情绪管理基准。设计2×2分类体系（支持、防御、修复、魅力）覆盖多种互动目标；每个场景由模拟器扮演用户，动态更新情绪-关系状态，并根据最终状态生成锚定评分。将逐轮状态变化作为强化学习中的密集奖励信号，结合最终结果奖励，用于训练模型。提出CTC-GRPO算法，融合模拟器的逐轮状态反馈与传统最终奖励，优化策略学习。

Result: 15个主流开源与闭源模型在EIBench上测试显示：模型在支持与亲密度构建任务中表现尚可，但在压力情境下的边界维护能力弱。使用CTC-GRPO训练后，Qwen3-8B在EIBench得分从-22.4提升至+22.4，在SAGE和EQBench3等外部数据集上分别提升+12.4和+20.9%，证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: EIBench不仅是一个有效的多轮情绪管理评估基准，也可作为训练环境。通过模拟器追踪用户状态变化，可提供丰富的密集反馈，助力模型学习长期情绪与关系管理能力。提出的CTC-GRPO方法显著提升了模型在复杂交互中的情绪智能表现，为未来高阶人机情感交互研究提供了新路径。

Abstract: Emotional intelligence (EI) in Large Language Models (LLMs) is often evaluated through static understanding tasks or single-response dialogue generation. However, emotion management is interactive: a good model should not only recognize a user's emotion, but also improve the user's emotional and relational state over several turns. We introduce EIBench, a simulator-based benchmark for interactive emotion management. EIBench contains 2,222 scenarios, with 2,009 for training and 213 for held-out testing. The scenarios are organized by a 2x2 taxonomy covering Support, Defense, Repair, and Charm, which together capture different forms of support, boundary maintenance, trust repair, and rapport building. In each scenario, an LLM simulator plays the user, updates an emotion-relation state after each turn, and maps the final state to an anchor-based score. This design makes EIBench both an evaluation benchmark and a training environment: the final state gives the outcome reward, while the per-turn state updates provide dense feedback for RL. We evaluate 15 open- and closed-source LLMs. Current models perform well on support and rapport-building scenes, but struggle with boundary maintenance under user pressure. To improve the EI ability of LLMs, we propose Centered Turn-Credit GRPO (CTC-GRPO), a GRPO extension that reuses the simulator's per-turn state updates as dense turn-level feedback while preserving the final outcome reward. CTC-GRPO improves Qwen3-8B from -22.4 to +22.4 on EIBench and also improves on out-of-distribution evaluations including SAGE (+12.4) and EQBench3 (+20.9%). Our results show that simulator-tracked user states can support both evaluation and training for multi-turn emotion management.

</details>


### [135] [LLM-Assisted Stance Detection in Scientific Discourse: A Test Case in Bayesian Cognitive Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15566)
*Eyup Engin Kucuk,Tarik Kelestemur,Ömer Dağlar Tanrikulu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在理论复杂、解释性强的定性编码任务中，如何利用大语言模型（LLM）实现可扩展的专家级标注。以判断作者是否将贝叶斯模型视为心理与神经机制的真实描述（现实主义）或仅作为数学工具（工具主义）为例，提出结合理论驱动的编码手册、专家标注参考集、诊断引导的提示优化搜索，生成适用于三个前沿LLM（GPT-5.1、Claude Sonnet 4.6、Gemini 3 Pro Preview）的零样本统一提示。最终提示在保留率上达到0.76（ICC=0.79，α=0.74），且所有诊断指标达标。在6,858条引文上的部署显示，三模型在引文层面具有高一致性（ICC=0.80，α=0.76，组合=0.78），文章层面排名稳定性极佳（r=0.96–0.97）。结果显示，总体偏向弱现实主义，但多数文章立场不单一：仅1.4%使用单一立场，59.5%跨越四个以上等级。低层次感知/运动类文章现实主义得分显著高于高层次认知类（p<.001，d=0.60），验证了长期存在的质性直觉。该框架为类似理论密集型任务提供可推广的方法论范例，而非适用于所有定性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 定性编码在社会科学中至关重要，但专家标注难以规模化。尽管大语言模型（LLM）提供了扩展可能性，但在目标构念具有解释性、理论负载重且间接表达时，需谨慎验证其有效性。本文聚焦于一个极具挑战性的案例：识别作者对贝叶斯模型是持现实主义（视为真实心理/神经机制）还是工具主义（视为有用数学工具）立场，旨在建立一种可信赖、可扩展的自动化编码方法。

Method: 研究采用理论驱动的代码书、专家标注的参考数据集，通过诊断引导的提示优化搜索，为三种前沿大语言模型（GPT-5.1、Claude Sonnet 4.6、Gemini 3 Pro Preview）生成共享的零样本提示。随后进行多评分者信度分析，评估模型间一致性，并在大规模语料（6,858条引文，210篇文章）上部署验证。

Result: 最终提示在保持率上达到0.76（ICC=0.79，α=0.74），所有诊断标准满足。在大规模文本上，三模型在引文层面达成高一致性（ICC=0.80，α=0.76，组合=0.78），文章层面排名高度稳定（r=0.96–0.97）。结果显示，整体倾向弱现实主义，但文章内部立场多样：仅1.4%为单一立场，59.5%跨越四个及以上等级。低层次感知/运动类文章现实主义得分显著更高（p<.001，d=0.60），支持已有质性观察。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了一种由专家主导、面向理论密集型定性编码任务的可推广框架。该方法通过系统化提示设计与严格可靠性检验，使大语言模型在复杂解释性任务中具备可信应用潜力，但其适用范围应限于类似高理论密度的任务，而非所有定性分析场景。

Abstract: Qualitative coding is central to social science, but expert annotation is difficult to scale. LLMs offer a possible extension, yet require careful validation when the target construct is interpretive, theoretically loaded, and only indirectly expressed. We study this problem in a difficult case: detecting whether authors treat Bayesian models as descriptions of mental and neural mechanisms (realism) or as useful mathematical tools (instrumentalism). Our method combines a theory-driven codebook, expert-coded reference annotations, a diagnostic-gated prompt-optimization search yielding a shared zero-shot prompt for three frontier LLMs (GPT-5.1, Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 3 Pro Preview), and multi-rater reliability analysis. The final prompt achieved a held-out combined reliability score of 0.76 (harmonic mean of ICC = 0.79 and $α$ = 0.74), with all diagnostics satisfied. Deployed on 6,858 quotes from 210 articles, the three LLMs reached substantial quote-level agreement (ICC = 0.80; $α$ = 0.76; combined = 0.78) and near-perfect article-level rank stability ($r$ = 0.96-0.97 across rater pairs). The corpus was predominantly weakly realist, but article-level stances were rarely uniform: only 1.4% of articles used a single band, while 59.5% spanned four or more. Low-level perception/motor articles scored 8.8 Realism points higher than high-level cognition articles ($p < .001$, $d = 0.60$), quantifying a long-held qualitative intuition. We present this as an expert-led case study; the framework is intended to generalize to similar theoretically demanding tasks, not to all qualitative analysis.

</details>


### [136] [LLM Judges Have Dark Current: A Psychometric Datasheet for LLM-as-a-Judge Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15610)
*Hiroyasu Usami,Keisuke Hara,Ayato Tsuboi,Naohiko Matsuda*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Judge Datasheet的计量协议，用于系统化评估大语言模型作为评判者（LLM-as-a-judge）的性能，强调应将模型视为测量仪器而非简单指标输出。该协议涵盖暗电流、跨敏感性、位置偏差、目标敏感度及平局处理准则等维度，揭示了模型在不同输入条件下的稳定性与偏见。案例研究显示，不同模型在真空环境、质量梯度响应和位置敏感性上表现各异，且提示词仅改变判断标准而非分辨能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型作为评判者常被简化为准确率或胜率等单一指标，但缺乏对评判过程本身的系统性评估。这种做法忽视了模型内在的偏差与稳定性问题，导致评估结果不可靠且难以复现。因此需要建立一套类似仪器校准的标准化评估框架，以确保下游评价的可信度。

Method: 提出并应用Judge Datasheet协议，通过五项核心指标评估模型：1）真真空条件下的暗电流；2）相同质量表面变化下的稳定交叉敏感性；3）位置引起的虚假偏好；4）在可控质量梯度上的目标敏感度；5）由平局规则引发的判别准则。结合方向-稳定性分解分析，区分真实偏好与位置偏差。

Result: 实验表明：Llama-3.1-8B存在高暗电流与展示冲突型零差偏好；Qwen2.5-14B虽清洁但存在稳定与位置过度区分混合；Qwen2.5-32B表现最佳，具备低暗电流、低交叉敏感性和低位置偏差。严格平局规则可消除虚假偏好，但可能掩盖微弱信号。最终发现，提示词影响的是判断标准而非分辨能力。

Conclusion: 本文不验证任何下游机制假设，而是贡献了一个面向评判模型的计量学协议——即在做出下游评价前，必须先对评判工具本身进行系统性校准。这有助于提升开放式模型评估的透明性、可重复性与科学性。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-judge systems are now routinely used for open-ended model evaluation, where human preference annotation is costly, slow, and difficult to reproduce. Yet these judges are often reported as scalar accuracy, win-rate, or agreement devices. We argue that a judge should instead be reported as a measurement instrument. We introduce a Judge Datasheet protocol that measures dark current under true-vacuum inputs, stable cross-sensitivity to same-quality surface variation, positional false preference, target sensitivity on a controlled quality ladder, and the criterion or operating point induced by tie instructions. The direction-stability decomposition reveals that apparent Delta0 preference can be stable surface response or disguised position bias. In a three-judge open-weight case study, Llama-3.1-8B shows high dark current and presentation-conflicted Delta0 behavior, Qwen2.5-14B is vacuum-clean and target-sensitive but mixes stable and positional over-discrimination, and Qwen2.5-32B is vacuum-clean with low stable cross-sensitivity and low positional false preference. A strict tie criterion eliminates Qwen32B Delta0 false preference but absorbs marginal Delta1 target signals into ties while preserving Delta5 sensitivity. The results show that prompting moves the criterion, not the resolution. We do not claim that the downstream mechanism hypothesis that motivated this work is confirmed; the contribution is a metrological protocol for measuring the measuring device before downstream claims are made.

</details>


### [137] [Distilling Examples into Task Instructions: Enhanced In-Context Learning for Real-World B2B Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15641)
*Guy Rotman,Adi Kopilov,Danit Berger Zalmanson,Omri Allouche*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了在低资源场景下，上下文学习（ICL）在专业化领域中的有效性，特别是在复杂多参与方的B2B对话分类任务中。作者提出了一个名为	exttt{Call Playbook}的新数据集，包含五个基于真实销售对话的任务。为解决传统ICL在长上下文时的性能下降问题，提出了一种新的知识提取方法，将冗长示例压缩为紧凑、可解释的结构化分类标准和精确任务描述，实现99%的令牌使用减少，并提升宏平均AUC达7%，且在上下文增长时仍保持稳定，优于现有压缩基线。该框架支持直接调整分类逻辑，增强了透明性、效率与用户交互能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上下文学习在处理复杂、多参与方的B2B对话时，因上下文过长导致性能下降，尤其在多示例拼接时效果不佳，缺乏可解释性和可维护性，限制了其在实际应用中的可用性。

Method: 提出一种新型知识提取方法，将原始的冗长示例转化为紧凑、结构化的分类规则与任务描述；结合	exttt{Call Playbook}数据集，实现高效、可解释的少样本分类。

Result: 相比传统ICL，新方法减少99%的令牌使用，宏平均AUC提升最高7%，在上下文增长时表现稳定，优于现有压缩方法（F1下降超过9点），并支持分类逻辑的直接修改。

Conclusion: 所提方法显著提升了低资源环境下复杂对话分类的性能与实用性，具备高可解释性、高效性与可交互性，适用于真实世界自然语言处理系统。

Abstract: In-context learning (ICL) is the standard method for low-resource classification, yet its efficacy in specialized domains remains largely unexplored. We address the challenge of classifying semantically complex, multi-party B2B conversations, where traditional ICL encounters significant limitations, especially as context length increases due to the concatenation of multiple few-shot examples. We introduce the \texttt{Call Playbook} dataset, featuring five classification tasks derived from real-world B2B conversations targeting core sales concepts. To bridge the gap between performance and practical utility, we propose novel knowledge extraction methods that distill verbose examples into compact, interpretable representations of structured classification criteria and precise task descriptions. Our approach achieves a 99\% reduction in token usage and improves macro-averaged AUC by up to 7\% over traditional ICL. Notably, it remains robust as context grows, unlike advanced token compression baselines which degrade by over 9 F1 points. Importantly, our framework enables direct refinement of classification logic, addressing critical needs for transparency, efficiency, and user interaction in real-world NLP applications.

</details>


### [138] [Extending Item Response Theory for Efficient and Meaningful Multilingual Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15643)
*Gili Lior,Tzviel Frostig,Gabriel Stanovsky,Matan Eyal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Multilingual-IRT的统一统计框架，用于解决多语言基准测试中评估规模大、自动翻译错误难以发现以及通用与文化特定知识混淆的问题。该框架通过引入每种语言的难度偏差、分离内容与语言影响的区分度，以及每种语言的能力残差来改进评估。在MMLU-Pro-X数据集上对25个大型语言模型在29种语言上的应用表明，其拟合参数支持三项实际应用：预测未观测到的（项目，LLM，语言）实例，误差比基于准确率的最强基线低11-16%；在所有28种非英语语言中识别出潜在的翻译错误，而基于准确率的基线仅集中在少数语言；恢复被准确率基线遗漏的文化特定题目。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多语言基准测试在评估大型语言模型跨语言性能方面至关重要，但存在三个主要问题：评估规模随语言数量线性增长，自动翻译引入的错误难以在大规模下察觉，以及部分题目混淆了通用知识与文化特定知识。这些问题限制了评估的效率和准确性。

Method: 提出Multilingual-IRT框架，扩展项目反应理论，引入每种语言的难度偏差、分离内容与语言影响的区分度，以及每种语言的能力残差，从而实现更精确的跨语言评估。

Result: 在MMLU-Pro-X数据集上对25个大型语言模型在29种语言的应用中，该框架显著提升了预测未观测实例的准确性（降低11-16%的二元交叉熵），有效识别出分布广泛的翻译错误，并成功恢复了被传统方法忽略的文化特定题目。

Conclusion: Multilingual-IRT提供了一个统一且有效的统计框架，能够克服现有多语言评估中的关键挑战，提升评估的准确性、覆盖率和可解释性，为大型语言模型的跨语言能力评估提供了新范式。

Abstract: Multilingual benchmarks are central to evaluating large language models (LLMs) across languages, but they suffer from three issues: exhaustive evaluation scales linearly with the number of languages, automatic translation introduces errors that are easily missed at scale, and some items conflate general and culture-specific knowledge. We address all three with a unified statistical framework, Multilingual-IRT, which extends Item Response Theory with per-language difficulty deviations, split discriminability separating content from language effects, and per-language ability residuals. Fitting Multilingual-IRT on 25 LLMs across 29 languages of MMLU-Pro-X, we show that its fitted parameters support three practical applications: predicting unobserved (item, LLM, language) instances with 11-16% lower binary cross-entropy than the strongest accuracy-based baseline, surfacing candidate translation errors distributed across all 28 non-English languages, whereas accuracy-based baselines concentrate detections in a few languages, and recovering culture-specific items that accuracy-based baselines miss.

### [139] [Beyond English: Uncovering the Multilingual Gap in Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15714)
*Hanyang Chen,Hongliang Li,Jiarui Cao,Yang Li,Yang Jiang,Haonan Wen,Kaiyu Huang,Shengnan Guo,Huaiyu Wan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在多语言指令遵循中的表现。通过扩展现有基准数据集，构建多语言指令，并在仿真环境中评估多个代表性VLA模型，发现仅以英语训练的模型在其他语言上性能显著下降，即使其语言主干具备多语言能力。分析表明，性能下降与指令理解及动作执行均相关，且多语言指令引发的表征偏移可能是主要原因。为此，提出一种简单有效的多语言微调方法——多语言主成分对齐（Multilingual PCA Alignment），利用主成分分析对齐多语言表征，有效缩小多语言性能差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型主要在英语指令下进行训练和评估，尽管底层大语言模型具备多语言能力，但其是否能在VLA中有效迁移仍不明确。因此，亟需系统研究VLA模型在多语言指令下的表现及其局限性，以推动通用机器人政策在多语言环境中的应用。

Method: 1. 构建多语言指令数据集：将现有基准数据集中的指令翻译为多种语言；2. 在仿真环境中评估多个代表性VLA模型在多语言任务上的表现；3. 通过跨语言迁移行为分析和表示分析，探究性能下降的原因；4. 提出多语言主成分对齐（Multilingual PCA Alignment）方法，通过主成分分析提取并对齐多语言表征空间，提升多语言泛化能力。

Result: 实验揭示了显著的多语言性能差距：仅以英语训练的VLA模型在非英语指令下性能大幅下降；跨语言迁移分析表明，性能下降同时影响指令理解和动作执行；表示分析显示多语言指令导致表征偏移；提出的多语言主成分对齐方法能有效减少该差距，显著提升多语言任务表现。

Conclusion: 尽管底层语言模型具备多语言能力，但当前VLA模型在多语言指令遵循方面仍存在明显短板。多语言表征偏移是导致性能下降的关键因素。通过引入多语言主成分对齐的微调策略，可有效缓解这一问题，为构建真正具备多语言能力的通用机器人系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action models have recently demonstrated promising capabilities in learning generalist robot policies from large-scale multimodal data. However, most existing VLA systems are trained and evaluated primarily with English instructions, leaving their ability to understand and execute instructions in other languages largely unexplored. While the underlying large language models often possess multilingual capabilities, it remains unclear whether these multilingual capabilities transfer to VLAs during training. In this work, we present the first systematic study of multilingual instruction following in VLA models. We first construct multilingual instructions by extending existing benchmarks with translations of their instructions. Using these instructions, we evaluate several representative VLA models across a range of tasks in simulation settings. Our experiments reveal a significant multilingual gap: models trained primarily on English instructions exhibit substantial performance degradation when evaluated on other languages, even when the underlying language backbone is multilingual. We provide several findings and analyses to understand the multilingual gap. Cross-lingual transfer behavior analysis shows that performance drops correlate with both instruction understanding and action execution. Representation analyses suggest that multilingual instruction-caused representation shifts may contribute to the multilingual gap. Motivated by these findings, we further explore strategies to improve multilingual performance in VLAs. We propose a simple yet effective multilingual fine-tuning approach, Multilingual Principal Component Alignment, which leverages Principal Component Analysis to get the principal component subspace and align projected multilingual representations, effectively reducing the multilingual performance gap.

### [140] [Vernier: Probing Representational Misalignment Behind Lexical Gaps in Causal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15733)
*Zhenyu Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了指令微调的语言模型在因果推理任务中，当变量名被类型保持的占位符替换后，答案不一致的现象。通过配对视图权重更新作为工具，发现这种差异主要源于表示错位而非信息丢失。变量名探测器在占位符视图上表现更准确，激活修补实验表明决策标记的表示可在不同视图间传递答案身份。重新对齐视图的关键是基于原始和占位符提示的反事实增强，而答案子空间KL则主要强化中间答案信念的一致性。模型家族、规模和任务限制了成功边界，因果转移在Qwen系列中可靠，但在Llama和非因果重命名任务中表现较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究指令微调语言模型在变量名替换后因果推理结果不一致的根本原因，判断是信息丢失还是表示错位所致。

Method: 采用配对视图权重更新作为干预工具，结合变量名探测、激活修补（activation patching）及反事实增强等方法，分析模型在原始与占位符视图间的表征一致性与决策机制。

Result: 实验证明，答案不一致主要由表示错位引起；变量名探测性能提升，决策标记表示可跨视图转移答案身份；反事实增强有效对齐视图，但性能受限于模型架构、规模与任务类型。

Conclusion: 该现象并非因信息丢失，而是由于模型内部表示未对齐；通过反事实增强可部分修复错位，但其有效性受模型家族、规模和任务复杂性制约。

Abstract: Instruction-tuned language models can answer the same causal-reasoning question differently after its English variable names are replaced by type-preserving placeholders, although the structural causal model and the gold answer are unchanged. We ask whether this lexical gap reflects information loss in the placeholder view or a misaligned read-out from a representation that still carries answer-relevant content. Vernier uses a paired-view weight update as an instrument and then inspects the mechanism left after the gap closes. In the working regimes, the evidence favours representational misalignment. A variable-name probe becomes more accurate on the placeholder view, and activation patching on Qwen-7B, Qwen-14B, and Llama-3.1-8B shows that the decision-token representation can transfer answer identity between views. The update that realigns the views is counterfactual augmentation over original and placeholder prompts, while the answer-subspace KL mainly sharpens intermediate answer-belief agreement. Success is bounded by model family, scale, and task. CRASS transfer is reliable across Qwen scales and Llama, e-CARE remains weak, and preliminary non-causal rename tasks show a similar qualitative pattern.

### [141] [Retrievable Gradients: Continual Post-Training Without Cumulative Weight Drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15734)
*Weihang Su,Jiacheng Kang,Jingyan Xu,Qingyao Ai,Jianming Long,Hanwen Zhang,Bangde Du,Xinyuan Cao,Min Zhang,Yiqun Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ReGrad提出将梯度作为可检索的知识单元，通过离线预计算并存储文档特定梯度至梯度库，在推理时仅检索相关梯度进行临时权重调整，解决持续训练中的参数漂移问题。引入双层元学习目标优化梯度以提升下游任务适应性，实验表明其在通用与领域特定场景下均优于CPT和RAG基线，实现可扩展、可逆的参数化知识注入且无累积漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持续后训练会导致共享参数积累权重漂移，引发灾难性遗忘并损害模型泛化能力；而检索增强生成缺乏参数化知识的深度整合，因此需要一种既能避免参数漂移又能有效融合知识的新方法。

Method: 提出ReGrad框架，将梯度作为可检索的知识单元，离线预计算文档级梯度并存入索引梯度库，在推理时根据查询检索相关梯度进行临时权重调整；采用双层元学习目标对文档衍生梯度进行重构，使其成为适用于下游任务的通用化适应信号。

Result: 在通用和领域特定设置下的实验表明，ReGrad在性能上优于CPT和RAG基线，实现了可扩展、可逆的参数化知识注入，同时避免了权重漂移的累积。

Conclusion: ReGrad通过将梯度作为可检索的知识单元，并结合元学习优化梯度表示，成功实现了高效、稳定且可逆的持续知识注入，为解决持续学习中的参数漂移问题提供了新范式。

Abstract: Continual post-training enables models to absorb emerging knowledge after deployment, but repeatedly updating shared parameters can accumulate weight drift, potentially causing catastrophic forgetting and degrading general capabilities. Retrieval-augmented generation avoids such parameter drift, yet often lacks the depth of parametric knowledge integration. In this paper, we propose ReGrad (Retrievable Gradients), a new paradigm that treats gradients as retrievable units of knowledge. ReGrad pre-computes document-specific gradients offline, stores them in an indexed Gradient Bank, and retrieves only query-relevant gradients at inference time for temporary weight adaptation. However, raw language-modeling gradients are optimized for token-level document reconstruction rather than for query-driven knowledge use. We therefore introduce a bi-level meta-learning objective that reshapes document-derived gradients into generalizable adaptation signals for downstream tasks. Experiments across general and domain-specific settings show that \textsc{ReGrad} outperforms CPT and RAG baselines, enabling scalable and reversible parametric knowledge injection without accumulating weight drift.

### [142] [EHRNote-ChatQA: A Benchmark for Evidence-Grounded Multi-Turn Clinical Question Answering over Longitudinal Discharge Summaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15735)
*Jiyoun Kim,Muhan Yeo,Eunhye Jang,Jeewon Yang,Hangyul Yoon,Su Ji Lee,Hee Jo Han,Hee-Jae Jung,Doyun Kwon,Jun young Lee,Jaehun Lee,Jung-Oh Lee,Sunjun Kweon,Jong Hak Moon,Daseul Kim,Minjae Cho,Edward Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EHRNote-ChatQA 是首个针对患者多份出院总结的证据基础多轮临床问答基准，基于去标识化的 MIMIC-IV 数据构建，包含 967 个患者级别的多轮样本和 16,072 对由医学专家验证的问答对，涵盖八个临床类别。该基准通过专家指导的流程生成，并经 11 名医学专家审核修订。评估 22 个开源与闭源大语言模型发现：模型在证据溯源方面表现弱于内容回答，多轮错误会累积，且单轮临床问答性能无法可靠迁移至多轮场景。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有临床问答基准无法充分反映医疗专家在审查多份出院总结时需迭代整合信息并验证证据的实际工作场景，尤其缺乏对多轮、证据基础问答的评估。

Method: 结合出院总结结构化模板、专家设计的多轮问答模板与 LLM 生成，辅以 11 名医学专家对每一对问答进行评审与修订，构建高质量标注数据集。

Abstract: Discharge summaries are crucial clinical documents containing the context of a patient's overall hospital stay, and are routinely reviewed by medical experts for patient readmission, ongoing care, and diagnostic decision-making. When reviewing them, medical experts often must iteratively synthesize information across multiple summaries while verifying the evidence supporting each answer. Although large language models (LLMs) are increasingly explored for clinical question answering, existing benchmarks do not sufficiently reflect this setting: they often evaluate exam-style medical knowledge or focus on single-turn question answering with limited evidence-grounding evaluation. We introduce EHRNote-ChatQA, the first benchmark for evidence-grounded multi-turn clinical question answering over patients' multiple discharge summaries. Built from de-identified MIMIC-IV discharge summaries, EHRNote-ChatQA contains 967 patient-level multi-turn samples spanning one to five notes and 16,072 medical-expert-verified QA pairs (8,036 content questions, each paired with an evidence-grounding question) across eight clinical categories. The benchmark is constructed through an expert-informed pipeline combining discharge-summary structuring schema, expert-curated multi-turn QA templates, and LLM-based generation, followed by review and revision of every single QA sample by 11 medical experts. Benchmarking 22 open- and closed-source LLMs reveals several challenges, including that LLMs struggle more with evidence grounding than content answering, multi-turn errors compound across turns, and single-turn clinical QA performance does not reliably transfer to this setting. These findings establish EHRNote-ChatQA as a rigorous and practical benchmark for evaluating clinical QA systems. The dataset will be made publicly available through PhysioNet credentialed access.

*Molham Mohamed,Ali Hamdi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种基于自一致性重排序的自集成框架，通过生成多个候选答案并基于语义一致性选择最优答案，提升叙事问答任务的鲁棒性和准确性。在NarrativeQA数据集上，该方法显著提升了多个模型的表现，尤其在Pegasus-Large上提升达14.57%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖单一解码输出，易受生成波动影响，导致回答不完整或不一致，亟需更稳健的生成与选择机制。

Method: 采用多答案推理生成多个候选答案，利用语义相似性进行重排序，基于共识选择最终答案，无需修改底层模型架构。

Result: 在NarrativeQA数据集上，所有测试模型性能均提升，FLAN-T5-Base从82.32%提升至86.66%，Pegasus-Large从72.50%提升至87.07%，提升显著。

Abstract: Narrative question answering (NQA) is a challenging task in natural language processing that requires models to understand long textual contexts, capture relationships across events, and generate coherent responses. Despite recent advances in pretrained language models, most existing approaches rely on a single decoding output during inference, making them sensitive to generation variability and often resulting in incomplete or inconsistent answers .To address this limitation, we propose a self-ensemble Self-Consistency-Based reranking framework for narrative question answering. The proposed method generates multiple candidate answers for each story-question pair and selects the final answer based on semantic agreement among the generated responses. This allows the model to explore diverse answer formulations while improving robustness through consensus-based selection without requiring modifications to the underlying architecture .The framework combines pretrained and fine-tuned language generation with multi-answer inference and similarity-based reranking. We evaluate the proposed approach on the NarrativeQA dataset using multiple models, including FLAN-T5 (Base and Small) and Pegasus-Large, under both baseline and fine-tuned settings .Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method consistently improves performance across all models. In particular, FLAN-T5-Base achieves the best overall performance, improving from 82.32% to 86.66% (+4.34%) when combined with self-ensemble inference. Additionally, the largest improvement is observed with Pegasus-Large, which increases from 72.50% to 87.07% (+14.57%), highlighting the effectiveness of the proposed strategy.

### [144] [ttda704 at SemEval-2026 Task 6: Structured Chain-of-Thought Prompting for Political Evasion Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15770)
*Tai Tran Tan,An Dinh Thien*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究针对SemEval-2026任务6，提出两种方法：一是基于QLoRA的参数高效微调Qwen3模型（4B-32B），结合分层上采样与加权交叉熵损失缓解类别不平衡；二是采用结构化链式思维（CoT）提示推理型API模型（DeepSeek-V3.2和Grok-4-Fast）。实验表明，使用结构化CoT提示的推理模型显著优于基线微调方法。最佳系统为Grok-4-Fast结合扩展推理与少样本分层CoT提示，在子任务2（9类逃避策略）上达到0.5147的宏平均F1，子任务1（3类清晰度）达0.7979，分别在官方排行榜中位列第8名（共33队）和第13名（共41队）。消融实验揭示：在层次化标签体系中呈现类别有助于模型推理结构化，少量示例可校准任务理解；但最强提示方案间无显著差异，启用扩展推理模式能显著提升性能，因需多步语用分析以识别逃避意图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决美国总统访谈中问题-回答对的政治理由回避策略分类难题，尤其应对严重类别不平衡问题，并探索高效、可解释的模型方法。

Method: 对比两种范式：(1) 使用QLoRA对Qwen3系列模型进行参数高效微调，结合分层上采样与加权交叉熵损失；(2) 采用结构化链式思维（CoT）提示方式，利用DeepSeek-V3.2和Grok-4-Fast等具备推理能力的API模型。通过设计多层次提示策略，包括分层标签组织与少样本示例，增强模型对回避意图的多步语用分析能力。

Result: Grok-4-Fast配合扩展推理与少样本分层CoT提示，在子任务2上取得0.5147的宏平均F1，子任务1上达0.7979；分别排名第8（共33队）与第13（共41队）。消融实验表明，层次化标签结构与少样本示例有效促进模型推理，而开启扩展推理模式带来显著性能提升。

Conclusion: 结构化链式思维提示的推理型模型在政治回避策略分类任务中表现优于参数高效微调方法。提示设计中的层次化标签组织与少样本示例有助于模型任务理解，而启用扩展推理机制是实现高精度多步语用分析的关键。

Abstract: This paper describes our system for SemEval-2026 Task 6, which addresses the classification of political evasion strategies in English question-answer pairs extracted from U.S. presidential interviews. We systematically compare two distinct paradigms: (1) Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning of Qwen3 models (4B-32B) using QLoRA, enhanced with tiered upsampling and weighted cross-entropy loss to address severe class imbalance, and (2) structured Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting of reasoning-capable API models, namely DeepSeek-V3.2 and Grok-4-Fast. Our evaluation demonstrates that structured CoT prompting of reasoning-enabled models substantially outperforms our baseline parameter-efficient fine-tuning implementation in absolute Macro F1. Our best system, Grok-4-Fast with extended reasoning and few-shot hierarchical CoT prompting, achieves a Macro F1 of 0.5147 on Subtask 2 (9-class evasion) and 0.7979 on Subtask 1 (3-class clarity), ranking 8th out of 33 teams on Subtask 2 and 13th out of 41 teams on Subtask 1 on the official leaderboard. Furthermore, our ablation studies reveal key insights into effective prompt design for evasion detection: presenting labels within a hierarchical taxonomy helps structure model reasoning, while few-shot exemplars provide task calibration. However, the strongest prompt variants are not statistically distinguishable in Macro F1, and explicitly enabling extended reasoning modes yields substantial performance gains by facilitating the multi-step pragmatic analysis required to detect evasive intent.

### [145] [DYNA : Dynamic Episodic Memory Networks for Augmenting Large Language Models with Temporal Knowledge Graphs in Continuous Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15778)
*Ali Sarabadani,Mahtab Tajvidiyan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DYNA is a lightweight framework that enhances frozen LLMs with a temporal knowledge graph for updatable external memory, improving temporal recall and reducing forgetting without retraining.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs struggle to integrate new knowledge without forgetting old information or requiring costly retraining; existing methods like fine-tuning and standard RAG have limitations in preserving temporal context and retrieval accuracy.

Method: DYNA uses a temporal knowledge graph where events are nodes and timestamped directed edges represent temporal relations. It retrieves relevant information via random walks and centrality measures, then augments the LLM's response at query time.

Result: DYNA reduces catastrophic forgetting by ~7% compared to fine-tuning and improves temporal ordering by ~5% over standard RAG. Higher clustering coefficients in the graph correlate with better retrieval performance, indicating that graph structure influences effectiveness.

Conclusion: Episodic memory modeled as a temporal knowledge graph enables retraining-free LLM augmentation, and structural properties of the graph can predict retrieval success, offering insights for future memory-augmented systems.

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) struggle to incorporate new knowledge without forgetting or costly retraining. We propose DYNA, a lightweight framework that augments a frozen LLM with a temporal knowledge graph where events are nodes and temporal relations are directed, timestamped edges. The graph serves as an external, updatable memory. At query time, DYNA retrieves relevant nodes via random walks and centrality measures, then augments the LLM's response. Evaluated on three temporal recall tasks, DYNA reduces catastrophic forgetting by ~7% compared to fine-tuning and improves temporal ordering by ~5% over standard RAG. Higher graph clustering coefficients correlate with better retrieval, showing that graph structure matters. Contributions: (1) episodic memory as temporal KG, (2) retraining-free LLM augmentation, (3) graph properties as predictors of retrieval performance.

### [148] [The Truth Stays in the Family: Enhancing Contextual Grounding via Inherited Truthful Heads in Model Lineages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15821)

Method: 通过量化头级别的上下文真实性得分，分析不同模型家族中的得分一致性；利用注意力头权重的保留性验证该现象；提出基于软门控的TruthProbe策略以增强可信头的作用。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have produced many specialized multimodal LLMs (MLLMs) that share common foundational LLMs, forming distinct model lineages. It remains unclear whether a fundamental behavioral link exists between the foundational LLMs and downstream variants. We investigate this question by quantifying head-level context-truthfulness scores. Across diverse LLM and MLLM lineages, including Vicuna-, Qwen2.5-, LLaMA2-, and Mistral-based models, we find that Truth Scores are strongly preserved within model families, even after instruction tuning or multimodal adaptation. We further show that this inheritance is consistent with attention-head weight preservation, and that context-truthful heads attend to query-relevant evidence. Building on this finding, we propose TruthProbe, a soft-gating strategy that amplifies context-truthful heads while preserving other head contributions. TruthProbe improves contextual truthfulness on HaluEval and reduces multimodal hallucination on POPE and CHAIR, with base-LLM Truth Scores transferring effectively to their fine-tuned LLM and MLLM descendants. ### [149] [When Correct Edges Cannot Be Verified: A Provenance Gap in Incomplete KGQA and a Provenance-Favoring Completion Policy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15833)
*Yongqi Kang,Yu Fu,Yong Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在不完整知识图谱问答（IKGQA）中，文本可验证性是否真正反映边的正确性。通过分析标准随机删除协议下的真实删除三元组，发现76-96%的正确补全边在广泛检索下仍无文本支持，表明文本可验证性衡量的是来源可信度而非正确性。大多数自由基风格的事实并不在文本中以头尾共现形式出现。因此，边补全的核心问题从“边是否正确”转变为“在来源不确定的情况下是否应承认”。为此提出TGComplete，一种注重来源的承认策略，在推理断点处检索证据，通过轻量级循环验证候选边，并在缺乏支持时选择回避。相比生成式补全基线GoG，TGComplete在黄金标准上实现了更高的边精确率（15-21% vs 3-14%），EM无显著损失，且承认边的严格可验证性提高3.1-7.4倍，代价是召回率下降。该方法并非全面更优，而是在精确度、可验证性与召回之间的一个有原则的权衡点，适用于对审计性要求高的场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将文本支持视为边质量的代理，但未系统检验其是否真正反映正确性。本文旨在回答一个关键问题：文本可验证性是否真的追踪边的正确性？

Method: 利用标准随机删除协议提供的真实删除三元组，评估补全边的正确性与文本支持情况；通过在推理断点检索证据并进行轻量级循环验证，提出一种基于来源的承认策略TGComplete。

Result: 76-96%的正确补全边无文本支持，说明文本可验证性衡量的是来源而非正确性；多数正确答案不依赖于无支持的边；TGComplete相比基线在精确率和可验证性上显著提升，但召回率下降。

Conclusion: 文本可验证性反映的是边的来源可信度，而非正确性。边补全的核心问题应从‘是否正确’转向‘是否应在来源不确定时承认’。TGComplete是一种面向可审计性的有原则的折中方案，适用于需要高可验证性的场景。

Abstract: Incomplete Knowledge Graph Question Answering (IKGQA) requires completing missing edges to continue reasoning. A growing line of work verifies completed edges against retrieved text, treating textual support as a proxy for edge quality. We ask a question that, to our knowledge, has not been systematically tested: does textual verifiability actually track correctness? Exploiting the gold deleted triples provided by the standard random-deletion protocol, we measure both. The finding is counterintuitive: among gold-correct completed edges, 76-96% have no supporting passage even under exhaustive retrieval, robustly across deletion rates (20%/40%), datasets (CWQ/WebQSP), and relation types (structural, commonsense, long-tail). Most Freebase-style facts simply do not occur as head-tail co-mentions in text. Textual faithfulness therefore measures provenance, not correctness -- separated by a paradigm-level gap no in-corpus retrieval closes. This reframes edge completion. Since most completed edges -- correct or not -- are causally redundant for the answer (95-97% of correct answers do not depend on any unsupported edge), the central question shifts from "is the edge correct?" to "admit or abstain under provenance uncertainty?" Within this framing we present TGComplete, a provenance-favoring admission policy that retrieves evidence at a reasoning breakpoint, verifies a candidate through a lightweight loop, and abstains when support is absent. Against the generate-to-complete baseline GoG, it attains higher edge precision against gold (15-21% vs 3-14%), with no statistically detectable EM loss and 3.1-7.4 times higher strict faithfulness of admitted edges -- at the cost of lower recall. We position TGComplete not as uniformly better, but as a principled point on a precision/provenance-recall trade-off, appropriate when auditability matters.

</details>


### [150] [SciOrch: Learning to Orchestrate Expert LLMs for Solving Frontier Multimodal Scientific Reasoning Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15872)
*Jingru Guo,Xiangyuan Xue,Lian Zhang,Wanghan Xu,Siki Chen,Philip Torr,Wanli Ouyang,Lei Bai,Zhenfei Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SciOrch 是一个训练轻量级 8B 模型来协调多个前沿大语言模型进行科学推理的框架。该框架通过分解问题、调用不同商业模型的 API 处理子任务，并整合结果生成答案。由于 API 调用成本高，传统强化学习不可行，因此采用基于 MCTS 的方法生成多样化推理路径，并使用 GRPO 风格训练优化。在 240 道题的测试集上，SciOrch 达到 56.66% 平均准确率，优于最强单模型 3.74%，优于多智能体基线 3.33%，且 API 成本低于典型多智能体方法的一半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型在前沿科学推理任务中表现不足，且不同模型在不同类型问题上各有优势，单一模型难以全面覆盖。现有评估方式忽略这种互补性，亟需一种能有效整合多个模型能力的协作机制。

Method: 提出 SciOrch 框架，利用一个 8B 轻量级模型作为协调器，通过分解问题、选择合适的商业模型进行 API 调用处理子任务，并合成最终答案；采用基于 MCTS 的策略生成多样化的执行路径，提取单步样本并使用 GRPO 风格训练优化协调器。

Result: 在包含 SGI-Reasoning 和 Scientists' First Exam 的 240 题测试集上，SciOrch 达到 56.66% 的平均准确率，超越最强单模型 3.74%，超越最强多智能体基线 3.33%，同时将 API 使用成本控制在典型多智能体方法的一半以下。

Conclusion: SciOrch 成功实现对多个前沿 LLM 的高效协同，显著提升科学推理性能，同时大幅降低资源消耗，为解决复杂推理任务提供了可扩展、低成本的新范式。

Abstract: Frontier scientific reasoning remains a major challenge for large language models (LLMs), where even the strongest commercial systems fall short of expert-level performance. A closer look at model behavior reveals substantial complementarity that single-model evaluation hides: different frontier models excel on different question types, and no single model captures the full picture. We present SciOrch, a framework that trains a lightweight 8B model to orchestrate frontier LLMs for scientific reasoning. The orchestrator decomposes each question, delegates sub-problems to selected commercial models through API calls, and synthesizes a final answer. Training such an orchestrator is fundamentally harder than conventional agentic RL: each action triggers an API call that is expensive in both dollar cost and latency, making standard online rollouts infeasible. We address this with MCTS-based approach, producing diverse orchestration trajectories, extracting per-node single-turn samples, and optimizing the orchestrator with GRPO-style training. On a 240-question test set spanning SGI-Reasoning and Scientists' First Exam, SciOrch reaches 56.66% average accuracy, outperforming the strongest single commercial model by 3.74% and the strongest multi-agent baseline by 3.33%. It also attains the best accuracy on both SGI and SFE with less than half the API cost of typical multi-agent methods.

### [151] [Free Energy Heuristics: Fast-And-Frugal Cognition as Active Inference Under Uncertain Precision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15877)
*Alex Bogdan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出元不确定性（meta-uncertainty）是决定链式思维（CoT）在不同任务中表现优劣的关键因素。当模型对自己的证据可靠性不确定时，额外推理会引入虚假信心，反而降低准确性。研究通过理论证明与实证验证，发现高元不确定性情境下，长CoT会导致显著准确率下降（平均下降17.3点），而有确定答案的任务则无此代价。该框架统一了贝叶斯推理与快速简约启发法，表明‘少即是多’并非对贝叶斯认知的否定，而是元不确定性状态的体现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究发现，链式思维（CoT）在数学和符号推理中有效，但在规划、伦理争议或无法自我验证的任务中反而有害。然而，缺乏一个系统性理论解释为何在某些情况下更多推理会适得其反。本文旨在揭示决定这一现象的核心机制——元不确定性，即模型对其自身证据可靠性的不确定性程度。

Method: 结合主动推断（active inference）与预期自由能最小化理论，构建数学模型并证明：在重尾先验精度条件下，最优策略会在有限个高有效性线索后停止整合信息；在下降主导性条件下，该策略等价于‘取最佳’（take-the-best）启发法。随后，设计并实施一项预注册实验，使用FEH-79基准测试集，在七种模型、五种CoT长度下进行7,875次响应分析，通过模拟与恢复相关性（rho > 0.96）评估元不确定性状态，并设定严格门控标准验证预测。

Result: 实验结果支持理论预测：在高元不确定性任务中，长CoT导致平均准确率下降17.3点（95% CI [7.7, 25.5]），且该效应具有显著的制度依赖性——在中大型模型中明显，前沿模型中呈方向性，弱模型中则不存在甚至逆转。而具有确定答案的任务未出现此类代价。

Conclusion: 链式思维是否有益取决于任务的元不确定性水平。高元不确定性下，更长的推理过程会因制造虚假信心而损害性能。该研究统一了贝叶斯推理与快速简约启发法，表明‘少即是多’是元不确定性状态的合理反应，而非对理性认知的挑战。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) improves large language models' performance in math and symbolic reasoning. But on planning, contested ethics, and tasks where the model cannot check itself, more reasoning makes things worse. Both effects are documented; what has been missing is a principled account of which property decides the outcome. We argue it is meta-uncertainty: how unsure the model is about the reliability of its own evidence. When that uncertainty is high, extra reasoning stops adding signal and starts manufacturing false confidence. We prove that the policy minimizing expected free energy under uncertain precision stops integrating cues after a finite number of high-validity ones when the precision prior is heavy-tailed (Theorem 2.6.1), and under a Descending Dominance condition, is sample-wise identical to take-the-best (Theorem 2.7.4). Fast-and-frugal heuristics and active inference are, then, two descriptions of the same computation. The prediction is that on high-meta-uncertainty items, longer CoT should degrade accuracy. We score the regime per item (simulate-and-recover rho > 0.96), build FEH-79, a benchmark of Knightian frames with matched controls, and run a pre-registered study across seven models (five open-weight 3B-32B, two frontier), five CoT lengths, and 7,875 responses. The gate, fixed before any data, required a negative interaction with posterior probability above 0.95 and an accuracy drop of more than 6 points. It held. The high-regime drop is 17.3 points (95% CI [7.7, 25.5]); matched items with definite answers show no cost. The effect is regime-dependent: decisive in capable mid-to-large models, directional in the two frontier systems, absent-to-reversed in the weakest. The framework answers when CoT helps and unifies the Bayesian and fast-and-frugal traditions: less-is-more effects are evidence about the meta-uncertainty regime, not against Bayesian cognition.

</details>


### [152] [Koshur Diacritizer: A Byte-Level Sequence-to-Sequence Model for Kashmiri Diacritic Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15883)
*Haq Nawaz Malik,Nahfid Nissar,Faizan Iqbal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Koshur Diacritizer，一个基于ByT5-small的字节级序列到序列模型，用于恢复克什米尔语文本中的元音符号。研究构建了一个包含23.7万对对齐的无符号与有符号克什米尔语句子的公开数据集，并采用脚本感知归一化、对齐验证和骨架保持推理等方法，确保恢复效果可靠且保留原始字母序列。实验在测试集上取得DERm为0.2012、WER为0.2159的成绩，专家评估平均准确率达77.5%。相关数据集、模型和源代码已公开，为克什米尔语及低资源语言的后续研究提供可复现基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克什米尔语在数字文本中常省略元音符号，导致歧义，影响自然语言处理应用。因此需要一种有效的方法来恢复这些缺失的符号，以提升下游任务性能。

Method: 采用ByT5-small字节级序列到序列模型，结合脚本感知归一化、对齐验证和骨架保持推理策略，实现克什米尔语元音符号的精准恢复。

Result: 在独立测试集上，模型达到DERm 0.2012和WER 0.2159；由母语语言学家评估，平均准确率为77.5%。

Conclusion: 所提出的Koshur Diacritizer框架在克什米尔语元音恢复任务中表现优异，其公开的数据集、模型与代码为低资源语言研究提供了可靠的基准。

Abstract: Kashmiri, an Indo-Aryan language written in a modified Perso-Arabic script, frequently omits diacritic marks in digital text, creating ambiguity and challenging downstream NLP applications. We present Koshur Diacritizer, a ByT5-small byte-level sequence-to-sequence model for restoring diacritics in Kashmiri text. To support this task, we release a publicly available dataset of 23.7k aligned undiacritized diacritized Kashmiri sentence pairs. The proposed framework combines script-aware normalization, alignment validation, and skeleton-preserving inference to ensure reliable restoration while maintaining the original base-letter sequence. Experimental results on a held-out test set achieve a DERm of 0.2012 and a WER of 0.2159. Additionally, evaluation by a native Kashmiri linguistic expert yields a mean accuracy of 77.5%. The dataset, model, and source code are publicly released to provide a reproducible baseline for Kashmiri diacritic restoration and future low-resource language research.

### [153] [Neuron Level Analysis of Large Language Model in Legal Domain Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15884)
*Eri Onami,Youmi Ma,Shuhei Kurita,Naoaki Okazaki*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究对大语言模型（LLM）在法律领域的推理进行了神经元级别的分析，比较了其与其他应用领域任务的表现。通过神经元归因得分对关键神经元进行排序和抑制，发现抑制特定关键神经元会显著降低目标任务的准确率，而随机抑制则无此影响。研究发现存在一小部分跨七项任务均起重要作用的神经元；一旦这些通用神经元被移除，其余神经元的抑制仅影响其对应的特定任务，表明每个模型中都存在真正任务特异性的神经元。在法律领域内，三个基准测试表现出较高的神经元重叠，且常被共同影响，提示存在跨越司法管辖区的法律共性神经元。此外，实验结果表明，关键神经元是否集中于中间MLP层可能取决于输入格式与内容，并非普遍规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型在法律领域推理中的神经机制，揭示其与其它应用领域任务之间的差异，识别具有任务特异性及跨任务共享的神经元，以理解模型内部表示的本质及其泛化能力。

Method: 采用神经元归因分数对七个开源大模型中的神经元影响力进行评估；通过系统性地抑制高影响力神经元与随机神经元，对比其对任务性能的影响，进而识别任务特异性与跨任务共享的神经元；分析不同任务间神经元分布模式，探讨其与输入格式、内容的关系。

Result: 1. 抑制关键神经元显著降低目标任务准确率，而随机抑制无显著影响；2. 存在少数跨任务共享的神经元；3. 一旦移除共享神经元，剩余神经元表现任务特异性；4. 法律领域任务间神经元重叠度高，暗示存在跨司法管辖区的法律共性神经元；5. 关键神经元分布受输入格式和内容影响，中间MLP层并非普遍存在关键神经元的区域。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在法律领域的推理依赖于一部分共享神经元和大量任务特异性神经元，且神经元的影响力分布受输入内容特性制约，而非固定于特定网络层。这为理解模型在专业领域中的可解释性与泛化机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: We presented a neuron-level analysis of legal-domain reasoning in LLMs, comparing it with other applied domain tasks across seven open-weight models. Using neuron attribution scores to rank and suppress influential neurons, we confirmed that suppressing the identified neurons collapses accuracy on the target task, whereas suppressing the same number of random neurons does not. We further found a small subset of neurons influential across all seven tasks; once these are removed, suppressing the remaining neurons degrades only the task they were identified from, revealing genuinely task-specific neurons in every model studied. Within the legal domain, the three benchmarks exhibit relatively high neuron overlap and tend to be affected jointly, suggesting of legal components neurons that span jurisdictions. The distribution of identified neurons in our experiments suggests that the hypothesis that influential neurons are concentrated in middle MLP layers may depend on the input format and content, rather than being a universal phenomenon.

### [154] [BALTO: Balanced Token-Level Policy Optimization for Hallucination Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15893)
*Ning Li,Zixuan Guo,Yan Xu,Wenbo Fei,Yifan Niu,Chang Luo,Yasheng Wang,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: BALTO 是一种用于缓解大语言模型幻觉的平衡标记级策略优化框架。它通过提取可验证的事实性主张，基于参考上下文进行验证，并将主张级别的判断投影到标记级别标签。引入了平衡的标记级信用分配机制，重新分配不受支持内容的概率质量到忠实内容，而非抑制整个响应。理论分析表明，与响应级奖励相比，BALTO在训练稳定性和优化效率方面具有优势。在 ConFiQA、RAGTruth 和 FinLLM-Eval 上的实验显示，BALTO 在所有六个模型-基准设置中实现了最高的忠实度，并在 Q-Score 上持续优于现有后训练基线，展现出更强的忠实度-信息量权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在知识密集型场景中面临幻觉问题，尽管强化学习是潜在解决方案，但响应级忠实度奖励存在粒度不匹配问题，局部幻觉可能导致受支持内容被错误惩罚。现有细粒度反馈（如主张级验证和标记级奖励）仍存在信用分配不平衡问题，引发长度、冗余或优化噪声偏差。

Method: BALTO 框架首先提取可验证的事实性主张，利用参考上下文进行验证，并将主张级别的判断映射为标记级别的标签。设计了一种平衡的标记级信用分配机制，将概率质量从不受支持的内容转移至忠实内容，避免整体压制响应。

Result: 在 ConFiQA、RAGTruth 和 FinLLM-Eval 三个基准上的实验表明，BALTO 在所有六种模型-基准组合中均达到最高忠实度，并在 Q-Score 上显著优于现有后训练方法，表现出更优的忠实度与信息量之间的平衡。

Conclusion: BALTO 通过细粒度的标记级信用分配机制，有效缓解了幻觉问题，提升了训练稳定性与优化效率，在多个基准上实现领先性能，证明其在知识密集型任务中具备优越的实用性。

Abstract: Hallucinations remain a major obstacle to deploying large language models (LLMs) in knowledge-intensive settings, where generated responses must be faithfully grounded in provided evidence. Reinforcement learning (RL) is a promising direction for hallucination mitigation, but response-level faithfulness rewards suffer from a granularity mismatch: localized hallucinations can cause supported content to receive spurious penalties. Although recent work introduces fine-grained feedback such as claim-level verification and token-level rewards, unbalanced credit assignment can still induce length, verbosity, or optimization-noise biases. We propose BALTO, a Balanced Token-level Policy Optimization framework for hallucination mitigation. BALTO extracts checkable factual claims, verifies them against the reference context, and projects claim-level judgments to token-level labels. A balanced token-level credit assignment mechanism is introduced into the framework. This design redistributes probability mass from unsupported content toward faithful content, rather than suppressing the entire response. We systematically analyze the limitations of response-level rewards from a theoretical standpoint, and prove BALTO's advantages in training stability and optimization efficiency for hallucination mitigation. Experiments on ConFiQA, RAGTruth, and FinLLM-Eval show that BALTO achieves the highest faithfulness across all six model--benchmark settings and consistently outperforms existing post-training baselines in Q-Score, demonstrating a stronger faithfulness--informativeness trade-off.

</details>


### [155] [Control-Plane Placement Shapes Forgetting: An Architectural Study of Agent Memory Across Thirteen System Configurations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15903)
*Dongxu Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLM）在智能体记忆流水线中的位置对遗忘机制有效性的影响，通过对比13种配置在385个对抗性案例上的表现，揭示了三种放置模式的互补性：确定性原语适用于词汇/时间类遗忘但无法处理归一化问题；插入时使用LLM可恢复归一化但无助于意图感知删除；而变异时钩子则能有效实现意图感知删除，并显著提升整体遗忘性能（91.7–93.2%），且成本低、延迟可控。作者提出ForgetEval基准测试套件与适配器协议，支持异构记忆存储接入，具备高一致性与可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估记忆召回能力，忽视了遗忘失败这一关键问题。真实系统中，遗忘错误远多于召回错误，因此亟需一个能全面评估遗忘行为的评测框架和方法。

Method: 设计并实现ForgetEval评测体系，包含1000例模板案例与385例对抗性案例（含人工与LLM生成），采用确定性子串匹配评分；开发六种方法的Adapter协议，支持不同记忆存储系统的集成；通过13种系统配置对比分析LLM在不同阶段介入的记忆效果。

Result: 三种放置策略具有部分互补性：确定性方法在词汇/时间类别上有效但无法处理归一化；插入时使用LLM可解决归一化问题（100%成功率），但无法应对意图感知删除；变异时引入LLM可实现意图感知删除（78–85%），整体遗忘准确率达91.7–93.2%，每轮运行成本仅$0.17，单次变异延迟为2.3秒，优于传统确定性方法（64–191毫秒）。外部验证集与多人标注确认结果稳健。

Conclusion: LLM在记忆流水线中的介入时机决定了其对不同类型遗忘失败的修复能力。结合不同阶段的部署策略，可实现更全面的遗忘鲁棒性。本研究提出的ForgetEval与适配器协议为未来记忆系统评估提供了可复用工具。

Abstract: Where an LLM sits in an agent memory pipeline -- between the recall plane that retrieves stored facts (extensively benchmarked) and the control plane that mutates them via supersede, release, purge (largely untested) -- shapes which forgetting failure modes the system recovers. Comparing thirteen system configurations on a 385-case adversarial surface, we observe three placement regimes with partly complementary coverage: deterministic primitives suffice for lexical/temporal categories but fail canonicalization (5% on identifier-obfuscation, 0% on cross-lingual); inscribe-time LLM recovers canonicalization (100%) but cannot help intent-aware deletion (0% on prefix-collision and compound-fact); a mutation-time hook recovers intent-aware deletion (78-85%) and brightens nearly all categories simultaneously (91.7-93.2% overall, $0.17 per 385-case run, 2.3s/case mutation latency vs. 64-191ms/case deterministic, recall path unchanged).
  We expose the trade-off via ForgetEval, a 1000-case templated suite plus a 385-case adversarial layer (132 hand-crafted + 253 LLM-drafted oracle-validated) scored by deterministic substring match, paired with a six-method Adapter Protocol with honest N/A scoring that lets heterogeneous memory stores enter in 130 lines. Admission is corroborated by 10-annotator IAA (Fleiss' kappa = 0.958) and a 77-case external-authored subset (four blind contributors) that replicates the canonicalization asymmetry and amplifies the joint-placement lift (+27.8 pt). Production failures are predominantly forgetting failures rather than recall failures, yet existing benchmarks measure only recall. ForgetEval and all adapters are released under MIT.

### [156] [Calibrated Triage, Not Autonomy: Confidence Estimation for Medical Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15910)
*Reza Khanmohammadi,Kundan Thind,Mohammad M. Ghassemi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了视觉-语言模型在医学图像问答中的可靠性问题，发现模型常依赖语言先验而非图像信息，导致看似可信却错误的答案。研究评估了七种置信度估计器在五种开源大模型和三个医学视觉问答数据集上的表现，强调置信度信号对安全部署的关键作用。结果显示，标准指标无法有效区分方法，而经过域外温度缩放的自报告置信度虽可改善校准但不提升实际可用性。真正决定可用性的因素是高置信度区域的准确性：最佳置信度估计器仅在1-4%的错误中表现出高置信，而最差者高达41-45%。不同模型与领域间无统一最优估计器。安全交接依赖于两个层面：基础模型能力设定上限（如放射学可处理约三分之一病例，病理几乎不可），置信度层决定能否达到此上限。结论：当前模型应作为经校准的筛选工具，将安全案例自动化，其余交由医生处理。所有数据、标签与代码均已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学视觉-语言模型常依赖语言先验而非真实图像信息，导致答案看似可信却错误，亟需可靠的置信度评分来识别何时应避免自主决策，保障临床安全。

Method: 评估七种置信度估计器在五种开源大模型和三个医学视觉问答数据集（涵盖临床影像、放射学、病理）上的表现，所有探针均仅在自然图像上训练且未进行适配。采用有界选择性预测框架（仅当置信度超过阈值时自动处理，否则转交医生），对比各方法在不同场景下的表现。

Result: 标准评估指标（如区分度、校准性）无法有效区分置信度估计器；即使廉价的自报告置信度经温度缩放后校准性提升，也未提高实际可用性。关键差异在于高置信度区域的错误率：最佳估计器仅1-4%错误被高置信误判，最差者达41-45%。模型能力上限显著影响可部署范围（放射学约30%可安全自动化，病理几乎为零），置信度层决定能否触及上限。

Conclusion: 当前视觉-语言模型在医学影像中的角色应为经校准的三甲筛选工具，而非完全自治。只有通过可靠置信度评分识别出的安全案例才可自动化，其余必须交由临床医生处理。模型部署的核心是‘可信赖的退让’，而非单纯准确率。所有实验数据与代码已公开。

Abstract: A vision-language model can answer a question about a medical image fluently and confidently while barely using the image, leaning instead on language priors. In medicine this is the failure that matters most, because the answer looks trustworthy and is not, and the only protection is a confidence score reliable enough to tell the system when to abstain. We ask a deployment question rather than an accuracy one: how much imaging work a model can safely handle alone, and which confidence signal makes that possible. We evaluate seven confidence estimators across five open-weight LVLMs and three medical visual-question-answering datasets spanning broad clinical imaging, radiology, and pathology, with every probe trained only on natural images and applied without adaptation. Recast as bounded selective prediction (automate a case only when confidence clears a threshold, defer the rest), the comparison is cautionary. The standard metrics are poor guides: discrimination barely separates the methods, and the weak calibration of a cheap self-report is cheaply removed by off-domain temperature scaling without changing deployable yield. What distinguishes a usable estimator is the high-confidence region a clinician acts on: the weakest baselines are confidently wrong on 41 to 45 percent of their errors against 1 to 4 percent for the best probe, and no estimator is reliably best across domains or models. Safe handoff is governed at two levels: base-model competence sets a ceiling, so a well-calibrated score recovers roughly a third of radiology cases at a 20 percent error tolerance but almost none of pathology; the confidence layer then decides how much of that ceiling is reachable. The usable role today is calibrated triage, not autonomy: automate the cases a calibrated score marks safe, route the rest to a clinician. We release all outputs, correctness judgments, and confidence scores, with code.

### [157] [Interactor: Agentic RL oriented Iterative Creation for Ad Description Generation in Sponsored Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15911)
*Penghui Wei,Jiayu Wu,Chao Ye,Zhi Guo,Shuanglong Li,Lin Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出Interactor框架，通过多轮迭代生成高质量广告描述。该框架利用基于代理的强化学习（agentic RL），结合多个生成式奖励模型（GenRMs）对广告描述进行多维度评估（如知识容量、着陆页一致性），并提供反馈以指导生成模型持续优化。实验表明，该方法显著优于现有技术，在工业数据集上提升广告描述质量，自2026年5月起已在主流搜索广告系统上线，有效提升广告收入与用户体验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统广告标题侧重吸引点击，而广告描述具有更长文本空间，具备融入世界知识、精准响应用户搜索意图并展示产品细节的优势。然而，现有方法难以有效生成知识丰富且忠实于实际内容的描述，因此需要一种能持续优化、兼顾准确性和信息量的生成机制。

Method: 提出Interactor框架，采用多轮迭代的生成范式，将生成模型作为策略（policy），在由多个定制化生成式奖励模型（GenRMs）构成的环境中进行交互。GenRMs从知识能力、着陆页一致性等维度评估初始生成结果，并提供二值信号和推理反馈；策略根据反馈逐步优化描述内容，实现持续改进。

Result: 在工业级数据集上的实验结果显示，Interactor显著优于当前最先进的方法，在生成知识丰富、忠实度高的广告描述方面表现优异。自2026年5月起已部署于主流搜索广告系统，带来广告收入增长与用户体验提升。

Conclusion: Interactor框架通过融合多轮反馈与代理式强化学习，实现了高质量广告描述的自动构建，为广告内容生成提供了可扩展、可落地的新范式。

Abstract: This paper focuses on automatically generating informative ad descriptions in sponsored search. Unlike ad titles which are usually optimized to attract user click feedbacks, ad descriptions have a longer text span and possess the potential of incorporating world knowledge to address user search intents while presenting the fine-grained selling points of the ads. We propose Interactor, a multi-turn iterative creation framework optimized with agentic RL for ad description generation. The generation model acts as a policy that interacts with a customized environment consisting of multiple generative reward models. Given initial generations by the policy, the customized GenRMs evaluate multi-dimensional qualities including knowledge capacity and landing page consistency, providing both binary signals and reasoning feedbacks. The policy then iteratively refines the descriptions based on such feedbacks to ensure continuous improvement. Experiments on industrial datasets show that the Interactor framework significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches in generating knowledge-rich and faithful ad descriptions. Since May 2026, it has been deployed online in a leading search ads system, contributing to both ad revenue and user experience.

</details>


### [158] [Contaminated Collaboration: Measuring Gender Bias Transfer in LLM-Assisted Student Writing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15914)
*Ariyan Hossain,Kazi Kamruzzaman Rabbi,Farig Sadeque,S M Taiabul Haque*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLM）中的性别偏见是否会影响使用这些系统的学生所撰写的生涯规划论文。通过实验发现，带有性别偏见的提示会引发模型生成具有性别差异的语言；而在使用带有偏见的LLM辅助写作时，学生撰写的针对女性角色的论文表现出显著更低的主动性，并提出更多刻板的职业建议，而针对男性的论文则未受明显影响。这种偏见传递是不对称的，主要抑制了女性目标人物的主动性。研究呼吁在教育类AI工具中采取公平性意识的设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型中的性别偏见是否会通过AI辅助写作影响人类作者的文本内容，特别是对学生生涯规划类写作的影响，以揭示偏见传播的风险并推动更公平的AI设计。

Method: 采用控制实验设计，招募123名参与者，在三种条件下撰写针对性别不同但其他信息相同的生物档案的生涯规划论文：无AI协助、中性LLM协助、带有性别偏见的LLM协助。通过分析文本中的主动性程度和职业建议的性别刻板性来评估偏见转移情况。

Result: 在性别偏见的LLM辅助条件下，学生撰写的女性目标作文表现出更大的‘主动性差距’和更多性别刻板的职业建议，且这种影响对女性目标更为显著，表现为主动性被抑制，而男性目标写作基本不受影响，显示出偏见传递的不对称性。

Conclusion: AI辅助写作工具可能将模型中的性别偏见传递给使用者，尤其在涉及性别角色的情境下，导致输出内容进一步强化刻板印象。因此，必须在教育类AI工具的设计中引入公平性考量，防止偏见的隐性传播。

Abstract: Gender bias in LLMs has been studied extensively in model outputs, with biased prompts shown to amplify stereotyped generations. Whether such bias propagates into text produced by humans who use these systems, however, remains underexplored. We investigate whether gender bias in an LLM writing assistant transfers into career plan essays written by students. We first verify that a gender-biased prompt induces gender-differentiated language in LLM-generated essays, while a neutral prompt does not. We then recruited participants (N = 123) in a controlled environment to write career plan essays for paired biographical profiles differing only in gender under three conditions: no AI assistance, neutral LLM assistance, or gender-biased LLM assistance. Students in the biased condition produced essays with a significantly larger agentic gap and more gender-stereotypic occupation suggestions than those in the control and neutral conditions. Our results also reveal that this bias transfer is asymmetric: agency is suppressed in female-target essays while male-target writing remains largely unaffected. Our findings highlight the risk of bias propagation in AI-assisted writing, calling for fairness-aware design in educational AI tools.

TL;DR: 该论文调查了多模态代码智能，涵盖生成、编辑、优化、执行或基于视觉输入输出进行推理的系统。作者通过代码在任务中的角色（如渲染产物、可编辑符号结构、科学表示、中间推理轨迹或可执行策略/工具接口）对领域进行形式化，并将基准和方法组织为四个领域：图形用户界面、科学可视化、结构化图形以及前沿任务与框架。论文指出未来研究应聚焦于以验证为中心的方向，包括多信号验证、多状态验证、跨任务迁移测试和可验证代理轨迹，推动多模态代码生成从单输出模仿向基于证据的可执行系统演进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多真实编程任务依赖于视觉元素（如截图、图表、文档、矢量图、视频和交互状态）来表达意图，而现有大语言模型在处理这类任务时缺乏对视觉信息与代码正确性之间关联的理解，尤其在布局、几何、数据语义、可编辑性、交互行为及领域特定约束方面存在不足。因此需要建立一个系统性的多模态代码智能研究框架。

Method: 提出基于代码在任务中角色的分类体系，构建涵盖四大领域的多模态代码智能研究框架，并引入四种以验证为中心的研究方向作为未来发展方向。

Result: 建立了多模态代码智能的系统性分类与评估框架，揭示了不同任务对正确性证据的不同处理方式，并为未来研究指明了基于验证的演进路径。

Conclusion: 多模态代码生成需从单一输出模仿转向基于多源证据的可执行系统，未来研究应强化验证机制，提升模型行为与视觉输入之间的可信对齐。

Abstract: While LLMs have substantially advanced text-to-code synthesis, many real programming tasks specify intent through visual artifacts such as screenshots, charts, documents, vector drawings, videos, and interactive states. These tasks require models to connect visual perception to executable programs, because correctness depends not only on syntax but also on layout, geometry, data semantics, editability, interaction behavior, and domain-specific constraints that apply after execution. This survey examines Multimodal Code Intelligence, covering systems that generate, edit, refine, execute, or reason with code under visually grounded inputs and outputs. We first formulate the field by the role that code plays in each task, distinguishing code as a rendered artifact, an editable symbolic structure, a scientific representation, an intermediate reasoning trace, or an executable policy or tool interface. We then organize benchmarks and methods into four domains: Graphical User Interface, Scientific Visualization, Structured Graphics, and Frontier Tasks and Frameworks. This taxonomy connects mature artifact-generation problems to emerging agentic and unified settings and allows us to compare how different tasks treat evidence of correctness. Looking ahead, we argue that future research may benefit from four verification-centered directions. Multi-signal validation can combine complementary evidence of correctness, multi-state verification can test behavior across execution trajectories, cross-task transfer testing can probe reusable visual-code skills, and verifiable agent traces can reveal whether agent actions are grounded in visual evidence. Together, these directions may move multimodal code generation from single-output imitation toward evidence-grounded executable systems.

### [160] [FinBalance: A Multi-Document Accounting Reconciliation Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15949)
*Sasank Tumpati,Devansh Agarwal,Ayush Kedia,Arjun Neekhra,Murari Mandal,Krishna Garg,Yash Sinha,Suman Gupta,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FinBalance 是一个基于多文档会计对账的基准测试，涵盖八个行业、三种周期类型和五个难度级别。该基准通过确定性生成器创建真实业务场景、会计政策、税务/外汇处理、文档模式、干扰项和不一致模板，生成带有分录、资产负债表和23种不一致标签的账本。在710条评估数据上，六种主流大模型的最终资产负债表准确率最高仅达46%。四个模型在报告的资产负债表与通过账本重放获得的资产负债表之间存在26-41个百分点的差距，表明其虽能生成数值合理的分录，但无法正确关联支持文档并一致聚合。引用压力提示对文档链接错误改善有限，而账本反馈消融实验显著提升报告资产负债表质量，并揭示了不一致检测中的权衡关系。专家财务评审验证了基准设计与标签的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用确定性生成器构建包含人类编写业务场景、会计政策、税务/外汇处理、文档结构、干扰项及不一致模板的源文档包，自动生成对应的分录、资产负债表及23类不一致标签。通过账本重放机制验证模型输出的准确性，并设计对比实验分析不同提示策略与反馈机制的影响。

Result: 六种主流大模型在最终资产负债表精确度上最高仅为46%；四模型在报告资产负债表与重放后资产负债表间存在26-41个百分点的差距，显示其在文档绑定与一致性聚合方面严重不足。引用压力提示作用有限，而账本反馈显著提升准确性，并暴露出不一致检测中的性能权衡。

Conclusion: FinBalance 有效模拟了真实会计流程中的复杂对账任务，揭示了当前大模型在文档关联与逻辑一致性方面的关键缺陷。该基准可作为评估模型在真实财务语境中推理能力的重要工具，且账本反馈机制对提升模型表现具有重要意义。

Abstract: Existing financial-NLP benchmarks mostly evaluate prepared artifacts such as filings, tables, or extracted values. Real accounting begins earlier: source documents must be reconciled into cited journal entries, aggregated into a balance sheet, and checked for contradictions. We introduce FinBalance, a multi-document accounting reconciliation benchmark built from source-document bundles across eight industries, three period types, and five difficulty levels. Human-authored business scenarios, accounting policies, tax/FX treatments, document schemas, distractors, and inconsistency templates are composed by a deterministic generator whose ledger produces journal entries,balance sheets, and 23 inconsistency-code labels. On a 710-record evaluation split, six contemporary LLMs reach at most 46% exact final-balance-sheet accuracy. Four models show a 26-41 pp gap between BS_exact, the model's reported balance sheet, and BS_recon, the balance sheet obtained by replaying its entries through our ledger. Models often recover numerically plausible entries but fail to bind them to supporting documents and aggregate them consistently. Citation-pressure prompting barely changes document-linking errors, while ledger-feedback ablations substantially improve reported balance sheets and expose inconsistency-detection trade-offs. Expert finance reviewers validate the benchmark design and labels.

### [161] [SAG: SQL-Retrieval Augmented Generation with Query-Time Dynamic Hyperedges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15971)
*Yuchao Wu,Junqin Li,XingCheng Liang,Yongjie Chen,Yinghao Liang,Linyuan Mo,Guanxian Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SAG（SQLRetrieval Augmented Generation）是一种基于SQL查询的动态结构化检索增强生成框架，通过将文本块转换为语义完整的事件和索引实体，利用SQL连接查询在查询时动态构建局部超边，实现高效多跳推理。相比传统知识图谱方法，SAG避免了全局静态图的维护开销，支持增量更新、并发处理与可扩展性，且在多个多跳问答基准测试中表现优异，在MuSiQue上达到80.0% Recall@5，已成功应用于大规模生产环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG方法依赖密集相似度检索，难以处理结构化约束和多跳推理；虽引入知识图谱缓解部分问题，但面临语义碎片化、维护成本高及更新困难等挑战。因此需要一种既能保持结构化优势又具备灵活性与可扩展性的新架构。

Method: SAG将每个文本块转化为一个语义完整事件及其一组索引实体，不预先构建全局知识图谱，而是基于标准数据库系统，在查询时通过SQL JOIN操作动态连接共享实体的事件，形成局部超边结构，构建动态局部索引，从而实现高效、灵活的知识检索与推理。

Result: 在HotpotQA、2WikiMultiHop和MuSiQue三个多跳推理基准上，SAG在9个Recall@K指标中有8个达到最优；尤其在最复杂的MuSiQue上达到80.0% Recall@5；系统已部署于数亿级数据规模，线上检索延迟控制在秒级。

Conclusion: SAG通过动态构建基于SQL的局部索引结构，有效克服了传统RAG与知识图谱方法在多跳推理中的局限，兼具高性能、低维护成本与生产可用性，是面向大规模知识增强生成系统的可行解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) offers an effective approach for large language models to access external knowledge. However, existing methods rely on dense similarity retrieval and face inherent limitations in handling structured constraints and multi-hop reasoning. Incorporating knowledge graphs partially alleviates these issues, but at the cost of semantic fragmentation, high maintenance overhead, and difficult incremental updates. This paper introduces SAG (SQLRetrieval Augmented Generation), a structured architecture for retrieval and agent systems. Instead of pre-building a global static graph, SAG converts each chunk into one semantically complete event and a set of indexing entities, then uses SQL join queries to dynamically link events that share entities into local hyperedges,constructing, at query time, a dynamically instantiated local index structure. This design avoids the need for global graph rebuilding and ongoing maintenance; the system naturally supports incremental writes, concurrent processing, and continuous scaling through its reliance on standard database infrastructure. Across HotpotQA, 2WikiMultiHop, and MuSiQue, three standard multi-hop benchmarks,SAG achieves the best results on 8 out of 9 Recall@K metrics, reaching 80.0% Recall@5 on MuSiQue, the benchmark with the highest multi-hop reasoning demands.SAG has also been deployed at a production scale of hundreds of millions of data items, with online retrieval latency kept within seconds. Project site and code are available at https://github.com/Zleap-AI/SAG-Benchmark.

</details>


### [162] [Formalize Once, Edit the Rest: Efficient Lean-Based Answer Selection for Math Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15972)
*Ji Feng,Zhouxing Shi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: BASE proposes a base-and-edit pipeline to reduce the computational cost of formalizing multiple LLM-generated answers for verification in Lean proof assistants. Instead of independently formalizing each of K candidate answers, BASE formalizes only one 'base' answer and uses a rewriter model (LEANSCRIBE) to generate edit functions that modify the base formalization to produce the remaining K-1 formalizations. This approach achieves higher accuracy and reduces autoformalizer calls by about 5x at K=8, with greater savings as K increases, across 12 benchmark configurations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing methods require independent autoformalization of each candidate answer, leading to high computational cost. The goal is to reduce this cost while maintaining or improving answer selection accuracy.

Method: BASE introduces a base-and-edit framework: first, formalize a single base candidate using an autoformalizer; then, train a rewriter model (LEANSCRIBE) to identify the answer part in the base formalization and generate edit operations to adapt it for other candidates. This enables efficient reuse of formalization effort.

Result: BASE improves both selection accuracy and efficiency—achieving a Pareto improvement across all 12 (dataset, solver) configurations on four benchmarks and three solvers. It reduces autoformalizer calls by ~5x at K=8, with increasing gains as K grows.

Conclusion: The base-and-edit strategy significantly reduces the cost of formalizing multiple LLM-generated answers for Lean-based verification, enabling scalable and accurate answer selection without sacrificing rigor.

Abstract: With large language models (LLMs) increasingly applied to mathematical reasoning, formal proof assistants such as Lean can be leveraged to verify reasoning outputs with machine-checkable rigor, enabling use cases such as answer selection in test-time scaling with K sampled candidate answers. However, employing Lean requires that LLM outputs, originally in natural language, first be formalized. Existing Lean-based answer-selection work uses an autoformalization model to generate a formal statement in Lean for each candidate answer independently, incurring a significant computational cost. We propose BASE, a base-and-edit pipeline that formalizes a single base candidate per problem and derives the remaining K-1 statements by editing the answer expression in place. To facilitate this, we train a rewriter model LEANSCRIBE to localize the answer in the base formalization and generate a reusable edit function for the other K-1 candidates. BASE simultaneously improves selection accuracy and reduces formalization cost - a Pareto improvement that holds on all 12 (dataset, solver) configurations across four benchmarks and three solvers, cutting autoformalizer calls by about 5x at K=8, with the reduction expected to become larger as K grows. Code is available at https://github.com/ucr-rai/base-and-edit.

To ensure reliable assessment, we establish a human-LLM collaborative pipeline for key fact extraction and a multi-LLM consensus verifier for summary fact decomposition. Leveraging this framework, we evaluate 28 LLMs across four distinct categories grouped by reasoning capability and model scale. Our extensive empirical study reveals critical insights regarding the cross-scenario challenges current LLMs continue to face, the impacts of reasoning and scale, and the efficiency and adaptability of reasoning models. ### [165] [GRACE-DS: a Guarded Reward-guided Agent Correction Environment in Data Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16000)
*Aleksandr Tsymbalov,Danis Zaripov,Artem Epifanov,Anastasya Palienko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GRACE-DS 是一个用于评估基于大模型的自动化机器学习（AutoML）代理在数据科学任务中表现的受控环境，通过模拟从规划到代码修复的全流程，评估其性能、可复现性、协议合规性及奖励对齐等关键指标。实验表明，采用灵活迭代交互的结构优于单次生成、非结构化交互和重启基线，且在超过7000次实验中验证了其有效性，为组织级生产条件下的LMM-AutoML代理评估提供了可靠平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法难以全面衡量大模型驱动的AutoML代理在真实工作流中的可靠性与合规性，尤其缺乏对数据泄露、可复现性和流程规范性的有效检测机制，因此亟需一个贴近生产环境的综合评估框架。

Method: 构建一个隔离的评估环境GRACE-DS，包含多阶段工作流模拟（规划、数据检查、特征工程、建模、验证、代码修复与提交），并集成隐藏的可执行验证器，自动检测最终预测性能、数据泄露、可复现性、协议有效性、纠错行为与奖励对齐情况；采用灵活迭代交互策略作为核心评估范式。

Result: 相比单次生成、非结构化交互和重启基线，灵活迭代交互策略在端到端隐测试质量上表现更优，同时显著提升协议合规完成率，在超过7000个实验中验证了其稳定性和有效性。

Conclusion: GRACE-DS是一个强大且可靠的评估平台，能够有效衡量基于大模型的AutoML代理在接近真实生产环境下的综合能力，支持组织根据自身需求定制评估标准，推动其安全部署与持续优化。

Abstract: We introduce GRACE-DS, a Guarded Reward-guided Agent Correction Environment in Data Science for pre-deployment evaluation of LLM-powered AutoML agents. GRACE-DS is a set of evaluation metrics in an isolated environment that can be applied to tabular ML tasks specific to a particular organization. It exposes agents to realistic workflow stages, from planning and data inspection through feature engineering, model development, validation, and code repair to final submission, while hidden executable validators measure not only final predictive performance but also leakage avoidance, reproducibility, protocol validity, correction behavior, and reward alignment. The strongest structured regime, flexible iterative interaction (our approach), achieves higher end-to-end normalized hidden-test quality than single-shot generation, unstructured interaction, and restart-based baselines, while also improving protocol-valid completion. Validated across more than 7,000 episodes, these results establish GRACE-DS as a robust platform for assessing the capacity of LLM-based AutoML agents to execute machine learning workflows under production-like conditions and in accordance with organization-specific requirements.
