### [166] [Bridging the Usability Gap: Lessons from Interpreting Studies for Machine Interpreting Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16009)
*Claudio Fantinuoli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出机器口译（MI）虽在标准基准测试中取得显著进展，接近人类水平的文本保真度，但实际用户体验仍远逊于人工口译，存在“准确性幻觉”——系统看似准确，实则无法支持流畅、目标导向的互动。为此，作者将MI定义为语音翻译的一个独立子领域，强调需以交际有效性而非孤立保真度指标进行评估。基于口译研究，提出三个相互关联的设计优先原则：代理性（情境敏感的主动与修正）、语境化（多模态与话语层面的情境意识）和体验性（通过真实互动实现自适应改进），以弥合可用性差距，推动实现真正实时、自然的多语言交流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器口译系统虽然在文本保真度上接近人类水平，但实际使用中难以支持流畅、目标导向的交互，用户体验远低于人工口译，暴露出‘准确性幻觉’问题。现有评估方法依赖孤立的保真度指标，无法反映真实沟通中的有效性，亟需新的理论框架和评价体系。

Method: 结合口译学研究，分析专业口译实践的关键维度，提炼出适用于机器口译系统设计的核心原则；通过跨学科整合，构建以交际有效性为导向的评估与设计框架。

Result: 提出了机器口译的三大核心设计优先原则：代理性、语境化和体验性，为未来系统开发指明方向，有助于缩小技术性能与实际可用性之间的差距。

Conclusion: 机器口译应被视为一个独立的子领域，其发展需超越传统保真度评价，转向以交际有效性为核心的设计范式。通过落实代理性、语境化和体验性三大原则，可有效提升系统的实时多语言沟通能力，实现真正意义上的实用化。

Abstract: Machine interpreting (MI), the live, real-time branch of speech translation, has achieved remarkable progress on standard benchmarks, with some systems approaching human parity on textual fidelity. Yet the user experience remains far inferior to interpreter-mediated communication, revealing what we term the \emph{accuracy illusion}: systems that appear accurate on paper but fail in practice to support smooth, goal-oriented interaction. This paper defines MI as a distinct subfield of speech translation, with its own characteristics and the need for evaluation methods grounded in communicative effectiveness rather than isolated fidelity metrics. Drawing on insights from interpreting studies, we identify critical dimensions of professional interpreting practice that are overlooked by current systems, and consolidate them into three interdependent design priorities for future MI: \emph{agency} (context-sensitive initiative and repair), \emph{grounding} (multimodal and discourse-level situational awareness), and \emph{experience} (adaptive improvement through real interaction). Together, these priorities chart a path toward closing the usability gap and enabling systems that can sustain authentic multilingual communication in real time.

### [167] [Who Flips? Self- and Cross-Model Counterarguments Reveal Answer Instability in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16011)
*Nafiseh Nikeghbal,Amir Hossein Kargaran,Shaghayegh Kolli,Jana Diesner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种评估大语言模型答案稳定性的新协议，通过向正确回答施加合理但错误的反论来测试模型是否改变答案。实验在7个前沿模型和57个MMLU主题上进行，发现翻转率从17.5%到97.3%不等，表明稳定性差异显著且无法被传统准确率捕捉。自引用会显著提高翻转率（平均+7.1个百分点），跨模型整合错误论证可生成更强对抗性挑战。研究构建了MaxFlip数据集，使翻转率比标准挑战提升最高达+23.6个百分点。相关工具与数据已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准准确率基准无法评估大语言模型在面对合理反论时是否坚持正确答案，因此需要一种能衡量答案稳定性的新评估方法。

Method: 设计了一种受控评估协议：先让模型正确回答多选题，再以逻辑连贯的错误论证挑战其答案，记录模型是否翻转。该设置分离了论证内容与社会压力，并系统变化论证长度、自我归因及来源模型。通过跨模型收集并筛选最强错误论证，构建了MaxFlip挑战集。

Result: 七种前沿模型的翻转率跨度大（17.5%–97.3%），自引用显著增加翻转率（均值+7.1pp，最高+18.7pp）；跨模型错误论证组合比单一模型更有效；MaxFlip挑战集使翻转率较标准挑战提升最高+23.6pp。

Conclusion: 答案稳定性是评估大语言模型的重要维度，应与准确率并列作为基准。本文提出的协议和工具为稳定性评估提供了可复现的框架，有助于揭示模型在面对质疑时的鲁棒性差异。

Abstract: Standard accuracy benchmarks are designed to test how closely large language models (LLMs) approach correct answers, but are not suitable for testing whether LLMs stick with a correct answer when that answer is challenged by a plausible counter-argument. We introduce a controlled protocol for evaluating answer stability: after a model answers a multiple-choice question correctly, we challenge the model's answer with a coherent argument for an incorrect option and measure whether the model flips. The setup a) isolates argumentative content from overt social pressure and b) varies argument length, self-attribution, and cross-model source. Across seven frontier models and 57 MMLU subjects, flip rates range from 17.5% to 97.3%, revealing large differences in stability that are not captured by accuracy metrics alone. We find that self-attribution consistently increases flip rates (mean +7.1pp, up to +18.7pp). Also, pooling wrong-answer arguments across models and selecting the most effective one per question yields stronger adversarial challenges than relying on any single source model. We further construct MaxFlip, a curated challenge set that amplifies flips by up to +23.6pp over standard self-generated challenges. We release the protocol, challenge records, and MaxFlip to support stability evaluation alongside standard accuracy benchmarks. Materials are available at https://github.com/nafisenik/WhoFlips and https://hf.co/datasets/nafisehNik/WhoFlips.

</details>


### [168] [Scaling Human and G2P Supervision for Robust Phonetic Transcription](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16019)
*Alexander Metzger,Aruna Srivastava,Ruslan Mukhamedvaleev*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在英语语音标注中，人工标注与自动图素转音（G2P）模型标注的协同效果。基于一个包含80小时的基准数据集（涵盖母语、非母语及中风后言语），发现当人工标注少于20-30小时时，G2P标注能有效提升性能；超过此阈值后，G2P不再带来显著收益，甚至损害跨方言鲁棒性。在此之后，使用ASR预训练可实现比以往系统2.3倍的加权音素特征错误率降低，尤其在非母语和失语症语音上表现优异。结果表明，单纯依赖数量驱动的G2P扩展对泛化能力的提升有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 专家语音标注成本高昂，尤其是在非标准方言和异常语音情况下。为降低成本，常采用图素转音（G2P）模型自动生成语音标签，但其在不同监督水平下的有效性尚不明确。本文旨在探究人工与G2P标注在不同规模下的协同效应及其对模型鲁棒性的影响。

Method: 在80小时的多类型语音数据集（包括母语、非母语及中风后言语）上，系统评估不同规模的人工标注与G2P标注组合的效果，并引入ASR预训练策略以进一步优化性能。通过对比不同配置下的音素错误率，分析监督质量与数量对模型泛化能力的影响。

Result: 当人工标注低于20-30小时时，G2P标注能有效提升性能；超过该阈值后，其贡献不再显著，甚至削弱跨方言鲁棒性。采用ASR预训练后，加权音素特征错误率降低2.3倍，且在非母语和失语症语音上取得显著改进。

Conclusion: 单纯依赖大量G2P标注进行模型扩展难以持续提升泛化能力，反而可能损害模型鲁棒性。相比之下，结合高质量的ASR预训练可更有效地提升系统性能，尤其在复杂语音场景下。

Abstract: Expert phonetic annotation is costly, especially for non-standard dialects and atypical speech. A common alternative is using Grapheme-to-Phoneme (G2P) models to auto-generate phonetic labels from text transcripts at scale. We study how automatic phonetic transcription performance scales with human and G2P supervision in English. Using a curated 80-hour benchmark spanning native, non-native and post-stroke speech, we identify a supervision quality threshold: G2P supervision helps only when fewer than 20-30 hours of human annotation are available. Beyond this threshold, it provides no significant benefit and can reduce cross-dialect robustness. What is effective after this threshold is ASR pretraining which we use to achieve a 2.3x reduction in weighted phone feature error rate over prior systems, with strong gains on non-native and aphasic speech. These results suggest that quantity-driven G2P scaling may yield diminishing returns for robust generalization.

Our contribution is a reproducible recipe for training a supervised classifier from routinely collected cancer registry data. It describes how to build the in-domain training set and a production-matched holdout, and to choose operating points that keep the false-negative rate (FNR) very low while keeping reviewer workload manageable. The pipeline standardizes data curation with facility-stratified sampling and separate handling of reports linked to registry cases, and includes a blinded manual audit to estimate positive-case prevalence and label noise. On a 418k-report holdout set, the Kentucky model achieved FNR 0.003 and false-positive rate (FPR) 0.097, improving over the Seattle-trained MOSSAIC OncoID baseline (FNR 0.010, FPR 0.183) and raising F1 from 0.860 to 0.922. *Jakub Bąba,Jarosław A. Chudziak*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将ARIC任务重构为智能体之间的辩论，采用主张者-反对者-裁判的多智能体架构，并引入信心门控机制，仅对置信度低的预测进行辩论，高置信度结果直接采纳。

However, standard training-free models often miss sophisticated details, specifically in contexts where two parts of the text have to be analyzed together. Furthermore, self-correction mechanisms tend to reinforce initial hallucinations in reasoning. Overcoming these limitations typically requires expensive, domain-specific supervised fine-tuning. Recent work has shown that a multi-agent paradigm can address such weaknesses for the component classification task through dialectical refinement with a Proponent-Opponent-Judge architecture, setting a promising direction for training-free approaches in the field. In this paper, we extend and evaluate this framework on the Argument Relation Identification and Classification (ARIC) task, reformulating it as a debate over component pairs. Besides that, we introduce a confidence gating mechanism that enables debating only on the uncertain cases and accepting the initial prediction when confidence is high. On the UKP Argument Annotated Essays v2 corpus, we demonstrate that the selective debate achieves the highest Macro F1 among all training-free methods, while debate over all samples degrades performance below that of one of the baselines. All generative approaches also outperform fine-tuned RoBERTa models on Macro F1, suggesting that the under-representation of the Attack class was more damaging to supervised fine-tuning than to inference-only models. Additionally, our framework produces human-readable debate transcripts, offering interpretability absent from both single-agent and supervised classifiers.

  Results: We present PVminerLLM2, an improved set of LLMs for structured patient voice extraction that applies preference optimization to address token-critical errors beyond the reach of supervised fine-tuning. Our method introduces (i) a preference objective with token-level gated stabilization term that prevents degradation of absolute token likelihood under preference optimization, and (ii) confusion-aware preference pair construction to better capture low-separation distinctions. Motivation: 解决Transformer自注意力机制在长序列上计算复杂度高（O(N^2)）与状态空间模型（SSM）虽线性扩展但存在选择性回忆瓶颈之间的根本权衡问题。

Method: 设计并行混合架构（PHA），让GSS、GQA和FFN以并行方式运行，各自专注于不同任务：GSS捕获全局上下文，GQA执行选择性检索，FFN提供补充处理，三者通过可学习的混合机制融合输出。

Result: 在WikiText-103上，125M参数模型达到16.51 PPL，优于Hedgehog（16.70）和H3-125M（23.70）；180M参数模型达16.42 PPL，性能接近纯注意力基线，同时实现24%更高吞吐量和最高40%内存降低。在OpenWebText上，125M模型达19.72 PPL，优于标准Transformer（20.60）和GSS基线（19.80）。

Conclusion: 将序列建模范式分离为并行专业化分支，是实现高困惑度性能与高效长上下文建模相结合的有效路径。

Abstract: Modeling long-range dependencies remains a central challenge in natural language processing. Transformer architectures achieve strong performance via self-attention but scale quadratically ($O(N^2)$) with sequence length, while State Space Models (SSMs) scale linearly ($O(N)$) but suffer from a selective recall bottleneck, struggling to retrieve precise information from compressed states. This creates a fundamental tradeoff between efficiency and perplexity. To tackle these challenges, we propose the \textit{Parallel Hybrid Architecture (PHA)}, which runs Gated State Spaces (GSS), Grouped Query Attention (GQA), and Feed-Forward Networks (FFNs) as independent parallel branches fused by a learnable mixing mechanism. Instead of forcing SSMs to approximate attention or serializing the two paradigms, PHA allows each branch to specialize: GSS captures global context, while attention performs selective retrieval, with FFN providing complementary processing. On WikiText-103, PHA achieves 16.51 PPL at 125M parameters, outperforming Hedgehog (16.70) and H3-125M (23.70). Scaling to 180M parameters yields 16.42 PPL, which gives comparable results with the pure attention baseline while delivering 24\% higher throughput and up to 40\% lower memory usage at long contexts. On OpenWebText, our 125M model achieves 19.72 PPL, outperforming standard Transformers (20.60) and GSS hybrid baselines (19.80). These results demonstrate that separating sequence modeling paradigms into parallel specialists enables Transformer-level perplexity with substantially improved efficiency for long-context language modeling.

</details>


### [173] [Towards Pareto-Optimal Tool-Integrated Agents with Pareto Ranking Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16111)
*Junyi Li,Xiaowei Qian,Yingyi Zhang,Wenlin Zhang,Guojing Li,Sheng Zhang,Xiao Han,Yichao Wang,Xiangyu Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ParetoPO提出一种两阶段多目标优化框架，用于对使用工具的大语言模型进行对齐，在多个竞争目标之间实现更优的准确率与效率权衡。第一阶段采用基于超体积引导的动态标量法调整奖励权重；第二阶段通过帕累托排序计算优势，实现非支配轨迹的优先优化。实验表明，该方法在数学推理和多跳问答任务中显著优于静态和启发式基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐方法主要关注任务准确性，忽视了工具使用效率等辅助目标，影响实际部署效果。因此需要一种能同时优化多个冲突目标的方法。

Method: 提出两阶段多目标优化框架ParetoPO：第一阶段使用超体积引导的动态标量法自适应调整奖励权重；第二阶段采用帕累托排序的优势计算，实现基于支配关系的信用分配。

Result: 在数学推理和多跳问答任务上，ParetoPO consistently 发现了在准确率与效率之间具有更优权衡的策略，优于静态和启发式基线方法。

Conclusion: ParetoPO能够有效实现多目标优化，提升工具使用型大模型在复杂任务中的综合性能，为实际应用提供更优解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in tool-integrated language agents have significantly improved their ability to solve complex reasoning tasks. However, existing alignment methods predominantly focus on maximizing task accuracy, while overlooking auxiliary objectives such as tool-use efficiency, which are essential for practical deployment. To address this gap, we introduce ParetoPO, a two-stage multi-objective optimization framework for aligning tool-using large language models (LLMs) under competing objectives. In the first stage, ParetoPO leverages hypervolume-guided dynamic scalarization to adapt reward weights based on global Pareto frontier progress. In the second stage, it replaces scalarized learning signals with Pareto-ranking-based advantage computation, promoting nondominated trajectories through dominance-aware credit assignment. This design enables fine-grained, action-level optimization across multiple conflicting objectives. Experimental results on mathematic reasoning and multi-hop QA tasks show that ParetoPO consistently discovers policies with superior accuracy-efficiency trade-offs compared to static and heuristic baselines.

*Andreas Einwiller,Max Klabunde,Florian Lemmerich*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AuAu 是一个全面的基准测试，用于评估大语言模型（LLM）生成具有威权倾向回应的风险。该基准结合了三种评估方法：心理测量问题、情境行为案例和真实用户提示。它不仅评估总体威权主义倾向，还考察威权攻击性、威权顺从性和传统主义三个子概念。在来自中国、欧盟、俄罗斯和美国的17个模型上进行测试，发现所有模型在心理测量评估中均表现出显著的威权回应率，但在更真实的下游任务中该比例显著下降。此外，威权系统提示可轻易使15个模型中的15个表现出更强的威权倾向。研究强调需要持续系统地审计基于LLM的AI系统，以检测并减轻生成内容中的非期望威权倾向。代码与数据已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The worldwide surge of authoritarianism, combined with the increasing central role in users' everyday lives, raises the question of to what extent specific models exhibit or promote authoritarian attitudes and characteristics. This benchmark combines three evaluation approaches: (i) psychometric questions from an extensive pool of 15 human validated instruments; (ii) contextual behavior vignettes probing intended actions in concrete situations; and (iii) responses to realistic user prompts. Unlike prior work, AuAu evaluates not only a general closeness towards authoritarianism but also the established sub-concepts Authoritarian Aggression, Authoritarian Submission, and Conventionalism. Evaluating 17 models from China, the EU, Russia, and the USA, we find that all tested models exhibit substantial authoritarian response rates under the psychometric evaluation, though rates drop significantly in increasingly more realistic downstream task. We further find that an authoritarian system prompt easily manipulates 15 out of 17 models to promote increased authoritarianism. Our results underscore the need for continued, systematic auditing of LLM-based AI systems to detect and ultimately mitigate undesired authoritarian tendencies in generated output. Our code and data are available at: https://github.com/andreaseinwiller/AuAu

Meanwhile, large language model (LLM)-based explanation generation often produces generic and ungrounded descriptions due to the lack of heuristic evidence and task-specific supervision, stemming from limited grounded explanation datasets for SDD. We therefore propose a training-free explanation framework that integrates XAI evidence with multimodal LLMs to generate grounded and specific explanations. ### [176] [GRACE: Step-Level Benchmark for Faithful Reasoning over Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16151)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建一个包含10个模型在4个数据集上生成的推理链的基准数据集，采用人工标注方式对每一步进行忠实度、错误类别和自然语言解释标注；通过无监督聚类发现数据驱动的错误分类体系，将失败归为两大类：推理错误（GRACE-Inference）和事实依据错误（GRACE-Grounding），每类下设四种子类。

Result: 实验显示当前模型在步骤级忠实度上表现不佳，存在显著提升空间；将步骤级忠实度信号融入强化学习后，下游任务准确率与推理可靠性均得到改善。

Conclusion: GRACE 为评估和改进大模型在复杂推理任务中的忠实度提供了有力工具，推动更可靠、可解释的人工智能推理系统发展。

Abstract: Many reasoning tasks require models to reason over input context, from document-grounded question answering to rule-based deduction. Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting produces traces that appear transparent, yet individual steps can silently deviate from the source evidence, even when the final answer is correct. Existing methods detect hallucinations at the response level but fail to identify where in the chain a failure occurs or what type it is. We introduce GRACE, the first human-annotated step-level faithfulness benchmark with a data-driven error taxonomy for context-grounded textual reasoning. GRACE covers CoT traces from 10 models across 4 source datasets, with each step annotated for faithfulness, error category, and natural language explanation. A data-driven taxonomy, discovered bottom-up via unsupervised clustering, organizes failures into two tracks: GRACE-Inference (deductive errors) and GRACE-Grounding (factual grounding errors), with four categories each. The evaluation set is human-annotated and challenging by design. Our experiments reveal substantial headroom for current models. In addition, integrating step-level faithfulness signals into reinforcement learning pipelines improves both downstream accuracy and reasoning reliability.

### [178] [PACT: Privileged Trace Co-Training for Multi-Turn Tool-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16215)
*Zhenbang Du,Jun Luo,Zhiwei Zheng,Xiangchi Yuan,Kejing Xia,Dachuan Shi,Qirui Jin,Qijia He,Shaofeng Zou,Yingbin Liang,Wenke Lee*

TL;DR: PACT提出了一种特权轨迹协同训练框架，用于多轮工具使用智能体的后训练。该方法在推理时保持仅基于提示的生成方式，而利用专家轨迹作为训练阶段的优化信号，通过两种互补信号：基于轨迹的强化学习代理评估提示生成的轨迹，并引入组件感知的监督微调损失来指导推理前缀和工具调用。同时，通过提示仅锚定机制减少对训练轨迹上下文的依赖。实验表明，PACT在FTRL、BFCL和ToolHop任务上均优于强基线模型，验证了特权轨迹协同训练的有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮工具使用智能体的后训练面临奖励稀疏和信用分配困难的问题，而使用专家轨迹进行监督微调虽提供密集过程监督但易导致模型过度约束于固定轨迹。因此需要一种既能利用专家知识又不破坏推理灵活性的方法。

Method: 提出PACT框架，采用仅提示推理（prompt-only inference）策略，结合专家轨迹作为训练优化信号，包含两个核心组件：（1）基于轨迹条件的强化学习代理，用于评估提示生成轨迹在专家轨迹上下文下的表现；（2）组件感知的监督微调损失，以渐进式强度监督推理前缀与工具调用。引入提示仅锚定机制降低对训练轨迹的依赖，并提供潜在轨迹视角解释双目标协同机制。

Result: 在FTRL、BFCL和ToolHop三个基准任务上，PACT显著优于基于SFT和RL的强基线模型，证明其在提升多轮工具使用能力方面的有效性。

Conclusion: PACT通过将专家轨迹作为训练期优化信号而非推理期引导，实现了对多轮工具使用智能体的有效后训练，既保留了推理的灵活性，又充分利用了专家知识，为复杂任务中的智能体学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Multi-turn tool-use agents must reason, call tools, and adapt to observations across several interaction turns. Post-training such agents is challenging, as reinforcement learning often suffers from sparse rewards and weak credit assignment despite matching the prompt-only inference setting, while supervised fine-tuning on expert traces provides dense process supervision but can over-constrain the model to fixed trajectories. To tackle this, we propose PACT, a Privileged trAce Co-Training framework for multi-turn tool-use agents. The key idea is to use expert traces only as training-time optimization signals rather than rollout-time hints. PACT keeps rollout generation prompt-only, then uses expert traces to guide optimization through two complementary signals: a trace-conditioned RL surrogate that evaluates prompt-only rollouts under expert-trace context, and a component-aware SFT loss that supervises reasoning prefixes and tool-calls with annealed strength. To reduce over-reliance on the training-only trace context, PACT further introduces a prompt-only anchoring. We also provide a latent-trace view that connects the two trace-based objectives and explains how expert traces can guide optimization without being used during rollout generation. Experiments on FTRL, BFCL, and ToolHop show that PACT consistently improves over strong SFT- and RL-based baselines, highlighting the value of privileged trace co-training for multi-turn tool-use learning.

### [179] [Creative Collision: Directorial Persona Steering and Competition in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16240)
*Subramanyam Sahoo,Justin Shenk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了在大型语言模型推理时通过叠加两个语义对立的引导向量（即“创意碰撞”）来控制模型行为的新范式。以斯皮尔伯格（乐观、救赎性道德观）和马丁·斯科塞斯（黑暗、道德模糊）为例，构建导演人格向量，并通过混合参数α和引导系数λ进行插值。实验发现：(i) 斯皮尔伯格的语义主导性强，在大部分插值范围内压制了斯科塞斯的影响；(ii) 中间碰撞点反而在高λ下提升了生成连贯性；(iii) 两个角色的特征均集中在40层解码器的第28层，揭示出共享的“道德基调底座”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激活引导方法多仅注入单一语义方向，难以实现复杂、动态的风格与价值控制。本文旨在探索双语义方向叠加的潜力，以更精细地操控模型生成内容的道德倾向与创作风格，推动可控创造性生成与价值对齐叙事合成的发展。

Method: 基于精选剧本语料库，采用均值-差异激活对比法构建斯皮尔伯格与斯科塞斯的导演人格向量；通过可调混合参数α和引导系数λ在残差流中叠加这两个向量，系统评估不同组合下的生成效果。

Result: (i) 斯皮尔伯格向量表现出显著的方向主导性，几乎在整个插值区间内压制斯科塞斯的道德影响；(ii) 在高引导强度下，中间混合状态反而带来更高的生成连贯性；(iii) 两个向量的影响力峰值均集中于40层解码器的第28层，表明存在一个共同的道德语义子空间。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了变换器残差流中竞争性语义方向的几何结构，展示了双方向叠加在可控创作生成中的潜力，为实现更具表现力与价值对齐的文本生成提供了新思路。

Abstract: Activation steering has emerged as a powerful tool for shaping the behaviour of large language models at inference time, yet most prior work injects a \emph{single} semantic direction into the residual stream. We study the richer setting in which two semantically opposing steering vectors are superimposed -- a regime we call \textbf{Creative Collision}. Concretely, we construct directorial persona vectors for Steven Spielberg (optimistic, redemptive moral valence) and Martin Scorsese (dark, morally ambiguous) via mean-difference activation contrast on curated screenplay-derived corpora, then interpolate between them with a scalar mixing parameter $α\in [0,1]$ and a steering coefficient $λ$. Across five evaluation axes -- moral valence, generation coherence, surface style, directional dominance, and vector geometry -- three principal findings emerge: (i)~Spielberg's representational signature exhibits robust \emph{directional dominance}, suppressing Scorsese's moral influence across almost the entire interpolation range; (ii)~intermediate collision points paradoxically \emph{improve} generation coherence relative to pure single-director steering at high $λ$; and (iii)~both personas localise maximally to layer~28 of a 40-layer decoder-only transformer, revealing a shared \emph{moral-tone substrate}. These results illuminate the geometry of competing semantic directions in transformer residual streams and have direct implications for controllable creative generation and value-aligned narrative synthesis.

</details>


### [180] [Who Should Lead Decoding Now? Tracking Reliable Trajectories for Ensembling Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16281)
*Heecheol Yun,Joonhyung Park,Joowon Kim,Eunho Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TIE是一种基于轨迹的迭代集成框架，用于融合掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）的知识。它通过追踪答案相关位置的置信度动态，识别可靠的解码轨迹，并在不同模型间选择性地传递部分去噪序列，从而利用各模型在生成过程不同阶段的互补优势，显著提升多任务推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）能力与知识覆盖范围日益多样化，如何有效整合这些模型的知识成为一个关键问题。现有方法缺乏对MDLM独特解码动态的理解，导致知识融合效率低下。因此，亟需一种能够捕捉并利用可靠生成轨迹的集成策略。

Method: 提出TIE（Trajectory-based Iterative Ensembling）框架，通过分析MDLMs在生成过程中的置信度动态，识别高可靠性解码路径；在不同模型间迭代传递部分去噪序列，允许不同模型在生成的不同阶段贡献其优势，实现知识互补与协同优化。

Result: TIE在多种推理任务中均表现出色，验证了其有效性；实验分析表明，该方法能有效识别并利用可靠的生成轨迹，提升生成质量与稳定性，为MDLM集成提供了新范式。

Conclusion: TIE通过基于置信度动态的轨迹跟踪与选择性信息传递，实现了多模型间的高效知识融合，为解决掩码扩散语言模型集成这一未充分探索的问题提供了一个实用且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Masked Diffusion Language Models (MDLMs) have emerged as a distinct paradigm for sequence generation. As MDLMs become diverse in capabilities and knowledge coverage, an important question is how to combine their knowledge. Toward this, we first investigate the unique decoding dynamics of MDLMs. We find that successful generations exhibit stable confidence dynamics over answer-relevant positions, while unreliable trajectories can often be corrected by injecting promising intermediate states from other models. Guided by this observation, we propose $\textbf{TIE}$ ($\textbf{T}$rajectory-based $\textbf{I}$terative $\textbf{E}$nsembling), a knowledge fusion framework in which MDLMs iteratively identify reliable decoding trajectories and relay them across models. TIE tracks confidence dynamics over answer-relevant positions to determine which model currently follows a more reliable trajectory and selectively transfers partially denoised sequences across models. As the model on the more promising trajectory often changes across denoising steps, TIE allows different models to contribute complementary strengths at different stages of generation. Strong performance across diverse reasoning tasks, along with our analyses, suggests that TIE offers a practical approach to the underexplored problem of MDLM ensembling.

### [181] [HiMPO: Hindsight-Informed Memory Policy Optimization for Less-Entangled Credit in Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16285)
*Jiangze Yan,Yi Shen,Wenjing Zhang,Jieyun Huang,Zhaoxiang Liu,Ning Wang,Kai Wang,Shiguo Lian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HiMPO是一种用于长时程智能体的记忆策略优化框架，通过事后信息减少记忆写入动作的信用混淆问题。它通过比较写入前后的记忆在相同状态下的任务相关信息恢复能力来估计局部效用，并利用事后相关性作为有界回溯过滤器，抑制因下游错误导致的不准确信用分配。该方法仅对记忆项使用特定优势，而轨迹级奖励仍优化其他行为，在开放域任务和压缩记忆问答中优于现有基线，同时保持上下文压缩效率。受控实验表明其能有效减少工具错误带来的责任误判，提升记忆更新的归因准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时程智能体依赖记忆机制压缩交互历史，但记忆写入的信用分配面临挑战：记忆更新可能因下游工具失败、观测噪声或推理错误被错误奖励或惩罚，导致有用证据被丢弃或无关信息被保留。这种因果纠缠的信用分配会影响记忆质量与决策有效性。

Method: HiMPO首先在相同预写状态下评估记忆更新的局部效用，即比较更新前后可恢复的任务相关信息；随后引入事后相关性作为有界回溯过滤器，若局部效用未被目标结果支持，则减弱记忆信用；最终将记忆特定优势仅用于优化记忆项，而整体轨迹奖励仍用于优化其余行为。

Result: 在基于裁判的开放域任务和压缩记忆问答任务中，HiMPO显著优于强记忆基线和强化学习基线，同时保持高效的上下文压缩能力。控制干预实验显示，其有效降低由工具错误引发的责任泄漏，提升记忆更新的归因精确性。

Conclusion: HiMPO通过分离记忆写入的信用信号，缓解了长时程智能体中记忆更新的因果纠缠问题，提升了记忆质量与系统鲁棒性，为高效、可解释的记忆机制设计提供了新路径。

Abstract: Long-horizon agents rely on memory mechanisms to compress interaction history, but optimizing memory writing faces a distinct credit assignment challenge: a memory update may be rewarded or penalized due to downstream tool failures, noisy observations, or reasoning errors rather than its own contribution. This causally entangled credit can lead agents to discard useful evidence or preserve irrelevant information. We propose HiMPO, a Hindsight-Informed Memory Policy Optimization framework for assigning less-entangled credit to memory-writing actions in long-horizon agents. HiMPO first estimates the local utility of a memory update by comparing the task-relevant information recoverable from the previous and updated memories under the same pre-write state. It then uses hindsight relevance as a bounded retrospective filter that attenuates memory credit when local utility is not supported by the target outcome. The resulting memory-specific advantage is applied only to memory tokens, while trajectory-level rewards optimize the rest of the agent behavior. Across judge-based open-domain tasks and objective compressive-memory QA, HiMPO improves over strong memory-based and RL-based baselines while preserving compressed-context efficiency. Controlled interventions further show that HiMPO reduces blame leakage from tool-induced errors and improves attribution fidelity of memory updates.

</details>


### [182] [PaperJury: Due-Process Review for Bounded LaTeX Revision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16322)
*Yiran Wang,Ruixuan An,Biao Wu,Wenhao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PaperJury 是一个闭环的审稿-裁决-修订-验证系统，通过确定性与语义分离的设计，实现对人类撰写的计算机科学论文的预提交加固。它解决了现有写作助手在跨轮次问题追踪、批判到裁决的确定性路由以及稿件控制方面的不足，引入了基于可争议性的路由、程序正义审判和风险比例保护链，支持无效丢弃、可修复有效和作者需介入三种终局结果。在视觉、自然语言处理和机器学习领域的双臂专家评估中，其在问题质量、裁决与路由准确性、编辑安全性、收敛性和成本方面优于四个基线，证明负载关键的安全性和完成逻辑应由确定性编排而非模型自主决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有写作辅助工具缺乏跨轮次持久的问题标识、从批评到裁决的确定性路由，以及能拒绝无效关切或推迟作者依赖型问题的稿件控制能力，无法满足预提交加固对对抗性全篇审查、明确不可修复结果和受控修订的需求。

Method: PaperJury 采用确定性与语义分离架构：确定性编排负责分解、冻结论点主干、持久化日志、路由、终止判断和精确一次的补丁应用；语义代理仅限于有限范围的评审、判断和修复。系统结合有限的整体评审、基于可争议性的路由、程序正义的审判机制及风险比例保护链，确保锚定边界内的安全编辑。

Result: 在包含视觉、自然语言处理和机器学习论文的双臂专家评估中，PaperJury 在问题质量、裁决与路由准确率、编辑安全性、收敛速度和成本控制方面均优于四个基线系统，验证了将负载关键的安全与完成逻辑置于确定性编排中的有效性。

Conclusion: 负载关键的安全性和完成逻辑应由确定性编排而非模型自主决策来保障，PaperJury 的设计为此提供了实证支持，并已开源（https://github.com/u7079256/paperjury）。

Abstract: Pre-submission hardening of human-authored LaTeX computer science papers differs from drafting assistance because it requires adversarial whole-paper review, explicit no-fix outcomes, and bounded artifact-safe revision. Existing writing assistants, critique generators, and judge-centered loops lack durable issue identity across rounds, deterministic routing from critique to adjudication, and manuscript control that can reject invalid concerns or defer author-dependent ones. We present PaperJury, a closed-loop review-verdict-revise-verify system built on a deterministic-versus-semantic split: deterministic orchestration manages decomposition, a frozen claim spine, a durable ledger, routing, stopping, and exact-once patch application, while semantic agents are limited to bounded review, judgment, and repair. PaperJury combines bounded holistic review, contestability-based routing, a due-process trial, and risk-proportional guard chains for anchor-bounded edits, yielding terminal outcomes of invalid-drop, valid-fixable, and author-required. In a two-arm expert-review evaluation on held-out Vision, natural language processing, and machine learning papers against four baselines, we assess issue quality, verdict and routing quality, edit safety, convergence behavior, and cost, supporting the thesis that load-bearing safety and completion logic should reside in deterministic orchestration rather than model discretion. PaperJury is available at https://github.com/u7079256/paperjury.

</details>

### [184] [Tyler: Typed Latent Reasoning for Language Models -- When to Think, What to Compute, and How Much to Allocate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16360)
*Hanyu Lin,Min Cai,Jiawei Wen,Haodi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Tyler 是一种有类型且预算感知的潜在推理框架，通过在自回归解码过程中动态决定何时调用潜在计算、执行何种计算以及分配多少资源，解决了现有方法中预定义触发和分配策略的问题。该方法在多个大型语言模型上实现了最高达14.49个百分点的准确率提升，显著优于传统的链式思维（CoT）和当前最强基线，并具备良好的跨领域泛化能力与低遗忘特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有潜在推理方法通常预先设定何时调用潜在计算及如何分配资源，缺乏对推理时机、计算类型和预算分配的动态决策能力，限制了其性能和灵活性。

Method: Tyler 提出一种基于策略的学习机制，在每个解码步骤中选择生成文本标记或切换到特定推理功能的潜在计算模块；一旦激活，操作符将当前推理状态映射为支持全局规划、局部状态更新或可重用过程抽象的潜在标记。

Result: 在三种骨干 LLM 上的广泛实验表明，Tyler 相比 CoT 最多提升 14.49 个百分点准确率，相比最强基线最多提升 4.30 个百分点；同时在多样推理任务中表现出优异泛化能力，最终阶段性能最佳且遗忘最少。

Conclusion: Tyler 通过动态、类型化和预算感知的方式实现高效潜在推理，显著提升了大模型的推理能力，为未来智能系统中的复杂推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting improves reasoning in large language models (LLMs) by externalizing intermediate computation as discrete text tokens, but this textual interface also introduces redundancy and inference overhead. Latent reasoning offers a promising alternative by carrying part of the computation in continuous representations. However, existing methods typically predefine when latent computation is invoked and how it is allocated during decoding, leaving a key problem unresolved: when to invoke latent computation, what type of computation to perform, and how much budget to allocate. We propose \textbf{Ty}ped \textbf{L}at\textbf{e}nt \textbf{R}easoning (Tyler), a typed and budget-aware framework for latent reasoning during autoregressive decoding. Tyler learns a policy that, at each decoding step, chooses between emitting a text token and switching to a latent computation module specialized for a particular reasoning function. Once invoked, an operator maps the current reasoning state into latent tokens that support global planning, local state updates, or reusable procedural abstraction. Across extensive experiments on three backbone LLMs, Tyler improves accuracy by up to 14.49 points over CoT and by up to 4.30 points over the strongest competing baseline. It further generalizes across diverse reasoning domains and achieves the best final-stage performance with the lowest forgetting.

</details>

### [185] [QPILOTS: Efficient Test-Time Q-Steering for Flow Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14801)
*Yifan Ruan,Chenyang Cao,Andreas Burger,Ali Pesaranghader,Kaveh Kamali,Jaehong Kim,Nandita Vijaykumar,Alan Aspuru-Guzik,Igor Gilitschenski,Nicholas Rhinehart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QPILOTS 是一种无需修改原始策略的新型方法，通过在推理时引导去噪过程来解决流匹配和扩散策略在时间差分强化学习中优化困难的问题。它避免了直接对多步去噪过程反向传播不稳定的梯度，而是将中间噪声动作投影到最终清洁动作估计上计算批评者梯度。提出两种变体：QPILOTS-U 使用快速单点近似，QPILOTS-M 通过学习的辅助网络生成可微后验样本。在标准离线到在线强化学习基准上，QPILOTS 达到 90% 的平均成功率；应用于预训练视觉-语言-动作基础模型时，在六项模拟操作任务中表现优于或匹配现有推理时方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在优化流匹配和扩散策略时面临数值不稳定性问题，尤其是在利用批评者动作梯度进行有效策略提取方面。直接反向传播梯度通过多步去噪过程会导致不稳定，而现有解决方案如丢弃梯度信息、简化策略或反复微调策略均存在局限性。因此需要一种新方法，在不改变原策略的前提下，稳定且高效地利用批评者信号。

Method: QPILOTS 在推理阶段通过投影中间噪声动作至最终清洁动作估计来计算批评者梯度，从而绕过不可靠的中间状态评价。其两个变体分别为：QPILOTS-U 使用单点近似快速估算；QPILOTS-M 利用学习的辅助网络生成可微后验样本，实现更精确的梯度估计。整个过程保持原始策略不变，仅在推理时施加引导。

Result: 在标准离线到在线强化学习基准上，QPILOTS 实现了 90% 的平均成功率，优于现有方法。在六项模拟操作任务中，应用于大型冻结预训练视觉-语言-动作（VLA）基础模型时，性能超越或匹配所有先前的推理时方法。

Conclusion: QPILOTS 提供了一种高效、稳定且无需修改原始策略的方案，能够有效利用批评者梯度指导扩散型策略的推理过程，显著提升性能，适用于复杂任务与大规模预训练模型的部署场景。

Abstract: Flow-matching and diffusion policies are expressive action generators, but optimizing them with temporal-difference reinforcement learning (RL) remains difficult. Effective policy extraction requires exploiting the critic's action gradient, yet directly backpropagating this signal through a multi-step denoising process can be numerically unstable. Existing methods work around this either by discarding gradient information, distilling the policy into a simpler one-step actor, or repeatedly fine-tuning the denoising policy as the critic improves. We propose QPILOTS, a method that leaves the original policy unmodified and steers the denoising process at inference time. At each denoising step, instead of evaluating the critic on the noisy intermediate action where critic predictions are unreliable, we first project that intermediate state to an estimate of the final clean action and compute the critic gradient there. We introduce two variants: QPILOTS-U uses a fast single-point approximation, while QPILOTS-M draws differentiable posterior samples via a learned auxiliary network. On a standard offline-to-online RL benchmark, QPILOTS achieves the best aggregate performance, reaching an average success rate of 90% across 50 tasks. We also apply QPILOTS to steer a large, frozen, pretrained Vision-Language Action (VLA) foundation model, outperforming or matching prior inference-time approaches across six manipulation tasks in simulation.

</details>


### [186] [GRAPE: Guided Parameter-Space Evolution for Compact Adversarial Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14865)
*Zhiyuan Ye,Xiangyu Zhou,Ji Qi,Hao Zhang,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRAPE提出了一种渐进式参数空间演化框架，通过逐步释放可优化维度并利用对抗谱利用率引导新容量至高压力模块，在保持计算预算相近的前提下，显著提升了模型的对抗鲁棒性。在CIFAR-10上，相比固定结构的AT方法，其PGD-20鲁棒准确率从51.70%提升至56.94%，同时减少了约21.4%的参数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对抗训练方法通常从一开始就使用固定的参数空间进行训练，忽略了参数可优化顺序对最终鲁棒性的影响。本文旨在探究参数空间逐步暴露的过程是否能影响最终的鲁棒模型性能。

Method: GRAPE结合了参数空间稳定与渐进式隐藏层扩展：先在当前可优化空间中稳定鲁棒优化，再逐步释放新的可优化维度，并使用对抗谱利用率分数指导新增容量向高压力模块集中。

Result: 在标准ℓ∞威胁模型下，使用ResNet-18架构的GRAPE在几乎相同的计算开销（FLOPs比为1.009）下，将PGD-20鲁棒准确率从51.70%提升至56.94%，且参数量减少约21.4%；序列增长变体也达到56.52%的准确率，证明提升不仅源于最终架构差异，更与参数空间暴露路径有关。

Conclusion: 引导式的参数空间演化能够实现紧凑且鲁棒的参数配置，在控制计算成本的前提下有效提升模型对抗鲁棒性，表明训练过程中的参数暴露路径对最终性能具有重要影响。

Abstract: Adversarial Training (AT) improves neural network robustness, but most methods train a fixed parameter space from the start. This paper asks whether the order in which parameters become optimizable can affect the final robust solution, even when the final architecture or computation budget is controlled.
  We propose GRAPE, Guided Parameter-Space Evolution, a training framework for compact adversarial robustness. GRAPE combines parameter-space stabilization with progressive hidden expansion: it stabilizes robust optimization in the currently exposed space, gradually releases new optimizable dimensions, and uses an adversarial spectral utilization score to guide newly released capacity toward high-pressure modules. In contrast to fixed-structure AT, GRAPE treats robust model learning as a process of progressive parameter-space exposure and evolution.
  Under the standard $\ell_\infty$ threat model on CIFAR-10, with fixed-structure ResNet-18 AT as a controlled reference, GRAPE improves PGD-20 robust accuracy from 51.70% to 56.94% at a nearly matched computation budget with a FLOPs ratio of 1.009x, while reducing parameter count by about 21.4%. A sequential grow variant with the same final ResNet-18 architecture reaches 56.52% PGD-20 robust accuracy, indicating that the gain is not only due to final architecture differences but also to the parameter-space exposure path. These results suggest that guided parameter-space evolution can yield compact and robust parameter configurations under matched computation.

*Tianhe Zhang,Xiguang Liu,Peng Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出α-FISP框架，通过约束优化平衡精算公平与团结公平，参数α调节公平权衡，确保偿付能力，并在数值实验中验证其计算可行性及与美国各州监管要求的契合性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 保险定价面临精算公平与团结公平之间的张力，尤其在数据精细化和监管压力下，需一种能明确权衡两者并保证偿付能力的定价框架。

Method: 将保险定价建模为带预算约束的优化问题，通过调整精算保费以控制各风险组内的交叉补贴，形成由参数α参数化的公平连续体。

Result: 理论证明了框架的可行性；数值实验表明该方法计算高效，且与美国各州不同公平要求的监管环境相匹配。

Abstract: Fairness in insurance pricing remains a long-standing and deeply debated puzzle. On one hand, insurers, driven by profitability considerations, set premiums that differentiate across individual risks to achieve actuarial fairness. On the other hand, insurance serves a critical societal function by pooling risks across a population, motivating cross-subsidization among groups to promote solidarity fairness. The tension between these two competing notions of fairness makes insurance pricing inherently complex, particularly in modern settings where granular data allow for increasingly fine risk differentiation and regulators face growing pressure to protect vulnerable groups. To address this challenge, we propose an $α$-\textbf{F}air \textbf{I}ndividual \textbf{S}olvent \textbf{P}remium ($α$-FISP) framework for insurance pricing that explicitly captures the trade-off between actuarial and solidarity fairness while guaranteeing solvency, a fundamental requirement in insurance operations. We formulate the pricing problem as a constrained optimization task, where actuarially fair premiums are adjusted subject to budget constraints on cross-subsidization within each risk class. This formulation naturally yields a family of solutions parameterized by $α$, tracing a continuum between purely actuarial and purely solidarity-based pricing and enabling decision-makers to select an operating point along this fairness spectrum. We derive theoretical guarantees for the proposed framework. Numerical experiments show that $α$-FISP is computationally tractable and aligns well with the U.S. regulatory regimes featuring heterogeneous state-level fairness requirements.

### [188] [GRASP: Gradient-Aligned Sequential Parameter Transfer for Memory-Efficient Multi-Source Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14900)
*Mary Isabelle Wisell,Nicholas Jacobs,Aayush Manandhar,Salimeh Yasaei Sekeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRASP提出一种梯度对齐的顺序参数迁移方法，实现多源迁移学习中知识的有效融合，同时保持O(1)内存消耗。通过逐个源模型处理、参数级梯度对齐和迭代微调，避免负迁移并支持无限数量源模型的扩展。在多个持续学习基准上，GRASP达到93.5%平均准确率，远超集成方法的71.7%，且内存不随源模型数量增加而增长，适用于资源受限环境与动态演化数据域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多源迁移学习方法在参数融合时需同时加载所有源模型，导致内存开销为O(K)，或在推理时部署全部模型，难以实现生产级部署。因此亟需一种低内存、可扩展的多源知识整合方法。

Method: GRASP采用顺序处理策略，逐个将源模型知识融入目标模型；通过参数级梯度对齐机制，仅转移优化方向一致的参数以避免负迁移；结合迭代微调，在引入下一源前优化已迁移知识，提升融合质量。

Result: 在Yearbook、CLEAR-10和CLEAR-100三个持续学习基准上，GRASP在不同架构（1.3M~25.6M参数）下均取得93.5%的平均准确率，显著优于集成方法的71.7%；同时内存消耗恒定，不随源数量增长，具备良好可扩展性。

Conclusion: GRASP通过梯度对齐的顺序参数迁移，实现了高效、低内存、可扩展的多源知识融合，特别适合资源受限场景和持续演化的源域环境。

Abstract: Multi-source transfer learning faces a fundamental scalability bottleneck: existing approaches require either loading all K source models into memory simultaneously during parameter fusion, requiring O(K) memory, or deploying all models at inference time, making production deployment infeasible. We propose GRASP (Gradient-Aligned Sequential Parameter Transfer), which achieves superior knowledge integration while maintaining O(1) memory consumption through three key innovations: (1) sequential processing that merges one source at a time into an evolving target model, (2) parameter-wise gradient alignment that selectively transfers only parameters whose optimization directions align with the target domain, avoiding negative transfer, and (3) iterative fine-tuning that adapts transferred knowledge before integrating the next source. Extensive experiments across three continual learning benchmarks (Yearbook, CLEAR-10, CLEAR-100) spanning 10 to 108-year temporal distribution shifts and four architectures (1.3M to 25.6M parameters) demonstrate that GRASP achieves 93.5% mean accuracy over all datasets and architectures compared to ensemble method's 71.7% accuracy while requiring only constant memory versus K models for standard multi-source fusion. Critically, GRASP's sequential previously merged models and scales to arbitrarily many sources without memory growth, making it uniquely suitable for resource-constrained deployment and continually evolving source domains.

### [189] [Policy Regret for Embedding Model Routing: Contextual Bandits with Low-Rank Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14929)
*Yan Dai,Negin Golrezaei,Patrick Jaillet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了推荐系统中动态路由查询到多个嵌入模型的挑战，提出将该问题形式化为带有低秩专家的对抗性上下文线性带宽问题。针对标准遗憾度量存在的结构性误设或统计不可行性，提出一种名为Hypentropy Policy Gradient（HPG）的策略梯度算法，能有效适应未知的低秩结构，并在不完全信息下实现$\tilde{\mathcal O}(s\sqrt{M T})$的线性化策略遗憾，避免维度灾难。同时提供了一种计算高效且无需调参的HPG实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推荐系统依赖动态路由查询至多个嵌入模型，但该问题在对抗性查询、带宽反馈和模型可观测性受限等现实条件下缺乏深入理解，亟需建立更稳健的理论框架与学习算法。

Method: 将嵌入模型路由建模为对抗性上下文线性带宽问题，引入对数-二次策略类以平衡表达能力与学习效率；设计并分析了Hypentropy Policy Gradient（HPG）算法，其可自适应未知低秩结构，并在不完全信息下实现最优遗憾界。

Result: HPG算法实现了$\tilde{\mathcal O}(s\sqrt{M T})$的线性化策略遗憾，显著优于传统方法，且避免了维度灾难；同时具备计算高效性和无需调参的实用性。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论建模与算法设计，为动态嵌入模型路由提供了高效、鲁棒的解决方案，推动了推荐系统在复杂现实场景下的可扩展性与可靠性。

Abstract: Modern recommendation systems increasingly rely on dynamically routing diverse queries to multiple embedding models. Despite its practical significance, this problem remains poorly understood under realistic conditions like adversarial queries, bandit feedback, and limited observability of models. We formalize embedding model routing as an adversarial contextual linear bandit with low-rank experts, where contexts are queries, actions are items, and experts are the embedding models working on low-rank latent representation spaces. We first establish that standard regret notions suffer from structural misspecification or statistical intractability, and we identify a log-quadratic policy class that is expressive enough to capture query-dependent model routing, yet structured enough to allow efficient online learning. Second, we propose a policy gradient algorithm called Hypentropy Policy Gradient (HPG). It provably adapts to the unknown low-rank structure under incomplete information and attains $\tilde{\mathcal O}(s\sqrt{M T})$ linearized policy regret -- where $s, M$, and $T$ are the intrinsic rank of the experts, the number of models, and the number of rounds -- thus avoiding a curse of dimensionality. Finally, we also provide an computationally efficient and parameter-free implementation of HPG.

### [190] [Separable Neural Architectures as Physical World Models: from Mathematical Theory to Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14934)
*Reza T Batley,Andrew Kichline,Sourav Saha*

Method: 提出可分离神经架构（SNA），将局部坐标函数（原子）与全局稀疏低秩交互对象分离；在变分框架下构建VSNA，利用张量分解实现因子化表示；采用张量原生交替最小二乘法（ALS）进行优化，实现线性于维度的计算复杂度。

Result: VSNA在各类偏微分方程中表现出良好的数值稳定性与收敛性，成功实现7维参数化制造模拟与真实材料反演；在标准笔记本上完成百万次查询仅耗时102秒，相较全网格有限元方法提速15万倍；支持实时生成式逆向重建（<100ms），显著提升工程仿真效率与可交互性。

Conclusion: SNA作为具有理论保障的紧凑数学结构，能够有效应对高维参数化偏微分方程挑战，为物理世界建模提供‘一次求解，任意查询’的能力，适用于实时反演、优化与不确定性量化，是未来智能仿真系统的重要候选架构。

Abstract: This work introduces the Separable Neural Architecture (SNA), a function representational class combining neural approximation with tensor decomposition. The SNA decouples localized coordinate functions (atoms) from global interactions governed by a sparse, low-rank interaction object. This architecture possesses a compact and smooth inductive bias well-suited for solving partial differential equations (PDEs). When viewed as a Galerkin trial space under the variational SNA (VSNA) framework, the formulation satisfies classical variational guarantees under Lax-Milgram: well-posedness, quasi-optimality, convergence, and stability. In high-dimensional spatiotemporal--parametric PDEs, the VSNA mitigates the curse of dimensionality by scaling algebraically rather than exponentially. Exploiting an entirely factorized, tensor-native alternating least squares (ALS) optimization framework reduces this cost to linear in dimension. The VSNA is validated across elliptic, hyperbolic, and parabolic systems, demonstrating close alignment with predicted algebraic and spectral scaling rates. We showcase the SNA as a "solve once, query anywhere" physical world model via two engineering case studies: a 7D parametric manufacturing simulation and an experimental thermal-to-property inversion pipeline for Inconel 718. The VSNA executes a 1,000,000-query Monte Carlo sweep in 102s on a standard laptop CPU, yielding a 150,000x speedup over a full-grid finite element baseline hosted on an NVIDIA A100 GPU. It further enables real-time generative inverse-mode reconstructions under 100ms. These results demonstrate that the SNA serves as a compact mathematical substrate for continuous parameter manifolds to enable real-time inversion, optimization loops, and rapid uncertainty propagation.

### [191] [Remember, Don't Re-read: Stateful ReAct Agents for Token-Efficient Autonomous Experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14945)
*Faramarz Jabbarvaziri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种有状态的ReAct代理框架，通过LangGraph实现持久化状态，显著降低自研究（autoresearch）模式中的令牌消耗。与无状态设计相比，该方法在超参数调优和代码性能优化任务中分别减少90%和52%的令牌使用量，同时保持相近的优化效果。核心优势在于将每轮迭代的上下文读取成本从O(n)降至O(1)，避免重复读取历史记录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自研究模式采用无状态设计，每次迭代需从头重建实验上下文，导致每次迭代产生O(n)的令牌开销，整体复杂度达O(n²)，限制了其在长序列任务中的效率。为解决这一问题，需要一种能持续保留实验历史并高效复用信息的机制。

Method: 将自研究模式重构为基于LangGraph的有状态ReAct代理，利用类型化的持久化状态存储实验历史，并通过工具调用接口在各迭代间传递信息；在固定大小的对话窗口内运行，实现每轮操作的常数时间复杂度。

Result: 在超参数调优任务中，令牌消耗从24,465降至2,492（减少90%）；在代码性能优化任务中，从1,275K降至627K（减少52%），且优化质量相当。证明了该方法在降低计算开销方面的结构性优势。

Conclusion: 有状态的自研究代理通过持久化实验历史和固定窗口交互，有效解决了无状态模式下重复读取历史带来的高成本问题，是一种可落地、高效且易于实现的改进方案，适用于各类自动化实验场景。

Abstract: The autoresearch pattern enables autonomous experimentation by having a large language model (LLM) iteratively modify code to optimize a target metric. Its stateless design, however, reconstructs experimental context from scratch at every iteration, incurring $O(n)$ token cost per iteration and $O(n^{2})$ total. This work reformulates the pattern as a stateful ReAct agent using LangGraph, where typed persistent state carries experimental history across iterations via a tool-calling interface. Two benchmarks are evaluated: hyperparameter tuning (15 iterations, small per-iteration observations) and code performance optimization (40 iterations, large per-iteration observations containing full source code and benchmark results). On hyperparameter tuning, the stateful agent consumes 90\% fewer tokens (2{,}492 vs.\ 24{,}465). On code optimization, the stateful agent consumes 52\% fewer tokens (627K vs.\ 1{,}275K) while achieving comparable optimization quality on both tasks. The token reduction is structural: the stateless agent re-reads the full history at $O(n)$ cost per iteration, while the stateful agent operates within a fixed-size conversation window at $O(1)$ cost. This paper describes the architecture in sufficient detail for practitioners to implement a stateful autoresearch agent for their own workflows.

Result: 深度学习模型普遍能更好捕捉生理数据中的复杂关系，但随机森林在部分情况下表现更优，兼具高效性和可解释性；Transformer在处理数值数据方面表现出良好适应性，性能接近LSTM和GRU模型。

Conclusion: 应根据具体目标选择合适的模型，综合考虑精度、效率与可解释性。生理数据在理解学生压力源和提升学业表现方面具有重要潜力，未来可进一步探索其在教育心理支持中的应用。

Abstract: This study investigates the application of machine learning models to predict exam outcomes using physiological data collected during examination sessions. Physiological stress indicators, including electrodermal activity, heart rate, and skin temperature, were analyzed to uncover their association with academic performance. A variety of machine learning approaches were employed, ranging from standard models like logistic regression, random forest, and support vector machines to more advanced architectures, including transformers, long short-term memory (LSTM), and gated recurrent unit (GRU) models. This diversity aimed to capture the complex interactions within the data effectively. A key focus was assessing the adaptability of transformers in processing numerical data and evaluating their performance in this novel context. Standard performance metrics, such as accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score, were used to compare model efficacy. The experimental results demonstrate that while deep learning models generally excel at capturing complex relationships in physiological data, simpler models like random forests can sometimes achieve superior performance while offering computational efficiency and interpretability. Furthermore, transformers demonstrated notable versatility, showcasing performances comparable to those of the LSTM and GRU models. This research underscores the importance of experimenting with a broad class of models that align with the objectives of the problem at hand, balancing precision, efficiency, and interpretability. By elucidating the relationships between physiological signals and academic performance, this study contributes to understanding stressors affecting students' mental health. It further promotes leveraging physiological data to enhance student well-being and academic outcomes.

### [194] [Benchmarking Instance-Dependent Label Noise with Controlled Corruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14965)
*Shadman Islam,Agustinus Kristiadi,Mostafa Milani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CILN框架，通过可控输入扰动生成显式且可调节的实例依赖标签噪声（IDN）基准数据集，相比传统基于标注者错误的方法，能更真实地模拟标签不确定性。在CIFAR10、MNIST和Adult上构建90种不同扰动类型与强度的基准设置，实验表明其噪声结构更贴近人类不确定性的分布，并揭示了现有方法（如Co-Teaching、DivideMix）在特定噪声结构下的失效模式，强调噪声结构对算法表现的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CILN框架，通过引入多种可控输入扰动（如图像失真、属性篡改等），构造被污染的样本；利用多样化的投票池对这些样本进行标注，从而生成具有明确来源和可调严重度的实例依赖噪声数据集。

Result: 构建了90个基准设置，涵盖多种扰动类型与强度；生成的数据表现出真实的实例依赖噪声特性，具备多样化的混淆结构；在CIFAR-10上生成的标签分布比已有合成基准更接近人类不确定性；揭示了主流方法在特定噪声结构下的失败模式，说明噪声结构影响算法性能。

Conclusion: 噪声结构在决定基准难度和算法行为中起关键作用，不应仅关注噪声率。CILN提供了一种可解释、可控制的新型基准生成方式，有助于深入理解噪声标签学习中的挑战与算法鲁棒性。

Abstract: Synthetic instance-dependent label noise (IDN) benchmarks are widely used to evaluate noisy-label learning methods, yet existing approaches typically generate noise through imperfect annotators or classifier raters, leaving the source of ambiguity implicit. We introduce CILN, a benchmark generation framework that creates IDN through controlled input corruptions. A diverse voter pool labels corrupted instances, producing benchmark datasets in which both the source and severity of ambiguity are explicit and controllable. Using CIFAR10, MNIST, and Adult, we construct 90 benchmark settings spanning multiple corruption families and severity levels. Our experiments show that the resulting benchmarks exhibit genuine instance-dependent noise, provide diverse confusion structures, and, on CIFAR-10, can produce label distributions that are closer to human uncertainty than an existing synthetic IDN benchmark. We further demonstrate that corruption-mediated IDN can expose failure modes of popular noisy-label learning methods, including Co-Teaching and DivideMix, that are not observed under comparable levels of rater-fallibility noise. These findings suggest that noise structure, not only noise rate, plays an important role in benchmark difficulty and algorithm behavior. By making ambiguity generation explicit and controllable, CILN provides a complementary benchmarking framework for studying noisy-label learning under diverse sources of instance difficulty.

### [195] [Zero-order Parameter-free Optimization for LMO-based Methods: Novel Approach for Efficient Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14970)
*Dmitriy Bystrov,Daniil Medyakov,Dmitry Bylinkin,Aleksandr Beznosikov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为AdaNAGED的新方法，结合了无梯度训练、自适应参数调整和非欧几里得更新几何，用于大规模大语言模型微调。该方法通过参数自由（PF）适应与基于线性最小化预言机（LMO）的零阶（ZO）优化相结合，解决了传统方法对步长和平滑参数敏感的问题，并在OPT-1.3B模型上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型微调方法面临反向传播带来的巨大内存开销，而零阶优化虽内存高效但对超参数敏感，需大量调参；同时，现有方法缺乏对参数块异质结构的几何感知能力。因此需要一种无需调参、能自适应调整且具备几何感知能力的优化方法。

Method: 提出AdaNAGED方法，融合参数自由自适应机制与基于线性最小化预言机（LMO）的零阶优化，实现无需手动调参的梯度自由训练，并利用非欧几里得更新几何捕捉参数块的异质结构。

Conclusion: AdaNAGED成功实现了无梯度、自适应、几何感知的高效微调，为大规模语言模型的低内存优化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) has become a central application of modern optimization, enabling pretrained models to adapt to diverse downstream tasks and domain-specific data. A major obstacle in large-scale fine-tuning is the memory overhead of backpropagation, which requires storing activations, gradients, and optimizer states. Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization offers a memory-efficient alternative, but its performance is highly sensitive to the stepsize and smoothing parameter, often requiring costly task-specific tuning. Parameter-free (PF) optimization addresses this issue by adapting algorithmic parameters without prior knowledge of problem-dependent constants. Moreover, large-scale fine-tuning can benefit from geometry-aware updates that account for the heterogeneous structure of parameter blocks, which can be modeled through methods that exploit linear minimization oracle (LMO). In this work, we study PF adaptation for LMO-based ZO optimization and introduce $\texttt{AdaNAGED}$, a method that unifies gradient-free training, adaptive tuning, and non-Euclidean update geometry. We establish convergence guarantees and validate the method on large-scale LLM fine-tuning task with $\texttt{OPT}-1.3\mathrm{B}$ model.

### [196] [FastMix: Fast Data Mixture Optimization via Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14971)
*Haoru Tan,Sitong Wu,Yanfeng Chen,Jun Xia,Ruobing Xie,Bin Xia,Xingwu Sun,Xiaojuan Qi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FASTMIX 是一种自动化数据混合发现的框架，通过训练单一代理模型实现高效优化。它将数据混合选择重新表述为双层优化问题，并通过梯度方法联合优化混合系数与模型参数，显著降低搜索成本并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大规模模型依赖于多样化的数据集，但如何确定预训练和后训练中的最优数据混合比例仍是一个开放难题。传统方法依赖启发式规则或资源密集型模拟，效率低下且难以扩展。

Method: FASTMIX 将混合系数优化转化为一个双层优化问题，证明了在均匀采样下，混合比例优化等价于对每类数据源分配损失权重。通过交替执行内循环（基于当前混合比例更新模型参数）和外循环（根据验证反馈更新混合比例），实现梯度驱动的联合优化。

Result: FASTMIX 在预训练和后训练任务中均优于现有基线方法，同时大幅降低了数据混合搜索的成本，具备更高的效率和可扩展性。

Conclusion: FASTMIX 提供了一种高效、可扩展的数据混合自动发现方案，通过统一优化模型与数据混合比例，显著提升了大规模模型训练的性能与资源利用效率。

Abstract: While large and diverse datasets have driven recent advances in large models, identifying the optimal data mixture for pre-training and post-training remains a significant open problem. We address this challenge with FASTMIX, a novel framework that automates data mixture discovery while training only a single proxy model. Instead of relying on predefined heuristics or resource-intensive simulations, FASTMIX jointly optimizes mixture coefficients and model parameters, substantially improving efficiency and scalability over prior approaches. At the core of FASTMIX is a reformulation of mixture selection as a bilevel optimization problem. Under this reformulation, we show that optimizing mixture ratios is mathematically equivalent to assigning per-source loss weights under uniform source sampling. This embeds the mixture coefficients directly into the differentiable iterative optimization objective, enabling efficient, gradient-based optimization of both mixture and model. To solve the optimization problem, FASTMIX implements an approximate iterative optimization procedure, alternating between (i) updating model parameters on data sampled according to current mixture ratios (inner loop) and (ii) updating mixture ratios based on validation feedback (outer loop). Across pre- and post-training, FASTMIX outperforms baselines while drastically reducing search cost. Code (https://github.com/hrtan/fastmix)

### [197] [Rational Sparse Autoencoder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14990)
*Naiyu Yin,Yue Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Rational Sparse Autoencoder (RSAE)，用可训练的有理函数替代传统SAE中固定的非线性激活（如ReLU、JumpReLU、TopK），以更灵活地适应预激活几何结构，同时保持对稀疏性的良好建模。通过两阶段流程：先基于合成数据用松弛的Remez交换法初始化有理系数并校准尺度参数，再进行微调。在三个开源语言模型的残差流激活上测试，RSAE在重建精度和下游行为指标上均优于现有方法，且不损失特征可解释性，仅增加少量参数，单个消费级GPU几分钟内完成训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SAE家族受限于固定非线性激活（如ReLU、TopK等），这些硬编码的稀疏机制可能扭曲重建与稀疏性之间的权衡。需要更灵活的激活形式来更好地适应数据内在结构，同时保持稀疏性和可解释性。

Method: 采用可训练的有理函数作为新的编码器激活，设计两阶段训练流程：第一阶段利用合成数据通过松弛Remez交换算法获得初始有理系数，并结合预训练权重和尺度参数校准；第二阶段在标准稀疏正则化重建目标下进行微调。

Result: 在三个开放权重语言模型的残差流激活上，RSAE在所有基线激活类型和不同稀疏度设置下，均显著提升重建性能和下游任务表现，且未牺牲稀疏探针下的特征可解释性。模型升级仅引入少量额外参数，训练速度快，可在单个消费级GPU上快速完成。

Conclusion: RSAE通过引入可训练的有理激活，实现了比传统SAE更优的重建与稀疏性平衡，在保持可解释性的同时显著提升了性能，是一种高效且通用的改进方案。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are standard tools for mechanistic interpretability, but current SAE families are constrained by fixed encoder nonlinearities such as ReLU, JumpReLU, and TopK. This hard-codes a particular sparsity mechanism into the model and can distort the reconstruction-versus-sparsity trade-off. We introduce the Rational Sparse Autoencoder (RSAE), which replaces the fixed encoder activation with a trainable rational function. Rational activations are flexible enough to uniformly approximate the activation primitives used by existing SAE families on compact domains (for TopK, the thresholded gate obtained after a separating top-k threshold is supplied), while also providing a richer function class for adapting to the observed pre-activation geometry. We realise this idea through a two-stage pipeline: an initialisation procedure that copies the pre-trained baseline SAE weights, plugs in rational coefficients obtained by the relaxed Remez exchange on synthetic data, and calibrates the scale parameters along with the rational coefficients; followed by a fine-tuning step under the standard sparsity-regularised reconstruction objective. Empirically, on residual-stream activations of three open-weight language models and across all three baseline activation families, the RSAE strictly improves on it after the fine-tuning step, both on reconstruction-side metrics and on downstream-behaviour metrics, without sacrificing feature-level interpretability under sparse probing. These gains are consistent across host language models, across baseline activation families, and across the full range of baseline sparsity we tested, while the upgrade itself adds only a handful of scalar parameters per autoencoder and runs in minutes on a single consumer GPU.

### [199] [How Should World Models Be Evaluated? A Decision-Making-Centric Position](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15032)

TL;DR: 本文系统梳理了世界模型在现代AI中的多重含义与评估标准的多样性，指出当前研究中存在主张与证据不匹配的问题。文章提出应以决策为中心的评估框架，强调模型在干预、规划和策略优化中的实际效用，而非仅关注视频生成的视觉真实性。为此构建了从L0到L7的评估阶梯，区分不同层次的验证目标，并提出包含反事实动作保真度、闭环滚动有效性、奖励预测等在内的关键评估指标。

Abstract: World models have rapidly become one of the central abstractions in modern AI. Yet the term now refers to several different objects: action-conditioned environment models, latent imagination models, future-video predictors, interactive neural simulators, latent predictive representations, and synthetic-data engines. Evaluation has broadened with the term. Recent papers measure video realism, perceptual similarity, instruction following, physical plausibility, policy ranking, executability, planning success, and downstream policy improvement. The result is not only metric diversity but also a recurring problem of claim/evidence mismatch: papers frequently make a stronger claim about what their model is useful for than their evaluation can actually establish.
  This paper surveys the recent literature and argues that the central question is use-dependent. When a model is presented as a world model for embodied decision-making, a more decisive issue is not whether it generates visually compelling videos, but whether it supports reliable counterfactual reasoning, policy evaluation, planning, and policy optimization under intervention, policy-induced distribution shift, and long-horizon rollout. We organize the literature using an L0--L7 ladder that ranges from visual plausibility to policy optimization utility. In our interpretation, L0--L3 are most naturally read as diagnostics of generated artifacts, L4 is often the first genuinely interventional test, and L5--L7 provide the most direct evidence of decision usefulness. Based on this diagnosis, we propose a decision-making-centric evaluation framework and a benchmark protocol that foreground counterfactual action fidelity, closed-loop rollout validity, reward/value prediction, policy-ranking agreement, optimization lift, model exploitability, and uncertainty calibration.

Motivation: 探索深度学习模型能否从椭圆曲线的弗罗贝尼乌斯迹数据中自动发现解析数论中的已知结果，并理解其内部工作机制。

Result: 模型在测试集上达到>99%准确率，且对无同构或二次扭转变换的曲线表现稳定；发现一个由20个神经元构成的稀疏电路，能以AUROC 0.992实现高精度预测；顶层神经元的输入权重与梅斯特雷-纳加奥求和启发式高度吻合；所有模型在函数空间中高度一致，但读出路径存在缺陷。

Conclusion: 该模型成功从数据中学习到解析数论中的重要结果，展示了深度学习在数论问题上的潜力，同时揭示了模型内部机制的可解释性特征与潜在缺陷。

Abstract: We train a two-layer transformer encoder to classify rational elliptic curves $E/\mathbb{Q}$ of conductor $\leq 10000$ as either rank 0 or rank 1 from the first 128 normalized Frobenius traces. We achieve >99% accuracy on both classes, and accuracy is essentially unchanged on test curves with no isogeny or quadratic-twist relative in the training set. We then apply techniques from mechanistic interpretability such as attention analysis, linear probing, activation patching, logit attribution, and neuron-level circuit analysis to reverse-engineer the algorithm the (centroid in function space) model learned. We find that a sparse circuit of 20 out of 512 layer-1 MLP neurons is sufficient for rank prediction under a linear probe with an AUROC of 0.992 at plateau, implementing a push-pull detector architecture of rank-0 and rank-1 detectors with a one-sided readout. However, we notice that the model has sub-optimal readout problems indicating a mismatch in rank-order between the readout pathway and the discriminative circuit. Critically, the learned input weights of the top discriminating neuron match the Mestre-Nagao sum heuristic weights $\log(p)/(p\cdot \log{B})$ with a Spearman coefficient $r = 0.997$ and Pearson coefficient $r = 0.952$: the model has learnt a result from analytic number theory from the Frobenius trace data alone. We additionally find that all 50 independently trained models concentrate CLS attention on prime positions at 2-50$\times$ the rate of composite positions. The CLS embedding encodes $\log{L(E,1)}$ with $R^2 = 0.962\pm 0.011$ across the 50 models (after controlling for the conductor). Activation patching analysis reveals that attention weights are dissociated from causal information flow. Additionally, the 50 solutions from training are near-identical in function space (with pairwise agreement $>$98.8%) despite large weight space barriers.

</details>


### [201] [Temporal Difference Learning for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15048)
*Qizhen Ying,Yangchen Pan,Victor Adrian Prisacariu,Junfeng Wen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种时间差分（TD）目标，通过惩罚去噪路径上多步进展的一致性来改进扩散模型的性能，尤其在少步采样时效果显著，适用于离散和连续时间扩散模型，并通过重加权方法稳定训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型通常在单个时间步或相邻对上进行局部去噪训练，缺乏跨时间步的一致性，导致性能下降，尤其是在少步采样时。为解决此问题，引入一种能强制跨时间一致性的新目标。

Method: 将扩散过程建模为马尔可夫奖励过程，将去噪视为强化学习中的策略评估问题，推导出统一的TD方法；设计基于样本的重加权机制以稳定训练。

Result: 实验表明，使用TD训练可显著提升生成样本质量（以FID衡量），尤其在采样步数较少时优势更明显，适用于低计算预算场景。

Conclusion: TD方法是一种通用且可直接插入的改进方案，能够增强跨时间一致性，提升多种扩散生成模型的生成质量。

Abstract: Diffusion models are typically trained with objectives that focus on local denoising targets at individual time steps (or adjacent pairs), which do not enforce consistency between predictions along the denoising trajectory. This lack of cross-time consistency can degrade performance, especially for few-step samplers. We introduce a temporal difference (TD) objective that penalizes inconsistency of the model's multi-step progress along the denoising path. By reformulating the diffusion process as a Markov reward process and casting denoising as a policy evaluation problem in reinforcement learning, we derive a unified TD approach that applies to both discrete- and continuous-time diffusion formulations. We further propose a principled sample-based reweighting method that stabilizes training. Empirically, we show that using our TD training can significantly improve sample quality measured by FID, with stronger advantages when the number of sampling steps is small, highlighting its practical utility under low-computation-budget scenarios. We provide ablation studies to justify our design choices, including pairwise loss reweighting, regularization weight, and one-step stride. Overall, our TD approach can be a general drop-in that enforces cross-time consistency and improves generation quality across different diffusion generative models.

### [202] [Physics-conforming Latent Twins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15053)
*Matthias Chung,Yutong Bu,Deepanshu Verma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Physics-conforming Latent Twins框架，通过在潜在空间中约束动力学以满足物理规律（如守恒律、不变量、耗散结构），实现对复杂时变系统的高精度、物理解释性强的代理模型。方法结合编码器、解码器与潜在流映射，并通过结构传递视角确保潜空间约束与原始空间物理结构一致，理论证明了结构保持性边界，数值实验显示其在长期行为和结构保真度上显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统代理模型虽能快速预测，但难以保证时间依赖系统中的物理一致性，如守恒律、不变量等，导致长期模拟失真。因此需要一种能够显式集成物理原理的代理建模方法。

Method: 基于潜双生（Latent Twin）框架，联合学习编码器、解码器和潜在流映射；通过在潜空间施加结构约束（如保持或耗散特定量），使潜在动力学自动满足预设的物理原则。引入约束转移视角，建立原始空间与潜空间之间的物理结构对应关系，并推导出保持线性和二次不变量、或强制耗散不等式的代数条件。

Result: 在典型常微分方程和偏微分方程基准测试中，该方法显著提升了约束满足度、结构保真度和长期模拟的定性行为，同时保持了高精度的预测能力。

Conclusion: Physics-conforming Latent Twins成功实现了物理原理驱动的潜空间动态建模，为科学机器学习中的可靠代理模型提供了新范式，尤其适用于需长期稳定性和物理正确性的复杂系统模拟。

Abstract: Surrogate models are central to scientific machine learning, where they enable fast prediction, simulation, inference, and control for complex physical systems. For time-dependent problems, however, accurate interpolation of training trajectories is not sufficient: reliable surrogates should also respect the conservation laws, invariants, admissibility conditions, and dissipative structures that give those trajectories physical meaning. We introduce Physics-conforming Latent Twins, a framework for learning latent surrogate solution operators whose dynamics satisfy selected physical principles by design. The method builds on the Latent Twin formulation by jointly learning an encoder, a decoder, and a latent flow map between arbitrary time-indexed states, while constraining the latent dynamics to preserve or dissipate prescribed structural quantities. We develop a constraint-transfer viewpoint that connects physical structure in the original state space with compatible constraints in latent space, and prove structure-preservation bounds showing how latent enforcement improves control of physical defects after decoding. We also derive algebraic conditions for latent flow maps that preserve linear and quadratic invariants or enforce dissipative inequalities. Numerical experiments on representative ODE and PDE benchmarks demonstrate improved constraint satisfaction, structural fidelity, and qualitative long-time behavior while maintaining accurate surrogate prediction.

### [203] [Size Doesn't Matter: Cosine-Scored Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15054)
*Silen Naihin,Lev Stambler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出使用余弦相似性与输入幅度的可学习混合替代稀疏自编码器（SAEs）中的内积得分，以解决高范数令牌过度占据字典槽的问题。新方法让每个特征独立决定对幅度的依赖程度，训练中从未选择超过一半的幅度依赖。在重建性能相当的情况下，余弦编码器能更频繁地学习到与人类可识别概念对齐的特征，且避免了内积导致的范数探测浪费。尽管优势不适用于所有任务和深度，但作者认为在归一化表示上的字典学习应默认采用余弦评分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准稀疏自编码器（SAEs）使用内积作为激活得分，导致特征激活同时受方向对齐和输入范数影响。在批量顶部K（BatchTopK）机制下，高范数的输入会无差别地放大所有预激活值，从而占据字典槽位，而这些槽位实际上并未反映有意义的内容对齐。由于子层归一化已丢弃输入幅度信息，模型无法读取这一量，因此这种机制引入了无关的信号。

Method: 提出一种新的得分函数，为每个特征引入一个可学习的加权组合，融合余弦相似性和输入幅度，使每个特征能够自主决定其对输入范数的依赖程度。训练过程中，优化器始终未选择超过一半的幅度依赖，表明模型偏好基于方向而非大小的判别。

Result: 在匹配的重建性能下，采用余弦相似性得分的编码器学习到的特征更常与人类可识别的概念对齐，有效利用字典槽，避免了传统内积方法因范数敏感而导致的无效特征占用。即使通过损失重加权来平衡梯度，差距依然显著，说明前向传播得分几何结构是关键因素。

Conclusion: 虽然该方法的优势并非在所有任务和网络深度上都成立，但在归一化表示的字典学习中，余弦评分应作为默认策略，以提升特征语义相关性和效率。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) detect features via inner product, so a feature's activation scales with both its directional alignment and the input's norm. Under BatchTopK, high-norm tokens inflate all pre-activations simultaneously, claiming dictionary slots regardless of content alignment. This matters because sublayer normalization has already discarded the magnitude the score measures, so the encoder detects a quantity the model does not read. We replace the score with a learned blend of cosine similarity and input magnitude, letting the optimizer choose how much norm to use; a per-feature extension lets each feature decide independently. In both regimes, training is free to recover inner product but never does, with no feature ever choosing more than half-magnitude dependence. At matched reconstruction, the cosine encoder learns features that align with human-recognizable concepts far more often than standard, filling dictionary slots that inner product wastes on norm detectors. Loss reweighting that equalizes gradients barely closes the gap, confirming forward-pass score geometry as the lever. The advantage is not universal across tasks or depths, but we believe cosine scoring should be the default for dictionary learning on normalized representations.

</details>


### [204] [Machine Learning and the Random Walk Puzzle: Forecasting the CAD/USD Exchange Rate with Expanding Window Evaluation and SHAP Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15058)
*Louis Agyekum,Edmund Fosu Agyemang,Obu-Amoah Ampomah,Kofi Acheampong,Emmanuel Boadi,Priscilla Yaa Amakye,Fafa Shalom Tchorly,Enock Adu Bonsu,Eric Nyarko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究评估了五种机器学习模型（线性回归、随机森林、梯度提升、XGBoost、AdaBoost）在预测月度美元/加元汇率时是否能超越简单的随机游走基准。使用2017年1月至2026年5月的加拿大央行日度数据，经月度重采样后得到113个观测值。所有模型均采用扩展窗口框架进行评估，并通过Diebold-Mariano检验比较预测准确性。结果表明，随机游走模型仍是强大基准；仅有线性回归在统计上显著优于随机游走（DM = 3.0585，p = 0.0071），其余机器学习集成模型仅表现出微弱差异。结构断裂检测识别出四个关键断点：2018年美中贸易战升级、2020年新冠疫情经济复苏、2022年加拿大央行加息周期顶峰以及2024年降息周期启动。SHAP分析显示，短期滞后项（如滞后1和滞后2）及近期滚动均值是主要预测驱动因素，与汇率近似随机游走的特性一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索机器学习模型在外汇汇率预测中的实际表现，验证其是否能有效超越经典的随机游走基准，同时揭示影响预测的关键因素，为金融时间序列建模提供实证支持与解释性洞察。

Method: 采用扩展窗口框架进行严格外样本评估，使用Diebold-Mariano检验比较模型预测精度；结合结构断裂检测识别关键宏观经济事件对汇率的影响；利用SHAP值分析最佳模型的特征贡献，增强可解释性。

Result: 线性回归是唯一在统计上显著优于随机游走模型的算法，其他机器学习模型仅呈现边际改进；所有模型中，随机森林在扩展窗口下达到最低MAPE（1.17%）；SHAP分析确认短期滞后与近期均值为主要预测因子，支持汇率具有近似随机游走行为的假设。

Conclusion: 尽管机器学习模型在理论上具备更强的非线性拟合能力，但在实际月度美元/加元汇率预测中，其性能并未显著超越随机游走基准。线性回归虽表现最优，但仍难以突破随机游走的基准水平。核心预测因子为短期历史值与近期趋势，反映出汇率变动的高度依赖性和弱可预测性。

Abstract: This study examines whether machine learning (ML) models can outperform the naive random walk benchmark in forecasting the monthly USD/CAD exchange rate. Using daily data from the Bank of Canada spanning January 2017 to May 2026, resampled into 113 monthly observations, five ML models are evaluated: linear regression, random forest, gradient boosting, XGBoost, and AdaBoost. These models are benchmarked against the naive random walk model and exponential smoothing with Holt-Winters seasonality (ETS). All models are evaluated using an expanding-window framework to maintain strict out-of-sample integrity, and forecast-accuracy differences are assessed using the Diebold-Mariano (DM) test. Structural break detection identifies four significant breakpoints in the series, corresponding to the escalation of the US-China trade war in 2018, the COVID-19 economic recovery in 2020, the peak of the Bank of Canada rate-hiking cycle in 2022, and the start of the Bank of Canada rate-cutting cycle in 2024. SHAP, or Shapley Additive Explanations, analysis is applied to interpret the drivers of the best-performing ML model. The results show that the naive random walk model remains a formidable benchmark. Linear regression is the only model that statistically outperforms the naive random walk model, with a DM statistic of 3.0585 and a p value of 0.0071, whereas the ML ensemble models show only marginal differences. Random Forest with an expanding-window framework achieves the lowest MAPE of 1.17 percent among all models except the random walk. SHAP analysis confirms that short-term lags, particularly lag1 and lag2, and recent rolling means dominate predictions, consistent with the near-random-walk behavior of exchange rates.
