### [205] [Phase-Localized Curation Does Not Help: A Negative Result on Per-Phase Metric Selection for Demonstration Filtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15064)
*Aarav Bedi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在操纵演示中按阶段进行数据筛选的策略，发现基于阶段的筛选方法在三个接触丰富的LIBERO任务中表现不如全局或均匀应用的单一指标。研究指出，当缺陷信号集中在某一阶段时，跨阶段的评分聚合会稀释有效信号，导致选择较差的演示子集。此外，各阶段的最佳指标不具有任务间可迁移性，需针对每个任务重新确定，增加了复杂性。因此，研究建议优先寻找一个对缺陷最敏感的单一指标，而非分解为多阶段筛选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证在操纵演示中按阶段进行数据筛选是否优于全局或均匀应用指标，并理解其失败原因。

Method: 将轨迹分割为多个阶段，分别使用局部最有效的度量标准评估各阶段，再进行聚合；与全局和均匀应用指标的方法对比，在三个任务上进行了五次随机种子测试。

Result: 在所有任务和种子条件下，阶段门控筛选从未成为最佳策略；在两个任务中甚至表现最差（任务1：86.0 vs. 92.0；任务3：22.7 vs. 48.0）。主要原因是缺陷信号集中于单个阶段时，跨阶段聚合会稀释信号。且不同任务间无共享最优指标，无法复用。

Conclusion: 阶段划分的筛选策略并不优于单一缺陷敏感指标。实践中应优先识别一个对缺陷最敏感的全局指标，避免复杂的阶段分解与重复搜索。

Abstract: Manipulation demonstrations have temporal phase structure, and a natural hypothesis is that demonstration-curation metrics should be applied within phases rather than globally. The idea is to segment each trajectory into phases, score each phase with the metric that is locally most informative, and then aggregate. This follows directly from prior work showing that a single global metric can be the best detector of a defect and yet the worst curator of the resulting policy. We test the per-phase hypothesis on three contact-rich LIBERO pick-and-place tasks with a controlled early-release structural defect, comparing phase-gated curation against the same metrics applied uniformly and against a strong single global metric. Across all three tasks and five random seeds per condition, phase-gated curation is never the best curation strategy, and it is the worst of the three on two of the three tasks (Task 1: 86.0 vs. 92.0 for global; Task 3: 22.7 vs. 48.0 for uniform). We trace the failure to a concrete mechanism. When the defect signal is concentrated in a single phase, rank-aggregating across phases dilutes that signal with uninformative scores from defect-free phases, selecting a worse demonstration subset than simply applying the defect-informative metric everywhere. We further show that the per-phase metric selection does not transfer across tasks, since no phase shares a winning metric between any two tasks, so the selection cannot be reused and must be re-derived per task from a noisy sweep. These results bound a plausible and previously untested method, and they argue that practitioners should prefer identifying a single defect-informative metric over decomposing curation by phase. We release the full pipeline, all metric implementations, and per-seed results.

</details>


### [206] [TriAdReview: Triangular Adversarial Review Architecture for Multi-Model Technical Document Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15074)
*Zhiqiang Zhou,Junliang Dai,Xu Ling*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TriAdReview，一种基于三角对抗审查的架构，通过两个独立的评审模型（工程与边界视角）和三角判断机制，迭代优化生成模型输出。在五个基准任务上评估，三模型配置相比单模型基线整体提升10.1%，尤其在安全审计、代码生成和架构设计中表现显著；但在需求分析任务中下降7.5%，揭示系统存在简化倾向的结构性偏差。通过任务类型框架分析该边界条件，并证明提示适配可部分缓解问题。研究首次实证揭示多模型对抗审查在何种情境下有益或有害，对协作式AI系统设计具重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单模型生成技术文档常存在过度工程化、安全盲点和覆盖不全等问题，亟需更可靠的多模型协同审查机制以提升生成质量。

Method: 提出三角对抗审查架构（TriAdReview），包含两个独立的评审模型（分别从工程与边界角度审视）及一个三角判断机制，通过迭代反馈优化生成模型输出。采用三种配置进行对比：单模型（基线）、双模型（单次评审）、三模型（完整系统）。

Result: 三模型配置在75次实验中总体优于单模型基线（26.2 vs. 23.8，p<0.05），提升10.1%；安全审计+27.6%、代码生成+20.8%、架构设计+15.6%；但需求分析任务下降7.5%，表明系统存在结构化简化偏倚。提示适配可部分缓解该问题。

Conclusion: 多模型对抗审查并非普适有效，其效果受任务类型影响显著。本研究首次实证刻画了其适用边界，为未来协作式AI系统的设计提供了关键依据。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for technical document generation, yet single-model outputs often suffer from over-engineering, security blind spots, and incomplete coverage. We propose TriAdReview, a triangular adversarial review architecture that employs two independent reviewer models (engineering and boundary perspectives) and a triangular judging mechanism to iteratively improve a generator model's output. We evaluate TriAdReview across five benchmark tasks - architecture design, code generation, proposal review, security audit, and requirements analysis - using three configurations: single model (baseline), dual model (single review), and triple model (full system). Results across 75 experiments (n=5 per cell) show that the triple model configuration achieves a 10.1% overall improvement over the single model baseline (26.2 vs. 23.8 out of 50; p<0.05, paired t-test), with particularly strong gains on security audit (+27.6%), code generation (+20.8%), and architecture design (+15.6%). A second scorer (mimo-v2.5-pro) confirms the direction with a smaller effect (+2.7%), suggesting moderate inter-rater agreement. However, the system shows a -7.5% degradation on requirements analysis, revealing that adversarial review architectures have a structural bias toward simplification that is counterproductive for completeness-oriented tasks. We analyze this boundary condition through a task-type framework and demonstrate that reviewer prompt adaptation partially mitigates the issue. Our findings provide the first empirical characterization of when multi-model adversarial review helps versus harms, with implications for the design of collaborative AI systems.

</details>


### [207] [An Integrable Token Mixing Layer from the Generalized Yang Baxter Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15085)
*Snigdha Chandan Khilar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: YB Mixer 是一种基于自由费米子和广义杨-巴克斯特结构的序列标记混合层，利用可积系统中的局部代数约束保证全局计算稳定性。通过伊辛交换代数，该混合器构建了保持范数的正交映射，并生成可交换的转移矩阵，实现无序推理且适应任意变量预算。为支持更长序列的泛化，采用谱循环生成器，维持系统的正交性和可交换性，从而形成一个高度稳定且数学基础坚实的序列处理架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了构建一个在序列处理中具有全局计算稳定性的模型，同时具备对长序列的泛化能力以及灵活的变量预算适应性，提出基于可积系统原理的新型混合层。

Method: 基于自由费米子与广义杨-巴克斯特结构设计序列混合层；引入伊辛交换代数构造正交且保范的映射；利用谱循环生成器保持系统性质；通过可交换转移矩阵实现顺序无关的推理机制。

Result: YB Mixer 实现了精确的范数保持、全局计算稳定性、顺序无关推理及对任意变量预算的适应性，并能有效泛化到更长序列长度。

Conclusion: YB Mixer 提供了一个数学严谨、计算稳定且可扩展的序列建模框架，适用于需要高稳定性与灵活性的序列处理任务。

Abstract: The YB Mixer is a sequence token mixing layer derived from free fermion and generalized Yang Baxter structures. It applies a core principle from integrable systems where a local algebraic constraint guarantees global computational stability. By using the Ising exchange algebra the mixer creates a free fermionic structure that acts as an exactly norm preserving orthogonal map. This algebra also produces commuting transfer matrices which allow inference to be order free and adaptable to any variable budget. To ensure the model can generalize to longer sequence lengths it uses a spectral circulant generator. This generator maintains the crucial orthogonal and commuting properties of the system. The result is a highly stable and mathematically grounded architecture for sequence processing.

</details>


### [208] [High-Dimensional Random Projection for Activation Steering in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15092)
*Minh-Hieu Pham,Bach Do,Laziz Abdullaev,Tan Minh Nguyen,Khoat Than*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HiDRA is a training-free activation steering method that uses high-dimensional random projection to better capture nonlinear discriminative signals in LLMs, outperforming linear methods with minimal computational cost.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing difference-in-means methods only capture mean differences in activations and fail to exploit nonlinear feature structures under the superposition hypothesis.

Method: HiDRA performs activation addition in a randomly projected high-dimensional space to recover richer discriminative patterns beyond linear methods.

Result: Experiments show HiDRA consistently improves behavioral control across diverse LLM families and benchmarks, surpassing baselines without significant computational overhead.

Conclusion: HiDRA effectively enhances activation steering by leveraging high-dimensional projections, offering superior control over LLM behavior while remaining training-free and efficient.

Abstract: Activation steering has emerged as a key methodology for controlling the behavior of large language models (LLMs). Existing difference-in-means based methods, however, are fundamentally limited: they capture only mean differences between class activations and fail to recover discriminative signals that naturally exist in the nonlinear feature subspace under the superposition hypothesis. Motivated by that, we propose High-Dimensional Random-projection for Activation Steering (HiDRA), a training-free approach that integrates seamlessly with existing activation steering methods. By performing activation addition in the projected high-dimensional space, HiDRA can provably capture a better discriminative structure beyond the reach of linear methods. Experiments across diverse LLM families and benchmarks demonstrate that HiDRA consistently outperforms baseline counterparts, achieving stronger behavioral control without significant computational overhead.

### [209] [Diversity-Driven Offline Multi-Objective Optimization via Nested Pareto Set Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15115)
*Yiyi Zhu,Yaolin Wen,Xiang Xia,Xin An,Hanyi Si,Xiang Shu,Yangde Fu,Liang Dou,Hong Qian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DOMOO的多样性驱动的离线多目标优化方法，旨在解决离线多目标优化中的分布外（OOD）问题。通过引入累积风险控制模块、嵌套帕累托集学习策略以及基于$	ext{IGD}_	ext{offline}$的多样性选择机制，有效提升了解的质量与多样性。实验表明，DOMOO在收敛性和多样性方面均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在离线多目标优化中，由于无法访问真实目标函数，且存在分布外（OOD）问题，导致代理模型预测不准确，进而使优化器偏向于帕累托前沿的极端解，影响解的质量和多样性。因此需要一种能够缓解OOD问题并提升解集多样性和质量的方法。

Method: 提出DOMOO方法，包含三个核心组件：1）累积风险控制模块，用于估计候选解的风险以缓解OOD问题；2）嵌套帕累托集学习（PSL）策略，联合学习偏好与PSL参数并进行优化，适应不同几何结构的帕累托前沿；3）多样性驱动的选择策略，结合专为离线场景设计的$	ext{IGD}_	ext{offline}$指标，兼顾收敛性与多样性，避免传统超体积指标的偏差。

Result: 在合成数据和真实世界基准测试中，DOMOO在收敛性和多样性方面均取得了最优平均排名，显著优于对比方法，证明了其在离线多目标优化中的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: DOMOO通过风险控制、自适应帕累托学习和多样性驱动选择，在离线多目标优化中实现了高质量、高多样性的解集生成，有效缓解了分布外问题带来的负面影响，是当前该领域的一项重要进展。

Abstract: Multi-objective optimization (MOO) has emerged as a powerful approach to solving complex optimization problems involving multiple objectives. In many practical scenarios, function evaluations are unavailable or prohibitively expensive, necessitating optimization solely based on a fixed offline dataset. In this setting, known as offline MOO, the goal is to find out the Pareto set without access to the true objective functions. This setting suffers from the out-of-distribution (OOD) issue, where the surrogate model is not accurate for unseen designs. Due to the OOD issue, surrogate errors may cause the optimizer to select solutions that do not lie on the true Pareto front and are biased toward its extremes. To address this, this paper proposes Diversity-driven Offline Multi-Objective Optimization (DOMOO), which aims to find out a diverse and high-quality set of solutions. First, DOMOO incorporates an accumulative risk control module that estimates the potential risk of candidate solutions and alleviates the OOD issue between the training data and the generated solutions. In addition, a nested Pareto set learning (PSL) strategy is proposed to jointly learn preference and PSL parameters, then optimize them, enabling adaptation to diverse Pareto front geometries. To further enhance solution quality, we design a diversity-driven selection strategy that extracts a representative and well-distributed set of final solutions. To achieve this diversity-driven selection strategy, we propose $\text{IGD}_\text{offline}$, a tailored indicator for the offline setting that considers both diversity and convergence, and avoids the bias of hypervolume indicator. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world benchmarks show that DOMOO achieves the best average rank across tasks in both convergence and diversity among the compared methods.

</details>

Conclusion: 仅依赖最终答案准确率的评估方式会掩盖模型在处理偏见时的行为差异，应引入痕迹级别的诊断机制以实现更负责任的评估，推动模型可解释性与透明度的提升。

Abstract: Reasoning models are increasingly used in settings where the final answer is not the only object of review: educational tools may show students intermediate steps, decision-support systems may require human oversight, and audit workflows may inspect traces for misleading or biased input. In such settings, two responses can receive the same final-answer score while differing in whether the trace explicitly flags injected biasing content. Accuracy-only evaluation collapses these cases. We study this gap as a measurement blind spot for responsible evaluation and introduce a minimal trace-level diagnostic with two axes: \emph{susceptibility} (whether the bias breaks a previously correct answer) and \emph{acknowledgment} (whether the trace contains a rubric-defined surface reference to the injected content). Across thousands of biased GSM8K trials, GPT-4o and Claude Sonnet~4 have similar susceptibility rates ($1.3\%$ vs.\ $1.2\%$) but substantially different acknowledgment rates ($13.0\%$ vs.\ $75.0\%$) under the same rubric.

The probability of spillover varies across individuals, and their connections, leading to heterogeneity. Understanding and accurately estimating the spillover probabilities among users in social networks is crucial for improving the effectiveness of stimulated word-of-mouth. To address this, we present a novel contextual multi-armed bandit framework that learns individual spillover probabilities and ranks connected users to maximize rewards from stimulated word-of-mouth. Experiments on real-world network datasets demonstrate that accounting for spillover heterogeneity enhances the targeting precision of top-$k$ connected users, boosting rewards and outperforming baseline methods that do not learn individual spillover effects.

### [212] [False Sense of Safety in Selective Signal Classification: Auditing Bound Tightness and Exchangeability for Risk Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15153)
*Jingwen Zhou,Mingzhe Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究评估了在信号域检测器（如机器异常声音检测和AI生成图像取证）上，四种校准规则（NAIVE、Hoeffding、Clopper-Pearson、WSR）在分布无关风险控制下的表现。发现：(i) 常用的NAIVE阈值方法在49-73%的合成实验和高达68%的真实数据分割中超过预设误差预算，虽无理论保证但造成虚假安全感；(ii) 严格性至关重要：CP和WSR能提供有效覆盖而Hoeffding无法做到，且在可交换分割下未出现预算超限；(iii) 在分组部署场景（如未知机器类型或生成器）中，认证规则仍出现9-30%的超限，远高于置信水平delta，问题根源在于交换性假设失效，而非边界本身不成立，采用每组保守阈值可恢复有效性但显著降低覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证选择性预测在真实信号域任务中的实际可靠性，揭示现有校准规则在非理想条件下的失效机制，特别是交换性假设破裂的影响。

Method: 通过合成数据与真实数据分割实验，对比NAIVE、Hoeffding、Clopper-Pearson和WSR四类校准规则在异常声音检测和AI图像伪造检测任务中的误差率控制表现，分析其在不同部署场景下的预算遵守情况。

Result: NAIVE方法频繁超预算；CP与WSR在可交换条件下表现稳健且无超限；分组部署中所有认证方法均出现明显超限，表明问题源于交换性假设失效，而非统计边界本身不可靠。

Conclusion: 当前分布无关的选择性预测方法在真实世界部署中面临严峻挑战，尤其当存在未见机器类型或生成器时，其有效性依赖于严格的交换性假设。建议在分组场景中使用保守阈值以保障安全性，但需接受覆盖率下降的代价。

Abstract: Selective prediction with distribution-free risk control promises that, with confidence 1-delta over the calibration draw, the error rate of accepted inputs stays below a user budget alpha. We audit this promise on signal-domain detectors -- machine anomalous-sound detection (ASD) and AI-generated-image forensics -- for four calibration rules: uncertified empirical thresholding (NAIVE) and certified Hoeffding, Clopper-Pearson (CP), and betting (WSR) upper confidence bounds. We report three findings. (i) NAIVE thresholding, common in practice, exceeds its declared budget in 49-73% of synthetic trials (n=200 calibration points) and in up to 68% of real-data splits: a false sense of safety rather than a broken theorem, since the rule never had a certificate. (ii) Tightness matters: CP and WSR certify substantial coverage where Hoeffding certifies none, with zero observed budget overruns under exchangeable splits. (iii) Under grouped deployment (unseen machine types or generators), certified rules overrun in 9-30% of trials -- far above delta -- showing the failure lies in the broken exchangeability premise, not in the bounds; a conservative per-group threshold restores validity at a severe coverage cost.

### [214] [PolyKV: Heterogeneous Retention and Allocation for KV Cache Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15157)
*Chao Fei,Panos Kalnis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PolyKV 是一种分层的 KV 缓存优化框架，通过为不同 Transformer 层选择合适的压缩策略并分配非均匀缓存预算，在保持总预算不变的前提下，显著提升长上下文大模型推理性能。实验表明，PolyKV 在相同平均 512 token 缓存预算下，分别恢复了 LLaMA-3.1-8B 和 Qwen3-8B 上 54.5% 和 25.7% 的 LongBench 性能差距，并在 128-1024 的预算范围内持续优于最强基线 1.7%-6.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 KV 缓存压缩方法通常采用统一的压缩策略和固定的缓存预算，忽略了不同 Transformer 层在预填充和解码阶段所起作用的差异，导致资源分配不合理，限制了性能表现。因此需要一种更灵活、分层的优化机制来适配各层特性。

Method: 提出 PolyKV 框架，结合层级信号动态选择适合的 KV 压缩策略，并在固定总预算下实现非均匀的缓存预算分配，支持多种已有方法的异构组合。

Conclusion: PolyKV 通过分层设计实现了对 KV 缓存压缩策略与预算分配的精细化控制，有效提升了长上下文推理效率，验证了异构组合与自适应资源配置在大模型推理优化中的有效性。

Abstract: KV cache compression is essential for reducing the memory cost of long-context large language model inference. Existing approaches, however, typically apply a single compression policy and a uniform cache budget across all transformer layers. This uniform design ignores the fact that different layers can play different roles during prefill and decoding, and may therefore require different eviction strategies and cache capacities. We present PolyKV, a layer-wise KV cache optimization framework that considers design space with method selection and budget allocation. PolyKV routes each layer to a suitable KV compression policy based on layer-level signals, while assigning non-uniform budgets under a fixed total budget. This formulation enables heterogeneous compositions of existing KV cache methods. Experiments on LLaMA-3.1-8B and Qwen3-8B show that, under the same 512-token average KV budget, PolyKV recovers 54.5% and 25.7% of the LongBench performance gap between the strongest single-policy baseline and FullKV, respectively. Despite recent progress, most existing methods are trained under the assumption of abundant training data, which substantially limits their effectiveness in data-scarce settings. In this paper, we propose TimeMoDE, a novel framework that integrates Diffusion Transformers with Mixture-of-Experts to exploit both domain adaptability and diffusion-stage awareness for time series generation under data scarcity. It is pre-trained on a large-scale collection of multi-domain datasets to extract domain-agnostic temporal representations and domain-specific information benefiting generalization during fine-tuning. We propose Domain Prompts to condition expert assignment for indistinguishable noised tokens, mitigating the limitations of capturing inter-dataset relationships. Moreover, we incorporate diffusion timestep signals to equip the experts with awareness of time series degradation variations, facilitating adaptive calibrate to stage-dependent denoising requirements. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TimeMoDE outperforms existing methods under diverse low-data settings. It establishes an innovative paradigm for advanced time series few-shot generation.

### [216] [StarOR: Synergizing Tree Search and Test-Time Reinforcement Learning for Optimization Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15197)
*Jiajun Li,Yu Ding,Shisi Guan,Ran Hou,Wanyuan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: StarOR 是一种结合蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）与测试时强化学习的协同搜索-适应框架，用于优化建模。它将建模过程分解为四个阶段，在每个非终止节点通过GRPO更新临时的LoRA适配器，利用MCTS生成的兄弟节点作为局部比较集，将搜索过程转化为针对具体实例的策略优化。同时，采用无监督多维度奖励系统，为中间建模决策提供细粒度反馈，无需真实标签。在五个优化基准上的实验表明，StarOR 在仅使用4B主干模型的情况下，性能超越现有方法及前沿大模型，达到当前最优水平。

Result: 在五个不同的优化基准上进行实验，StarOR在仅使用4B规模主干模型的情况下，性能显著优于现有方法和当前最先进大语言模型，实现了状态领先的表现。

Conclusion: StarOR通过将搜索探索与测试时自适应相结合，有效克服了传统方法在可扩展性、泛化性和中间决策反馈方面的局限。其框架具备良好的适应性与效率，为自动化优化建模提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Optimization modeling is inherently hierarchical, requiring a precise sequence of symbolic commitments. Traditional learning-based automated optimization modeling methods improve modeling policies through large-scale annotated or curated training data, but are costly to adapt to new problem distributions. Meanwhile, one-shot generation remains brittle in hierarchical modeling, where early symbolic errors can propagate into invalid formulations. Test-time scaling offers a promising alternative by enabling structural exploration with additional instance-level computation; however, existing search-based methods typically rely on a fixed policy, causing repeated rollouts to inherit similar modeling biases and providing limited credit assignment for intermediate decisions. To address these limitations, we propose StarOR, a synergistic search-and-adaptation framework that couples MCTS with Test-Time Reinforcement Learning for optimization modeling. StarOR decomposes the modeling process into four stages and updates a transient LoRA adapter via GRPO at each non-terminal node. By using MCTS-generated siblings as local comparison sets, StarOR transforms search-time exploration into instance-specific policy refinement. Moreover, an unsupervised multi-faceted reward system provides fine-grained feedback for intermediate formulation decisions without ground-truth labels. Experiments across five optimization benchmarks show that StarOR achieves state-of-the-art performance even with a 4B backbone, outperforming existing methods and the frontier LLMs.

### [218] [Can Neural Networks Achieve Optimal Computational-statistical Tradeoff? An Analysis on Single-Index Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15219)
*Siyu Chen,Beining Wu,Miao Lu,Zhuoran Yang,Tianhao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究神经网络在梯度方法下是否能实现学习高斯单指数模型的最优计算-统计权衡。提出一种统一的基于梯度的两层神经网络训练算法，可在多项式时间内实现与统计查询（SQ）下界匹配的样本复杂度 $\widetilde{O}(d^{s^\star/2} \lor d)$，适用于多种损失和激活函数。针对 $k$-稀疏情形，引入新颖的权重扰动技术，达到 $\widetilde{\Omega}(k^{s^\star})$ 的 SQ 下界，且算法性能与其匹配至多对数因子。该框架具有独立意义，可能推广至稀疏张量PCA等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，任何多项式时间算法在统计查询（SQ）框架下至少需要 $\Omega(d^{s^\star/2} \lor d)$ 样本，但尚不清楚神经网络能否达到这一样本复杂度。本文旨在探究梯度方法训练的神经网络是否可实现最优的计算-统计权衡。

Method: 提出一种统一的梯度基两层神经网络训练算法，结合标签变换、景观平滑等思想，并引入新的权重扰动技术以利用稀疏结构，适用于广泛损失与激活函数。

Result: 所提算法在一般情形下实现样本复杂度 $\widetilde{O}(d^{s^\star/2} \lor d)$，与 SQ 下界匹配；在 $k$-稀疏情形下达到 $\widetilde{\Omega}(k^{s^\star})$，算法性能与其匹配至多对数因子。

Conclusion: 神经网络通过梯度方法可在多项式时间内实现最优的计算-统计权衡，所提出的统一框架及权重扰动技术具有理论深度与潜在应用价值，为解决稀疏张量PCA等类似问题提供了新思路。

Abstract: In this work, we tackle the following question: Can neural networks trained with gradient-based methods achieve the optimal computational-statistical tradeoff in learning Gaussian single-index models? Prior research has shown that any polynomial-time algorithm under the statistical query (SQ) framework requires $Ω(d^{s^\star/2}\lor d)$ samples, where $s^\star$ is the generative exponent representing the intrinsic difficulty of learning the underlying model. However, it remains unknown whether neural networks can achieve this sample complexity. Inspired by prior techniques such as label transformation and landscape smoothing for learning single-index models, we propose a unified gradient-based algorithm for training a two-layer neural network in polynomial time. Our method is adaptable to a variety of loss and activation functions, covering a broad class of existing approaches. We show that our algorithm learns a feature representation that strongly aligns with the unknown signal $θ^\star$, with sample complexity $\widetilde{O} (d^{s^\star/2} \lor d)$, matching the SQ lower bound up to a polylogarithmic factor for all generative exponents $s^\star\geq 1$. Furthermore, we extend our approach to the setting where $θ^\star$ is $k$-sparse for $k = o(\sqrt{d})$ by introducing a novel weight perturbation technique that leverages the sparsity structure. We derive a corresponding SQ lower bound of order $\widetildeΩ(k^{s^\star})$, matched by our method up to a polylogarithmic factor. Our framework, especially the weight perturbation technique, is of independent interest, and suggests potential gradient-based solutions to other problems such as sparse tensor PCA.

### [221] [M-CTX: Exact and Scalable Spatial Context Retrieval for Trajectory Analytics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15244)
*Kun Ma,Qilong Han,Chengjing Song,Jingzheng Yao,Xiao Han,Yuee Zhou,Changmao Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: M-CTX 是一个精确且可扩展的空间上下文检索框架，用于轨迹分析。它将上下文构建转化为一次摄入、多次查询的时空数据库任务，通过可组合的索引支持操作替代了三个暴力搜索阶段（OSM范围检索、SDF计算、移动船只邻居查找）。其学习型范围索引后端 BR-LZ 提供完全召回的MBR重叠范围检索，并将候选放大减少1.1x–2.7x。在四个海事区域、八种基线系统、最多4000万空间特征的合成工作负载以及10^7条记录的AIS流上，M-CTX 完全复现了参考上下文。在548万锚点数据集上，将上下文构建时间从约17个CPU天缩短至1.8小时，实现226倍的端到端加速。可选存储模式进一步将SDF上下文压缩64倍，仅带来0.04米ADE变化。这些结果确立了精确空间上下文检索作为现代轨迹分析中的核心数据库问题。代码与数据集公开于 https://github.com/mark000071/M-CTX-Traj。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前轨迹预测模型越来越多地依赖外部空间上下文（如地图几何、符号距离场、邻近移动代理），但为每个训练锚点构建这些上下文已成为隐藏的系统瓶颈。在典型的海事AIS管道中，空间上下文构建耗时约17个CPU天，远超下游预测器的成本。因此需要一种高效、精确且可扩展的上下文检索方法。

Method: M-CTX 将上下文构建重构为‘一次摄入、多次查询’的时空数据库任务，采用可组合的索引支持操作替代传统的暴力搜索。其核心是学习型范围索引后端 BR-LZ，实现召回完整的MBR重叠范围检索，显著降低候选集放大率。同时支持高密度空间特征和大规模数据流处理，并提供可选压缩存储模式以节省空间。

Result: 在多个真实和合成场景下，M-CTX 精确复现了原始上下文；在548万锚点数据集上，将上下文构建时间从17个CPU天降至1.8小时，提速226倍；使用压缩存储模式可实现64倍空间压缩，仅引入0.04米的ADE误差。

Conclusion: M-CTX 成功将精确空间上下文检索提升为现代轨迹分析中的核心数据库问题，具备高度可扩展性与实际部署价值，显著降低了轨迹建模的系统开销。

Abstract: Modern trajectory predictors increasingly condition on external spatial context, such as map geometry, signed distance fields (SDFs), and nearby moving agents. While this context improves prediction quality, constructing it for every training anchor has become a hidden systems bottleneck. In a representative maritime AIS pipeline, spatial context construction requires roughly 17 CPU-days for a 5.48M-anchor corpus, dominating the cost of the downstream predictor. We present M-CTX, an exact and scalable spatial context-retrieval framework for trajectory analytics. M-CTX recasts context construction as an ingest-once, query-many spatial database workload and replaces three brute-force stages -- OSM range retrieval, SDF computation, and moving-vessel neighbour lookup -- with composable, index-backed operators. Its learned range-index backend, BR-LZ, provides recall-complete MBR-overlap range retrieval and reduces candidate amplification by 1.1x--2.7x relative to global-expansion one-curve baselines. Across four maritime regions, eight baseline systems, synthetic workloads with up to 40M spatial features, and 10^7-record AIS streams, M-CTX reproduces the reference context exactly. On the 5.48M-anchor corpus, it reduces context construction from about 17 CPU-days to 1.8 hours, a measured 226x end-to-end speed-up. An optional storage mode further compresses SDF context by 64x with only a 0.04 m ADE change. These results establish exact spatial context retrieval as a first-class database problem in modern trajectory analytics. Code and datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/mark000071/M-CTX-Traj.

### [222] [Exploring Starts Are Not Enough: Counterexamples and a Fix for Monte Carlo Exploring Starts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15247)
*Octave Oliviers,Glenn Vinnicombe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了蒙特卡洛探索起点（MCES）在表格设置下的渐近行为，通过构造反例证明初始访问和首次访问的MCES可能收敛到次优解。针对初始访问情况，提出一种基于状态的逆更新频率学习率调整方法，可保证收敛至最优。该方法适用于大规模问题中的值函数近似。同时，扩展分析表明首次访问MCES也可能收敛到次优解，从而基本解决了一个长期开放的基本问题：探索起点本身不足以保证收敛到最优。结果强调学习率选择与探索-利用平衡对算法收敛性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究蒙特卡洛探索起点（MCES）在表格设置下的收敛性，特别是其是否能保证收敛到最优策略，这是强化学习中一个长期未解的问题。

Method: 构造反例分析初始访问与首次访问的MCES行为；提出基于状态的逆更新频率学习率调整机制以恢复收敛性；扩展分析验证首次访问情形下的次优收敛可能性。

Result: 证明了初始访问和首次访问的MCES均可能收敛到次优解；提出的新学习率调整方法可确保初始访问MCES收敛至最优；该方法适用于大规模问题中的值函数近似；揭示了学习率与更新频率平衡对收敛的关键作用。

Conclusion: 探索起点本身不足以保证蒙特卡洛控制方法的收敛到最优；算法的收敛性高度依赖于学习率设计与不同动作更新频率的相对关系；合理的设计学习率策略对于实现高效、可扩展的蒙特卡洛控制至关重要。

Abstract: The asymptotic behaviour of Monte Carlo Exploring Starts (MCES) is a long-standing open question in reinforcement learning, even in the tabular setting. We investigated the convergence properties of tabular MCES by constructing examples in which the algorithm converges to suboptimal solutions. This paper presents new counterexamples for both initial-visit and first-visit MCES and gives a convergence-restoring modification for the initial-visit case. We show that stable suboptimal solutions may exist for initial-visit MCES with sample-average updates even when greedy actions are updated more often than non-greedy actions on average. However, by scaling learning rates inversely to update frequencies on a state-by-state basis, convergence to optimality is guaranteed. Unlike previous uniformisation methods, this modification is applicable to large-scale problems that require approximating the estimated value function. We then extend the example to show that sample-average first-visit MCES may also converge to suboptimal solutions. This largely settles a fundamental open problem and shows that exploring starts alone do not guarantee convergence to optimality. More broadly, these results highlight that convergence depends critically on the relative size and frequency of updates applied to different actions, making the choice of learning rates and the balance between exploration and exploitation central to the analysis of MCES and the implementation of scalable Monte Carlo control methods.

</details>


### [223] [AI for Social Good: An Investigation of the Causal Relationship Between Environmental Regulations and Their Effects on Air Pollution in London, UK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15257)
*Yang Han,Jacqueline CK Lam,Victor OK Li,Yiu-Wai Man*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Develops a Bayesian deep learning framework to estimate the impact of air pollution regulations on PM₂.₅ in London (2010–2020), integrating meteorological, socioeconomic, and policy data. Uses Bayesian LSTM and embedding layers to model temporal dynamics and adjust for non-random policy implementation via propensity scores. Finds an average PM₂.₅ reduction of 1.88 μg/m³ (12.35%) with strong effects from 2013 onward, demonstrating the value of uncertainty-aware causal AI in environmental governance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Estimating the effects of air pollution regulations is challenging due to non-random policy implementation and confounding factors like weather, socioeconomic trends, and overlapping interventions. Accurate assessment is critical for public health and evidence-based policy.

Method: Proposes a Bayesian deep learning framework combining Bayesian LSTM for temporal dependencies, Bayesian embedding layers for regulation and time inputs, and a regulation status prediction branch for propensity score adjustment. Counterfactual PM₂.₅ levels are generated under no-regulation scenarios, with uncertainty quantified via repeated Bayesian training and bootstrap resampling.

Result: London’s regulations reduced PM₂.₅ by an average of 1.88 μg/m³ (12.35%), with a 95% CI of 1.64–2.12 μg/m³. Effects were minimal before 2013, became evident between 2013–2017, and peaked in 2018–2019.

Conclusion: Sustained and cumulative regulatory efforts significantly improved London’s air quality. The study highlights the potential of uncertainty-aware causal AI to enhance environmental accountability and support data-driven governance.

Abstract: Air pollution regulation is central to urban public health governance, but estimating its effects is difficult because policies are implemented non-randomly and pollution trajectories are shaped by meteorology, socioeconomic change, temporal trends, and overlapping interventions. This study develops an uncertainty-aware Bayesian deep learning framework to estimate the aggregate effect of air pollution regulations on PM$_{2.5}$ concentrations in London from 2010 to 2020. The framework integrates daily PM$_{2.5}$ observations from Inner London monitoring stations, meteorological covariates, annual socioeconomic indicators, month-of-year and day-of-week indicators, and daily regulation status data for 32 policy measures. A Bayesian LSTM captures temporal dependencies in environmental and socioeconomic covariates, Bayesian embedding layers represent temporal and regulation status inputs, and a regulation status prediction branch supports propensity score-based adjustment for non-random policy implementation. Regulatory effects are estimated by comparing observed PM$_{2.5}$ concentrations with counterfactual predictions under a hypothetical no-regulation scenario, with uncertainty summarized across repeated Bayesian training runs and bootstrap resampling. Results show that London's regulations were associated with an average PM$_{2.5}$ reduction of 1.88 $μ$g/m$^3$, a relative reduction of 12.35%, with a 95% confidence interval of 1.64-2.12 $μ$g/m$^3$. Estimated effects were limited before 2013, became clearer from 2013 to 2017, and were strongest in 2018 and 2019. The findings suggest that sustained and cumulative regulatory interventions contributed to measurable improvements in London's air quality. This study demonstrates how uncertainty-aware causal AI can support environmental accountability, public health protection, and evidence-based governance for environmental decision-making.

### [224] [Trust-Region Diffusion Policies for Massively Parallel On-Policy RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15260)
*Huy Le,Onur Celik,Denis Blessing,Tai Hoang,Claas A Voelcker,Axel Brunnbauer,Felix Richter,Michael Volpp,Gerhard Neumann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为信任区域扩散策略（TruDi）的新方法，用于在大规模并行的在线策略强化学习中训练扩散策略。尽管扩散模型具有更强的表达能力，但大多数基于扩散的强化学习方法适用于离线或离线策略训练。TruDi通过引入信任区域优化规则，对整个扩散轨迹施加KL散度约束，以应对在线策略设置下数据分布快速变化带来的训练不稳定性问题。在包含73个任务的4个大规模并行基准测试中，TruDi在标准任务上表现优于或相当强于现有基线，在更具挑战性的人形控制任务上更是取得显著提升，建立了新的基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法多依赖于简单的高斯策略参数化，表达能力有限；虽然扩散模型具备更强的策略表达能力且在复杂控制任务中表现优异，但其多数方法仅适用于离线或离线策略训练，难以适应大规模并行、在线策略训练的动态环境。因此，亟需一种能稳定训练复杂扩散策略的在线策略框架。

Method: 提出信任区域扩散策略（TruDi），结合信任区域优化机制，对扩散策略在整个轨迹上的KL散度进行约束，从而在数据分布快速变化的在线策略环境中保持训练稳定性。该方法支持大规模并行模拟，适用于复杂的连续控制任务。

Result: 在73个任务的4个大规模并行强化学习基准测试中，TruDi在标准任务上表现与最强基线相当或更优，在更具挑战性的人形控制任务中实现明显性能提升，验证了其在复杂环境下的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: TruDi成功实现了在大规模并行在线策略强化学习中使用扩散策略的稳定训练，为复杂控制任务提供了一个强有力的新型基准，推动了扩散模型在在线策略强化学习中的应用发展。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with massively parallel simulations has become a standard framework for developing robust, deployable policies; however, most existing approaches still rely on simple Gaussian policy parameterizations. Diffusion models provide a more expressive policy class and have shown strong performance on challenging control problems, yet most diffusion-based RL methods are designed for offline or off-policy training. In this work, we ask whether diffusion policies can be trained effectively in the massively parallel, on-policy regime. To this end, we introduce Trust-region Diffusion Policies (TruDi), which enables diffusion policies for on-policy RL with massively parallel simulations. This setting is particularly challenging because the data distribution changes quickly across updates, making stable training with complex policies difficult. TruDi addresses this by integrating a trust-region optimization rule to enforce a KL-divergence constraint over the entire diffusion trajectory. Empirically, we evaluate TruDi on a diverse set of 4 massively parallel RL benchmarks comprising a total of 73 tasks. Across these tasks, TruDi consistently outperforms or is on-par with strong baselines on standard tasks and achieves clear gains on more challenging humanoid control tasks, establishing a strong new baseline for massively parallel on-policy RL.

### [225] [When to use what Schatten-$p$ norm in deep learning?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15268)
*Thomas Pethick*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了基于Schatten-$\infty$的优化器（如Muon）在不同场景下的表现差异源于问题的规模和维度，指出在低维情形下（包括Chinchilla缩放规律）更小的Schatten-$p$几何反而更优，并通过新的噪声鲁棒加速结果解释了为何此类方法无需预热、偏好大批次及提供了通用的批量大小缩放规则。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种针对$ p>2 $的SODA框架的新噪声鲁棒加速结果，结合对不同几何结构下优化性能的分析，建立理论依据以解释实际现象。

Result: 证明在低维情况下，较小的Schatten-$p$几何更优；解释了Muon类方法无需预热、自然偏好大批次的原因，并推导出适用于任意$ p $的批量大小缩放规则。

Conclusion: Schatten-$\infty$优化器的有效性依赖于具体应用的维度和规模，低维场景下更小的$ p $值更具优势，这统一了此前矛盾的实证观察。

Abstract: Schatten-$\infty$ based optimizers such as Muon have shown promising empirical performance, but there remains seemingly conflicting observations regarding whether they are beneficial. We resolve this conflict by showing that the conclusion is regime dependent. Even when the objective is smooth in the Schatten-$\infty$ geometry, smaller Schatten-$p$ geometries can be optimal, specifically in the low-dimensional regime, which we show includes Chinchilla scaling. This conclusion follows from a new noise-robust acceleration result for the SODA framework for $p>2$. The same analysis explains why Muon-like methods do not require warmup, why they naturally favor large batches, and yields a batch size scaling rule for arbitrary $p$.

*Jinhan Liu,Mahsa Shoaran*

Abstract: Affective and cognitive disorders manifest as distributed, time-varying brain network dynamics across regions, channels, and time, challenging robust representation learning from EEG/sEEG for clinical diagnosis. We propose RECTOR (Masked Region-Channel-Temporal Modeling), an end-to-end self-supervised framework that unifies joint region-channel-temporal representation learning beyond fixed anatomical priors. At its core, RECTOR-SA is a hierarchical, block-sparse self-attention induced by Adaptive Functional Partitioning that evolves region structures from static anatomical definitions to adaptive functional regions. The self-supervision is driven by Masked Topology and Representation Learning, which jointly optimizes three complementary objectives: Masked Predictive Modeling, Topological Structure Modeling, and Cross-View Consistency. Across diverse benchmarks, RECTOR sets a new state-of-the-art in EEG emotion recognition and sEEG task-engagement classification. Crucially, its strong robustness to missing channels and cross-montage generalization underscores its potential for large-scale pre-training on heterogeneous EEG/sEEG, providing interpretable insights at both region and channel levels.

### [227] [Rethinking Structural Anomaly Detection: From Decision Boundaries to Projection Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15280)
*Alexander Bauer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于几何视角的结构异常检测方法，通过学习正常样本流形上的投影算子，将异常定义为经投影后发生显著变化的样本。该方法将异常检测重新表述为投影残差问题，自然融入了流形数据的先验假设，避免了传统概率建模中的缺陷，尤其改善了对罕见但正常的样本的误判问题。同时，该框架统一解释了重建类方法的成功与局限，并揭示了投影对齐模型具有良好泛化能力的原因在于其向流形收缩的特性。实验表明，该方法在性能上优于边界法和现有重建法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有异常检测方法通常依赖于概率密度估计或学习封闭决策边界，隐含假设正常数据占据环境空间中非零体积区域。然而，实际数据往往位于低维流形上，导致现有方法的归纳偏置与数据结构不匹配，性能下降。因此，需要一种更符合流形数据特性的新方法。

Method: 提出一种基于几何视角的方法：学习正常样本流形上的投影算子，将异常定义为被投影后发生变化的样本，即通过投影残差判断异常性。该方法不依赖概率建模，而是以投影质量为核心，实现对异常的判定。

Result: 实验验证了投影对齐方法在多种数据集上的优越性能，不仅超越了传统的边界基方法，也改进了现有的重建基方法；同时有效缓解了对罕见但正常样本的误判问题，展现出更强的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 该方法从几何角度重构了异常检测范式，将流形结构纳入核心设计，提供了一个统一且有效的框架，既解释了现有方法的成败，又在实践中实现了显著性能提升。

Abstract: Most existing anomaly detection methods rely on estimating a probability density or learning an enclosing decision boundary, implicitly assuming that normal data occupies a region of non-zero volume in the ambient space. In contrast, structural anomaly detection considers data that lies near a low-dimensional manifold, creating a mismatch between the inductive bias of existing methods and the structure of the data, often resulting in degraded performance. To address this mismatch, we introduce a geometric perspective. Specifically, we learn a projection operator onto the manifold of normal samples and define a sample as anomalous if it is altered by this projection. This formulation naturally integrates the inductive bias of manifold-supported data and reframes anomaly detection in terms of a projection residual, thereby resolving issues arising from modeling degenerate distributions. Notably, it provides a unifying interpretation of reconstruction-based methods by explaining their success and failure in terms of projection quality. In particular, it explains the strong generalization ability of projection-aligned models as a consequence of contraction behavior toward the manifold. Moreover, by decoupling anomaly detection from probabilistic modeling, it reduces the tendency to misclassify rare but normal samples, a widely recognized limitation of existing approaches. Empirically, we demonstrate that projection-aligned methods achieve strong performance, outperforming boundary-based methods while improving upon existing reconstruction-based approaches.

This integration allows the model to reason about unmodeled factors and produce interpretable residuals, enhancing overall predictive accuracy. ### [230] [LatentGym: A Testbed For Cross-Task Experiential Learning With Controllable Latent Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15306)

TL;DR: LatentGym 是一个可控的基准测试套件，用于研究大语言模型代理在连续任务中如何从经验中学习。它通过引入真实存在的潜在变量来组织环境，从而能够衡量代理在探索（收集关于潜在变量的信息）和利用（使用已收集信息）方面的表现。该框架帮助揭示了前沿模型在跨任务适应中的失败原因，并评估了后训练对泛化能力的影响及其来源，同时分析了任务间反馈等设计选择对训练动态和泛化效果的影响。

Motivation: 现有训练与评估框架缺乏共享且可控的潜在结构，无法有效衡量或解释代理在面对一系列相关任务时的学习与改进过程。为了推动可适应、持续学习的智能体发展，亟需一种能精确控制任务间共享结构并量化学习行为的实验平台。

Method: 提出 LatentGym 基准测试套件，每个环境均围绕一个真实的潜在变量构建，该变量决定任务间的结构关系。通过设计可调控的潜在变量和任务序列，实现对探索与利用行为的分离测量。基于此，开展多项实证研究，分析模型适应机制、后训练效果及设计因素的影响。

Result: 验证了现有前沿模型在跨任务适应上的局限性；表明后训练确实提升了跨任务泛化能力，且提升主要来源于对潜在结构的理解与利用；揭示了任务间反馈机制显著影响训练动态与最终泛化性能。

Conclusion: LatentGym 为研究大语言模型代理在连续任务中从经验中学习提供了可控、可量化的基础，有助于理解其适应机制，并指导设计更可靠、更具个性化与交互性的智能体系统。

Abstract: We envision continually learning agentic systems that become more useful over time: as they encounter sequences of related tasks, they should infer the hidden structure shared across those tasks and use it to improve future decisions. This cross-task experiential learning capability is pivotal in domains such as personalization and interactive assistance, but existing training/evaluation frameworks do not provide shared, controllable latent structures and cannot measure whether or why agents improve. We introduce LatentGym: a controllable suite in which each environment is organized around a ground-truth latent variable governing the structure across tasks. Our construction yields metrics that separate exploration (whether the agent's actions gather information about the latent) from exploitation (whether the agent uses what it has gathered). We demonstrate our suite on empirical studies addressing three questions: how and why frontier models fail to adapt across related tasks; whether post-training on related task sequences improves general cross-task adaptation, and where those gains come from; and how design choices such as inter-task feedback shape training dynamics and generalization. Together, these results establish a controlled foundation for studying how LLM agents learn from experience across tasks, and for designing agents that adapt more reliably in sequential, personalized, and interactive settings.

</details>


### [231] [LLMs on Tabular Data with Limited Semantics: Evidence from Industrial Car Retrofit Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15314)
*Aina Vila Pons,Ioannis Tzachristas,Constantinos Antoniou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究分析了工业改造规划中结构化操作数据与大语言模型（LLM）的结合效果。基于包含28.4万车辆原型注册和4.87万次清理维修记录的数据集，比较了传统表格机器学习模型与三种基于LLM的策略（嵌入特征、直接提示分类、ML+LLM堆叠）。结果显示，经典树集成模型在多数任务中表现最佳；LLM嵌入在表格任务中仍有效（二分类AUC=0.982），但直接提示在语义信号被哈希破坏后性能骤降（二分类AUC=0.500，多分类加权F1=0.018）；而混合堆叠方法在多分类任务中达到最高性能（加权F1=0.626）。时间序列任务中，基于滞后变量的机器学习优于时序基础模型，但Chronos-small在零样本预测中表现良好。结论表明，在隐私受限的工业表格数据上，LLM更适合作为增强组件而非替代强表格基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业改造规划依赖结构化数据而非自由文本，需准确预测原型是否需要改造、所需改造类型及工期。现有方法在处理复杂工业数据时存在精度与可解释性不足的问题，亟需探索先进模型技术的应用潜力。

Method: 使用真实工业数据集（284,271辆原型车与48,716次维修记录），对比传统树集成模型与三种基于LLM的方法：基于Amazon Titan的嵌入特征、Claude Sonnet 4的直接提示分类、以及ML+LLM堆叠融合策略。评估任务包括二分类改造发生预测、15类改造类型分类、单次维修时长回归及月度聚合基准。

Result: 经典树集成模型在所有任务中表现最优；LLM嵌入在保留语义信息时有效（二分类AUC=0.982），但直接提示因哈希导致语义丢失而性能崩溃（二分类AUC=0.500，多分类加权F1=0.018）；混合堆叠方法在多分类任务中达最佳结果（加权F1=0.626）。在时间序列任务中，滞后变量模型优于时序基础模型，但Chronos-small在零样本场景下表现接近。

Abstract: Industrial retrofit planning depends on structured operational data rather than free text: planners must estimate whether a newly registered prototype will require a retrofit, which retrofit package it will need, and how long the work will take. We study an industrial dataset linking a prototype-registration system (284,271 vehicles) with a retrofit-management system (48,716 cleaned visits), and compare strong tabular machine learning baselines with three LLM-based strategies on row-serialized inputs: embedding features (Amazon Titan), direct prompted classification (Claude Sonnet 4), and an ML+LLM stacking approach. Across binary occurrence prediction, 15-way retrofit-type classification, per-visit duration regression, and an aggregated monthly benchmark, classical tree ensembles remain the strongest standalone models. However, the LLM results reveal a consistent pattern: embeddings remain useful on tables (binary AUC = 0.982), direct prompting collapses once semantic signal is stripped by hashing (binary AUC = 0.500; multiclass weighted F1 = 0.018), and hybrid stacking yields the best manually built multiclass model (weighted F1 = 0.626). On the monthly benchmark, lag-based machine learning outperforms time-series foundation models, though Chronos-small remains competitive in zero-shot forecasting. The results suggest that on privacy-constrained industrial tables, LLMs are more effective as complementary components than as replacements for strong tabular baselines.

### [232] [Semantic DLM+: Improving Diffusion Language Models through Bias-variance Trade-off in Transition Kernel Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15327)
*Keyue Jiang,Yuxiang Wang,Yanan Zhao,Xiang Yu,Qifang Zhao,Bohan Tang,Baojian Zhou,Yanghua Xiao,Lin Qu,Xiaoxiao Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了扩散语言模型（DLMs）对过渡核选择的敏感性，通过泛化误差分析识别出三个关键因素：渐近偏差、暴露偏差和由核分散引起的优化方差。研究比较了掩码扩散与均匀扩散的优劣，并重新审视了语义扩散语言模型（SemDLM），发现其虽在理论上可作为平衡点，但存在语义盆地问题导致生成文本多样性不足。为此提出SemDLM+，引入全局过渡机制和语义频率惩罚以提升多样性。实验表明，SemDLM+在训练动态和生成质量上表现良好，且保持较高多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散语言模型虽然具备强大的可扩展性，但其性能高度依赖于过渡核的设计，不当设计会导致训练不稳定、收敛慢和采样偏差等问题。因此需要从理论上理解并优化过渡核的选择，以提升模型性能。

Method: 通过泛化误差分析系统研究过渡核的影响，识别出三大关键因素；对比不同过渡核（如掩码扩散、均匀扩散）的特性；提出改进方法SemDLM+，结合全局过渡机制和语义频率惩罚来缓解语义盆地问题。

Result: SemDLM+在LM1B和OpenWebText数据集上表现出更稳定的训练过程，生成语言模型性能优异，同时在文本多样性和生成质量方面达到竞争水平。

Conclusion: 语义扩散语言模型（SemDLM）虽具理论优势，但受限于语义盆地问题。通过引入全局过渡与语义频率惩罚的SemDLM+有效解决了该问题，在保持高效训练与高质量生成的同时显著提升了多样性，为非自回归语言建模提供了一种可行的新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion Language Models (DLMs) have demonstrated strong scaling capacity as alternatives to autoregressive language models. However, their performance is highly sensitive to the choice of transition kernels, and poorly designed kernels can lead to issues like training instability, slow convergence, and biased sampling. In this paper, we study this sensitivity through a principled analysis of generalization error and identify three critical factors: asymptotic bias (difficulty in approximating the posterior distribution), exposure bias (error propagation during sampling), and optimization variance induced by kernel dispersion. We further compare different transition kernels: masking diffusion yields sparse and easier posterior-approximation targets, while uniform diffusion provides stronger sampling-side repair but induces harder approximation. Motivated by this trade-off, we revisit a previously overlooked variant, semantic DLM (SemDLM), where the transition kernel corrupts tokens to neighborhoods that are semantically similar. Our theory suggests that SemDLM can serve as a plausible middle ground by reducing the posterior approximation difficulty of uniform diffusion while retaining repair ability. However, we find that SemDLM suffers from a semantic basin problem, where sampling repeatedly stays within a semantic region and produces low-diversity text. To address this, we propose SemDLM+, which adds a global transition and a semantic-frequency penalty during sampling. Experiments on LM1B and OpenWebText show that SemDLM+ improves training dynamics and achieves competitive language modeling and generation quality with satisfactory diversity.

### [233] [Probabilistic Signature Inversion: Learning Conditional Distributions from Truncated Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15332)
*Junoh Kang,Kiseop Lee,Bohyung Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将截断签名反演问题重新表述为概率问题，通过签名条件流匹配模型估计路径的条件分布。理论推导出线性统计下的贝叶斯最优误差，并为log-GBM、log-fBM和OU过程提供解析或数值可计算的基准，证明截断签名比线性统计提供更丰富的信息。实验表明，基于线性统计的重建误差与理论基准一致，而使用截断签名时误差进一步降低，生成路径能准确恢复签名并保持关键分布和时间结构，验证了方法的有效性和校准性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 截断签名反演在结构上是病态的，因为截断签名映射不是单射的，传统方法难以解决此问题。因此需要引入概率框架以刻画不确定性，并建立可验证的理论基准。

Method: 将截断签名反演转化为学习路径给定签名的条件分布；采用签名条件流匹配模型作为估计器；推导线性统计下贝叶斯最优误差，获得log-GBM的闭式解及log-fBM、OU的数值公式作为理论基准。

Result: 理论基准有效上界贝叶斯误差；实验显示线性统计条件下的误差与理论一致；使用截断签名后误差下降；生成路径能精确恢复签名并保留关键分布与时间结构，说明模型良好校准。

Conclusion: 提出了一种良定义的概率框架用于截断签名反演，具备理论支持与实证验证，适用于真实金融数据，超越了理论覆盖的参数化过程族。

Abstract: The signature transform is a principled feature map for continuous-time paths, valued for its uniqueness and universality. Recovering a path from its truncated signature is, however, structurally ill-posed because the truncated signature map is not injective. We therefore reframe truncated signature inversion as a probabilistic problem -- learning the conditional distribution of a path given its truncated signature -- and adopt a signature-conditioned flow matching model as a practical estimator. This probabilistic formulation elucidates the fundamental difficulty of inversion: Bayes reconstruction error quantifies the irreducible uncertainty remaining after conditioning on a statistic. We derive the Bayes-optimal error under linear statistics, obtaining a closed form for log-GBM and numerically tractable formulas for log-fBM and OU, yielding a concrete theoretical baseline for model validation. This baseline upper-bounds the Bayes error under truncated-signature conditioning, since truncated signatures provide richer information than linear statistics. Experiments show that empirical reconstruction errors under linear-statistics conditioning faithfully align with the theory-derived baseline, while errors decrease when the statistic is replaced with truncated signatures. Moreover, generated paths faithfully recover the conditioning signature while preserving key distributional and temporal structures, indicating that the estimator is well-calibrated to the target conditional distribution. Together, these results establish a well-posed probabilistic framework for truncated-signature inversion, with applicability demonstrated on real financial data beyond the parametric process families covered by theory.

### [234] [DiRecT: Safe Diffusion-Based Planning via Receding-Horizon Denoising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15359)
*Paolo Giaretta,Zeyang Li,Navid Azizan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DiRecT 是一种无需训练的扩散模型约束采样方法，通过滚动时域的随机最优控制（SOC）实现，在仅对最终清洁样本施加约束的同时保持扩散过程的自然动态，显著提升安全性和任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型在推理时的安全性保障不足，传统方法对每一步去噪过程强制可行性，导致中间噪声样本被过度约束，从而降低生成样本质量。而实际约束仅需作用于最终干净轨迹，因此需要更高效的约束处理机制。

Method: 提出 DiRecT 算法，基于滚动时域的随机最优控制框架，将原本难以求解的约束 SOC 问题转化为可计算的近似形式，仅在最终阶段施加约束，分离了随机去噪与约束满足过程，支持多种优化器和先验信息。

Result: 在多个安全规划基准测试中，DiRecT 显著优于现有基于扩散模型的规划基线，在保证更高安全性的同时提升了任务完成率与样本质量。

Conclusion: DiRecT 提供了一种高效、灵活且无需训练的约束采样方法，能够有效避免中间步骤的过度约束，保留扩散模型的生成能力，为安全关键场景下的扩散模型应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion models have emerged as powerful tools for planning and control by learning multimodal distributions over actions and trajectories. Yet reliable inference-time safety enforcement remains a key barrier to their deployment in safety-critical tasks. Existing approaches typically project each denoising iterate onto the feasible set, even though constraints are defined only on the final clean trajectory. Enforcing feasibility on noisy intermediate samples can therefore overconstrain the sampling dynamics, substantially degrading sample quality. To address this limitation, we introduce DiRecT (Diffusion-based planning via Receding-horizon denoising with Terminal constraints), a training-free algorithm for constrained sampling from diffusion models via stochastic optimal control (SOC). DiRecT enforces constraints only on the final clean sample, avoiding unnecessary restrictions on the intermediate denoising dynamics. Inspired by model predictive control, we derive a principled receding-horizon surrogate for the otherwise intractable constrained SOC formulation, yielding an efficient algorithm that cleanly separates stochastic denoising from constraint satisfaction, progressively steering samples toward feasible final trajectories without distorting the learned diffusion dynamics. Furthermore, DiRecT is highly flexible: it can leverage off-the-shelf or domain-specific optimizers, incorporate priors over environment dynamics, and optimize additional soft rewards. Extensive experiments on safe planning benchmarks demonstrate that DiRecT substantially improves deployment safety and task performance over existing diffusion-based planning baselines.

### [235] [Repeated Bilateral Trade: The Quest for Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15369)
*François Bachoc,Roberto Colomboni,Emilie Kaufmann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从公平性视角研究重复的双边交易问题。平台在每轮中为新出现的买卖双方设定价格，只有当双方都接受时才发生交易。与以往仅关注交易收益最大化不同，本文考虑追求盈余分配均衡的平台。提出了一类基于非正 Hölder 平均的公平收益目标（从罗尔斯到纳什的单参数族），该目标通过聚合买卖双方净收益来实现公平。这种公平性设计导致期望收益需通过二维奇异核积分恒等式从阈值反馈中恢复，形成一种新型纯探索问题，其自然估计量为具有行列依赖和奇异权重的矩形双重求和。在买卖双方估值独立同分布、边际分布任意未知的前提下，本文刻画了整个公平收益族的最优学习速率，并给出了匹配的固定置信度样本复杂度与后悔界（仅相差多对数因子）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统双边交易模型通常以最大化交易收益为目标，但忽视了交易中买卖双方之间的公平性。本文旨在引入公平性考量，使平台在追求交易收益的同时，确保买卖双方获得相对均衡的盈余分配。为此，作者希望构建一个既能体现公平性又具备可分析性的收益优化框架。

Method: 提出一类基于非正 Hölder 平均的公平收益目标函数，建立买卖双方净收益的加权聚合机制；利用阈值反馈信息，通过二维奇异核积分恒等式还原期望收益；针对由此产生的新型纯探索问题，设计并分析具有行-列依赖结构和奇异权重的矩形双重求和估计器；在一般未知独立同分布估值假设下，推导最优学习率，并给出样本复杂度与后悔界的紧致上界。

Result: 揭示了从罗尔斯到纳什的公平收益目标族在重复双边交易中的学习性能；证明了该族目标下的最优学习速率存在，并且可通过匹配的固定置信度样本复杂度与后悔界刻画；发现此类问题的统计结构具有显著的奇异性和依赖性特征，需使用特殊估计方法。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入公平性原则，构建了一个新的公平收益优化框架，不仅丰富了双边交易的理论体系，还揭示了在公平约束下学习问题的全新统计结构与最优学习行为。研究结果表明，在广泛估值分布假设下，公平目标仍可实现最优学习效率，为平台设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study repeated bilateral trade from a fairness perspective. At each round, a fresh seller-buyer pair arrives, and the platform posts a price before observing the traders' valuations. Trade occurs only if both agents accept the price. Rather than maximizing only the gain from trade, we consider platforms that seek balanced divisions of the generated surplus. We show that natural fairness desiderata lead to a one-parameter Rawls-to-Nash family of fair-gain objectives, obtained by aggregating the seller's and buyer's net gains through nonpositive Hölder means. Unlike the standard gain-from-trade objective and the Rawlsian fair-gain objective studied in prior work, our proposed objectives induce a new statistical structure in which expected rewards are recovered from threshold feedback through a two-dimensional singular-kernel integral identity. This leads to a nonstandard pure-exploration problem whose natural estimators are rectangular double sums with row-column dependence and singular weights. Assuming independent i.i.d. seller and buyer valuation sequences with arbitrary unknown marginals, we characterize the optimal learning rates for the whole Rawls-to-Nash family of fair-gain objectives, giving matching fixed-confidence sample-complexity and regret bounds up to polylogarithmic factors.

Abstract: Inaccurately labeled training data, or "label noise", poses a significant threat to the integrity of supervised machine learning models. This corruption directly degrades performance by teaching the model erroneous mappings between features and labels, which leads to poor generalization and reduced accuracy on properly labeled validation and test data. Current seismological applications mainly rely on large-scale training sets or data augmentation to reduce the label-noise impact, which can be labor-intensive and costly. Here, we introduce a Label Noise-Contrastive Robust Learning (LaNCoR) approach that can effectively handle noisy labels in seismic signal processing tasks, without requiring large-scale training datasets. In this approach, the input waveform feature and label representation distributions are aligned in the feature space to correct mislabeling and reduce its impact on the training process. We present LaNCoR's performance on the task of P-phase arrival-time picking of real microseismic data using two baseline models and training approaches. Our results indicate that LaNCoR can improve performance by up to 28.8% across performance metrics. This approach holds great promise for model training in seismology and geosciences.

### [237] [A Compositional Framework for Open-ended Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15386)
*Ida Momennejad,Roberta Raileanu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文将开放性智能形式化为由有限基本集合 $P$ 和一组组合算子 $C$ 诱导的闭包 $\mathcal{L}(P,C)$，并研究其支持跨任务与环境无限组合生成的性质。提出开放性智能的数学基础需包含最小表示原语（如状态、动作）和算法原语（如最近邻），以及反映习得组合语法的组合模式（如递归、序列）。通过这些支柱的闭包，可实现跨多种场景的无限自适应响应生成。论文进一步提出‘下一原语预测’作为新型架构目标，鼓励模型习得可重用的算法原语与组合语法，以实现新解的重组生成。课程学习与自对弈机制支持终身学习，促进闭包在任务与世界族中的扩展。案例研究涵盖物理、进化与神经科学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能系统难以应对训练中未出现的新问题与环境，缺乏持续适应与生成能力。为构建真正具备开放性智能的系统，需建立一套可支持无限组合生成的数学框架，从而实现对未知任务与世界的泛化与适应。

Method: 形式化开放性智能为基于基本原语集 $P$ 和组合算子集 $C$ 的闭包 $\mathcal{L}(P,C)$；定义表示与算法原语，引入组合模式（如递归、序列）构成组合语法；设计‘下一原语预测’作为训练目标，结合课程学习与自对弈进行终身学习，以发现可重用的原语与转换模式；通过物理、进化与神经科学案例验证框架有效性。

Result: 所提出的框架能够支持跨任务与世界族的无限组合生成，实现自然的组合泛化；‘下一原语预测’训练目标有效促进了算法原语与组合语法的学习；课程学习与自对弈使系统能持续扩展其闭包能力；案例研究表明该框架在多领域具有普适性和解释力。

Conclusion: 开放性智能的本质在于可扩展的组合生成能力，其数学基础由基本原语、算法原语与组合语法共同构成。通过构建可自我演进的闭包系统，可实现真正的终身学习与泛化。该框架为评估解释性、设计原生组合泛化的架构提供了理论支持，并推动了智能系统向更高级的适应性发展。

Abstract: Open-ended intelligence is the capacity to adapt to novel problems and environments that are substantially different from those in training. We formalize open-ended intelligence as the closure induced by a finite primitive set \(P\) and a set of composition operators \(C\). We characterize properties of the induced closure \(\mathcal{L}(P,C)\) that support unbounded compositional generation across families of tasks and worlds. A mathematics of open-ended intelligence requires two pillars: a minimal set of representational primitives (e.g., states, actions) and algorithmic primitives (e.g., nearest neighbor), together with composition motifs (e.g., recursion, sequencing) that reflect an acquired compositional grammar. The closure of these two pillars enables the generation of infinite adaptive responses across a wide range of settings. The mathematics supports complementary research agendas, including evaluation metrics for explanation and interpretability, as well as building architectures where compositional generalization is native. We propose next primitive prediction as a novel architectural objective, where the training objective encourages the acquisition of reusable algorithmic primitives and their compositional grammar, such that new solutions are generated through recombination. Curriculum learning and self-play enable lifelong learning and expansion of the closure by discovering reusable primitives and transition motifs across families of tasks and worlds. We ground the framework through case studies in physics, evolution, and neuroscience.

### [238] [Constitutional Value Potentials: reading and steering internal priority margins in language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15420)
*Tong Che,Rui Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出宪法价值势能（CVP），通过分析模型激活状态中的结构化边际读出，量化语言模型在价值冲突中对不同价值的保留倾向。利用独立评判者对模型输出实际保留的价值进行监督，学习每个价值对应的标量势能，其差值代表价值优先级的边际。当该边际为负时，即表示违反了宪法条款，监控得分可有效预测冲突违规，AUROC高达0.95，并优于传统隐藏层探针。信号在生成初期（提示尾部和首个响应词）即可读取，可用于识别对抗性提示是否真正诱导模型违背价值，而不仅看提示表面特征。此外，该方向还可用于干预实验，实现对价值权衡的可控调节。结果表明，某些宪法相关优先级可作为激活空间中的边际存在，而不仅是输出行为的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖输出判断模型是否遵守价值观，但在价值冲突场景下，仅看提及哪个价值无法反映真实取舍。如何准确捕捉模型在面临冲突时的真实价值仲裁机制，是当前评估与控制语言模型伦理行为的关键挑战。

Method: 提出宪法价值势能（CVP）框架：为每个价值学习一个基于隐藏状态的标量势能；通过独立评判者的判决监督训练，构建价值间的优先级边际；设计单一监控分数以检测是否违反宪法条款；利用早期激活信号识别对抗性攻击的真实影响；支持基于方向的干预调控。

Result: CVP监控在预测价值冲突违规上达到最高AUROC 0.95，优于强基线隐藏层探针；在多个规模的Qwen2.5模型上对合成冲突具有良好的泛化能力；早期激活信号即可揭示真实价值妥协情况；可通过方向操控实现预期的权衡调整。

Conclusion: 语言模型中部分宪法相关的价值优先级可被编码为激活空间中的结构化边际，而非仅通过输出行为体现。这为实时监测、解释和干预模型的价值决策提供了新路径。

Abstract: A constitution tells a language model what to value, but little tells us whether it does. Adherence is judged from outputs, and output evidence is most fragile on value conflicts, where what matters is not which value a model mentions but which one it is willing to sacrifice. We provide evidence that this arbitration can be read from activations in a structured margin readout. We introduce Constitutional Value Potentials (CVP). For each value we learn a scalar potential from the hidden state: an internal pressure to preserve that value, supervised not by the prompt but by an independent judge's verdict on which value the model's own response actually preserved. The signed difference of two potentials is a priority margin. A constitutional clause becomes the claim that a margin stays positive, and a single monitor score flags when it does not. The monitor predicts conflict violations with AUROC up to 0.95, beats a strong hidden-state probe, and generalizes to held-out synthetic conflicts across three Qwen2.5 scales. The signal appears as the answer begins, from the prompt tail and first response token. Read this early, the same signal reveals whether an adversarial priority hack has actually pushed the model toward a violation, rather than only whether the prompt looks adversarial. The same directions also support intervention tests: under selected steering settings, moving along a value direction shifts judged trade-offs in the intended direction. Together, these results suggest that some constitution-relevant priorities are accessible as activation-space margins, rather than only as output behavior.

### [239] [Post-Launch Capability Expansion of Vision-Language Models via Prompting for On-Orbit Spacecraft Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15427)
*Nicholas A. Welsh,Lennon J. Shikhman,Monty Nehru Attazs,Seemanthini K. Putane,Van Minh Nguyen,Ryan T. White*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于提示的视觉-语言模型在轨后语义扩展的可行性，通过零样本实例分割实现对未见过卫星组件的自然语言驱动识别。在129张图像上测试，SAM3在固定阈值和单次推理下表现良好，大尺寸结构（如舱体、太阳能板）定位准确，但小部件（如天线、推进器）性能差。结构化提示（含空间与几何描述）可提升82%性能，且模型运行在嵌入式GPU资源范围内，表明该方法适用于主要结构的在轨语义扩展，但对细粒度组件仍存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星载感知系统在发射前部署模型，后续更新权重或扩展标签集操作困难；传统方法需重新训练并上传参数，难以实现轨道上的新功能扩展。因此需要一种无需修改模型权重即可通过自然语言添加新语义能力的方法。

Method: 采用冻结的视觉-语言模型（SAM3），在不调整权重的情况下，使用自然语言提示进行零样本实例分割，评估其对未见过卫星组件的识别能力；测试在129张图像上执行单次推理，保持全局阈值不变，无后处理。

Conclusion: 提示驱动的视觉-语言模型可在不修改模型权重的前提下，实现星载系统的在轨语义扩展，尤其适用于大型结构的识别；但对细小部件的零样本定位仍受限于域偏移与尺度问题，需进一步优化提示设计与模型适应性。

Abstract: Spaceborne inspection systems often deploy perception models prior to launch, after which updating model weights or expanding fixed label sets becomes operationally impractical. While supervised models can be integrated pre-flight, adding new semantic capabilities in orbit requires retraining and re-uploading parameters. We investigate whether prompt-driven vision--language models can enable post-launch semantic expansion, allowing new spacecraft components to be specified via natural-language prompts without modifying onboard weights. We evaluate zero-shot instance segmentation of spacecraft components under a strictly frozen, single-pass inference protocol on a test set of $129$ images of previously unseen satellites. Under fixed global thresholds and no post-processing, SAM3 achieves $0.385$ mAP@$0.5$ and $0.267$ mAP@$0.5{:}0.95$. Performance is strongly scale-dependent: large structural elements like spacecraft bodies ($0.639$ AP@$0.50$) and solar arrays ($0.598$ AP@$0.5$) localize reliably, while relatively small appendages like antennas ($0.221$ AP@$0.5$) and thrusters ($0.081$ AP@$0.5$) remain difficult. Prompt formulation influences performance, with structured prompts incorporating spatial and geometric descriptors yielding up to $82%$ improvement over short category-name prompts. The model operates within the memory and compute envelope of contemporary embedded GPUs, suggesting prompt-driven grounding can provide a practical mechanism for post-launch semantic extension of dominant spacecraft structures while highlighting limitations of zero-shot localization for fine-scale components under orbital domain shift.

### [241] [PHINN: Persistent Homology Inspired Neural Network for Rare-Event Time Series Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15452)
*Emre Yusuf,Ren Takahashi,Jayabrata Bhaduri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PHINN 是一种基于流匹配的生成框架，利用动态贝蒂曲线作为条件信号，并采用持久性景观损失以保证同调一致性。该方法能有效建模时间序列中的罕见事件，通过拓扑指纹（贝蒂数变化）提升对极端值的捕捉能力，在金融、流行病学和多模态数据上显著优于传统统计与扩散模型，在拓扑保真度上提升84%，贝蒂-均方根误差降低41-63%，同时在尾部覆盖率和形状保真度方面超越跳扩散模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出PHINN框架，使用动态贝蒂曲线作为条件信号，结合持久性景观损失确保同调结构的一致性，支持多变量数据、自然语言接口设定贝蒂目标、跨域元学习和少样本生成，并具备认证的对抗鲁棒性。

Result: 在金融、流行病学及多模态基准测试中，PHINN在拓扑保真度上显著优于统计与扩散基线（贝蒂-RMSE下降41-63%，过渡准确率提升84%），在尾部覆盖率上与跳扩散模型相当，但在形状保真度上更优；所有结果均具有95%置信区间。

Conclusion: PHINN通过引入拓扑信息作为生成条件，成功提升了罕见事件建模的能力，尤其在极端值生成与形状保持方面表现卓越，为高维时间序列中的稀有事件生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Rare events in time series are critical to model but hard to learn due to data scarcity. Current generative models struggle with extreme values. We observe that rare events leave distinct topological fingerprints - transitions in Betti numbers from point-cloud embeddings - that are more stable and discriminative than statistical moments.
  We introduce PHINN, a flow-matching framework using dynamic Betti curves as conditioning signals and a persistence landscape loss for homology consistency. It scales to multivariate data, includes a natural-language interface to set Betti targets, supports cross-domain meta-learning and few-shot generation, and provides certified adversarial robustness.
  On financial, epidemiological, and multi-modal benchmarks, PHINN outperforms statistical and diffusion baselines in topological fidelity (beta-RMSE down 41-63%, transition accuracy up 84%) and matches jump-diffusion models in tail coverage while exceeding them in shape fidelity. All results have 95% confidence intervals.

### [242] [Understanding Diversity Collapse in RLVR via the Lens of Overtraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15455)
*Suqin Yuan,Jinkun Chen,Jiyang Zheng,Muyang Li,Lei Feng,Dadong Wang,Tao Xiang,Tongliang Liu,Bo An*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了强化学习中可验证奖励（RLVR）方法在提升大语言模型推理能力时出现的'多样性崩溃'问题，即随着单次通过率（Pass@1）提升，高k值通过率（Pass@k）反而下降。作者从过训练视角解释这一现象：当问题对参考指标的贡献已饱和后，继续更新只会集中概率于偏好轨迹，而非扩展模型求解范围。在少量轨迹采样的设定下，一次成功即导致问题进入近似饱和状态，因此多数更新实为过训练。论文指出，尽管整体高k通过率下降，但仍有部分原本无法解决的问题在训练中变得可解，说明并非无推理增益。为此提出贝叶斯边界门控（BBG），通过估计每个问题对推理边界的边际贡献，避免过训练，有效提升多种推理基准上的平均Pass@k表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决RLVR中出现的多样性崩溃问题，理解其根本原因，并探索如何真正扩展模型的推理能力，而非仅优化单一指标。

Method: 通过分析过训练机制解释多样性崩溃；引入贝叶斯边界门控（BBG）方法，基于问题对推理边界的边际贡献动态调整优化方向，避免在已饱和问题上过度更新。

Result: BBG在多个推理基准上显著提升了不同k值下的平均Pass@k性能，尤其在高k值下表现突出，证明其能有效缓解过训练并扩展模型推理边界。

Conclusion: 多样性崩溃源于标准RLVR中的过训练，而非缺乏推理增益；通过引入贝叶斯边界门控（BBG）可有效引导优化避开过训练区域，实现对模型推理能力的实质性扩展。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become a key approach for enhancing the reasoning abilities of large language models. However, RLVR often suffers from \emph{diversity collapse}: Pass@$1$ improves while high-$k$ Pass@$k$ degrades, which is viewed as a narrowing of the model's reasoning boundary. We formalize this diversity collapse through the lens of \emph{overtraining}: once a problem's contribution to the reference metric has effectively saturated, further updates no longer expand what the model can solve but still concentrate probability mass on the trajectories favored by on-policy sampling. Under a standard setup with few rollouts per problem, even a single observed success places a problem in a nearly saturated regime for high-$k$ Pass@$k$, so most updates in standard RLVR are overtraining from the boundary perspective. This perspective also suggests a reading of whether RLVR can expand the model's reasoning abilities beyond the base model: since RLVR is structurally biased against high-$k$ Pass@$k$, its aggregate decline does not by itself mean that no new reasoning gains occurred. Interventionally, restricting updates to problems with zero observed success lifts Pass@$256$ above the base model on difficult benchmarks; observationally, a non-trivial fraction of initially unsolvable problems become solvable during standard RLVR training. Building on these findings, we propose \emph{Bayesian Boundary Gating} (BBG), which redirects optimization away from overtraining by estimating each problem's marginal contribution to the reasoning boundary. Across multiple reasoning benchmarks, BBG improves average Pass@$k$ across a wide range of $k$.

</details>


### [243] [Bayesian 3D Steerable CNNs: Enabling Equivariance and Uncertainty Quantification Simultaneously](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15479)
*Abhishek Keripale,Ponkrshnan Thiagarajan,Susanta Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种贝叶斯可旋转卷积神经网络（Bayesian Steerable-CNN），通过在基函数系数上放置后验分布，实现保持SE(3)等变性的随机核，同时支持不确定性量化。模型采用变分推断与贝叶斯反向传播优化损失函数，并能分解预测不确定性为认知不确定性和偶然不确定性。实验表明，该模型在分类准确率上表现良好，预期校准误差仅为0.0263，在分布外数据上优于确定性模型最多6.17%；利用不确定性估计还能提升性能约4%（覆盖84%测试集）。统计分析显示认知不确定性与预测误差显著负相关，说明不确定性具有语义意义。该框架成功融合了贝叶斯不确定性量化与等变卷积的归纳偏置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可旋转卷积神经网络（Steerable-CNN）虽保证了SE(3)等变性，但其确定性设计无法提供不确定性估计，限制了其在需要置信度评估场景中的应用。因此亟需一种既能保持等变性又能量化不确定性的方法。

Method: 将基函数系数建模为后验分布，构建贝叶斯可旋转卷积层；采用变分推断优化模型参数，使用贝叶斯反向传播进行训练；通过分解预测方差实现对认知不确定性和偶然不确定性的分离。

Result: 模型在分类任务中达到竞争性准确率，预期校准误差为0.0263；在添加高斯噪声的分布外设置下，性能优于确定性模型最多6.17%；利用不确定性指导推理，使84%测试样本的准确率提升约4%；认知不确定性与预测误差呈显著负相关，验证了不确定性估计的合理性。

Conclusion: 所提出的贝叶斯可旋转卷积神经网络成功将不确定性量化与等变归纳偏置相结合，既保持了精确的等变性，又提供了有意义的不确定性估计，适用于对可靠性要求高的实际应用场景。

Abstract: Steerable convolutional neural networks (Steerable-CNNs) guarantee SE(3)-equivariance by parameterizing kernels as linear combinations of steerable basis functions, but their deterministic nature precludes uncertainty quantification - limiting their use in settings where confidence estimates are essential. We propose a Bayesian Steerable-CNN that places posterior distributions over the basis coefficients, yielding stochastic kernels while preserving equivariance exactly. The loss function of the model is obtained via variational inference and minimized by Bayes-by-Backpropagation. The framework admits a decomposition of predictive uncertainty into epistemic and aleatoric components. Empirically, the model attains competitive classification accuracy alongside an expected calibration error of 0.0263 and outperforms its deterministic counterpart by up to 6.17% under distributional shift induced by additive Gaussian noise. Furthermore, we leverage the model's uncertainty estimates to enhance its performance significantly, achieving a notable gain - approximately 4% higher accuracy across 84% of the test dataset. A statistically significant negative correlation between epistemic uncertainty and prediction error confirms that the learned posterior variance is semantically meaningful. The framework unifies Bayesian uncertainty quantification with the inductive bias of equivariant CNNs.

### [244] [Model Stealing Through the Lens of Model Multiplicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15493)
*Eliott Baltz,Satoshi Hara,Ulrich Aïvodji*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了模型窃取攻击中高保真度代理模型等同于原始模型的常规认知，指出尽管代理模型在性能上与目标模型相似，但其在部署相关属性上存在显著差异。通过计算代理模型的Rashomon集并评估其多样性（如模糊性、差异性和Rashomon容量）以及公平性指标，发现即使在相同保真度下，代理模型在关键性能指标上仍表现出显著差异，从而质疑了高保真代理模型在实际部署中的等效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为高保真度的模型窃取攻击会威胁机器学习服务的知识产权，并赋予攻击者与原始服务提供者相当的经济杠杆。然而，该研究指出，基于查询的提取仅提供部分监督，导致多个近似最优的代理模型可能具有相似保真度但不同部署特性，因此需要重新审视高保真代理模型是否真正等同于目标模型。

Method: 计算代理模型的Rashomon集（即几乎同样准确的模型集合），使用多重性指标（模糊性、差异性、Rashomon容量）和群体公平性指标评估其多样性，并在表格数据、医学影像和自然语言处理任务上进行实证分析。

Result: 在真实世界数据集上的实验表明，尽管代理模型与目标模型具有相似的保真度，但在其他关键性能指标上存在显著差异，说明高保真代理模型并不必然等同于目标模型，在实际部署中可能存在重要区别。

Conclusion: 高保真度的模型窃取攻击虽能生成看似可靠的代理模型，但由于其多样性和部署相关属性的不一致性，不能简单等同于原始模型。这削弱了攻击者凭借此类模型获得经济优势的假设，提示需从更全面的角度评估模型安全性与知识产权保护。

Abstract: Model stealing attacks, where adversaries create high-fidelity surrogate models, are a significant threat to the intellectual property of machine learning services. Conventional wisdom suggests these surrogates could provide adversaries with economic leverage comparable to the original service providers. This paper challenges this assumption by evaluating model stealing attacks beyond mere fidelity to the target model. Because query-based extraction provides only partial supervision of the target's input-output behavior, the surrogate is not uniquely identified: many near-optimal surrogates can achieve comparable fidelity while differing in deployment-relevant properties. Instead of performing a classic learning-based model stealing attack, we compute the Rashomon Set (i.e., the set of almost-equally-accurate models) of surrogate models, and evaluate its diversity using multiplicity metrics (ambiguity, discrepancy, and Rashomon Capacity) and group fairness metrics. Across tabular, medical imaging, and NLP tasks, our experiments on real-world datasets reveal that despite exhibiting similar fidelity to the target model, surrogate models can display significant variances in other critical performance metrics. These findings cast doubt on the presumed equivalence between high-fidelity surrogates and the target model in practical deployment scenarios.

Conclusion: 神经算子预训练为实现跨融合装置配置的可重用、实时平衡推断提供了有效途径，突破了传统方法在通用性与实时性方面的瓶颈。

Abstract: Real-time reconstruction of magnetohydrodynamic equilibria is essential for plasma shaping, stability assessment and feedback control in magnetic confinement fusion. However, Grad-Shafranov equilibrium calculations remain largely device-specific and iterative, limiting their use in latency-constrained control settings. Existing neural approaches can accelerate individual equilibrium predictions, but they do not generally provide reusable models across changing plasma boundaries or tokamak geometries. Here we show that equilibrium reconstruction can be recast as a cross-device operator learning problem. We develop a domain-specific neural operator framework that maps geometry and profile parameters directly to the poloidal flux field, replacing repeated solve-on-demand computation with amortized operator inference. Using the analytically tractable Solov'ev family as a controlled Grad-Shafranov testbed, we generate equilibria across eight geometrically distinct tokamak-like configurations and benchmark five neural operator architectures under four transfer-learning strategies. Single-geometry pretraining gives poor transfer to unseen devices, whereas multi-geometry pretraining enables data-efficient adaptation. The Wavelet Neural Operator gives the strongest cross-geometry performance, reaching mean relative L2 errors below 4% with 100 labelled target equilibria and below 2% with full fine-tuning. The predicted magnetic fields satisfy the divergence-free constraint to numerical precision, and four architectures achieve millisecond or sub-millisecond inference. These results identify neural operator pretraining as a route towards reusable, real-time equilibrium inference across fusion device configurations.

While mechanistic approaches have shed light on where alignment resides in model weights, they do not by provide a general formal framework for deriving guarantees about when fine-tuning degrades it -- leaving the field without principled tools for predicting or preventing alignment collapse. We develop a local geometric framework through geometric analysis of parameter-space trajectories and apply it to understand the fragility of alignment in fine-tuning. While first-order analysis suggests orthogonal updates are safe, we prove this is illusory: the curvature of the fine-tuning loss induces second-order acceleration that can induce second-order drift into alignment-sensitive regions. We formalize a construct of our framework as the Alignment Instability Condition (AIC), three geometric properties that, when present, are sufficient to guarantee degradation. Our main result proves quartic onset of alignment degradation along gradient-flow trajectories, determined by how sharply alignment depends on specific parameters and how strongly tasks couple to these parameters. These findings yield formal sufficient conditions under which static first-order protection can fail under gradient descent. We further empirically validate the framework's foundations, showing that the Fisher Information Matrix provides a proxy for the degree of safety degradation across diverse fine-tuning.

Abstract: The Edge of Stability (EoS) phenomenon, where gradient descent operates with sharpness exceeding the classical convergence threshold yet the loss decreases over long timescales, is ubiquitous in modern deep learning but remains poorly understood in realistic settings. Prior rigorous analyses have been largely confined to scalar or low-dimensional losses with specific structural forms. In this work, we develop a bifurcation theory framework for gradient descent on the edge of stability that applies directly to overparameterized neural networks. By decomposing the training dynamics into components normal and tangent to the manifold of minimizers, we show that stable EoS training arises from a flip bifurcation in the normal direction, governed by the sign of the first Lyapunov coefficient, while the tangent dynamics drift toward regions of decreasing sharpness. Under mild spectral and geometric assumptions on the loss landscape, we prove convergence to the minimizing manifold when training at the EoS threshold. As a corollary, we recover and unify prior results: we show that the product-stability condition of Gan (2026) is an instance of our framework.

Abstract: Test-time training (TTT) adapts a pretrained model to each prompt via parameter updates, improving accuracy under pretraining-to-test distribution shifts. Yet, its performance often suffers from instability and sensitivity to hyperparameters such as update steps and subspace. We explain this behavior through a decision-theoretic lens, treating TTT as implicit Bayesian inference in the kernel regime. Under a Gaussian process benchmark, we show that TTT reduces prediction error when updates are spectrally matched to the prompt's signal-to-noise ratio and aligned with query-relevant eigen-directions. This perspective underpins the following results: (1) we show when fixed update steps and subspaces fail under distribution shifts, motivating adaptive strategies; (2) we prove that selecting update steps via prompt evidence admits a PAC-Bayes guarantee against overfitting; and (3) we characterize the Bayes-optimal update subspace under a linear-Gaussian correction model, yielding a scoring rule for selecting Transformer blocks and heads. Our theory helps explain the empirical instability of TTT, taking a step toward principled guidance for when, how far, and which directions to adapt.
